# Skyrim:Kill Lurbuk

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Dark Brotherhood.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Dark_Brotherhood.png) | **Silence a [terrible bard](/wiki/Skyrim:Lurbuk "Skyrim:Lurbuk"), permanently.** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Nazir](/wiki/Skyrim:Nazir "Skyrim:Nazir") |
| Location(s): | [Moorside Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Moorside_Inn "Skyrim:Moorside Inn"), [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal") |
| Reward: | Leveled gold |
| ID: | DBSideContract05 |
| --- | |
| |  |  |  | | --- | --- | --- | | **← Previous** [Whispers in the Dark](/wiki/Skyrim:Whispers_in_the_Dark "Skyrim:Whispers in the Dark") | **Concurrent** [Kill Hern](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_Hern "Skyrim:Kill Hern") | **Next →** [The Silence Has Been Broken](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Silence_Has_Been_Broken "Skyrim:The Silence Has Been Broken") | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | ← Previous | [Whispers in the Dark](/wiki/Skyrim:Whispers_in_the_Dark "Skyrim:Whispers in the Dark") | | Concurrent | [Kill Hern](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_Hern "Skyrim:Kill Hern") | | → Next | [The Silence Has Been Broken](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Silence_Has_Been_Broken "Skyrim:The Silence Has Been Broken") | | |

Silence at last

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Go to [Moorside Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Moorside_Inn "Skyrim:Moorside Inn") in [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal").
2. Locate and kill [Lurbuk](/wiki/Skyrim:Lurbuk "Skyrim:Lurbuk").
3. Return to [Nazir](/wiki/Skyrim:Nazir "Skyrim:Nazir").

## Detailed Walkthrough

This is a very simple assassination. Lurbuk is not known to ever leave the [Moorside Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Moorside_Inn "Skyrim:Moorside Inn") and can easily be picked off with an arrow when he isn't performing. The difficulty lies in the fact that whatever you tell him, he will never turn hostile and attack, which would potentially increase the chances of earning a bounty, no matter what you say to him.

Silence the merrymaker

If you are having difficulty killing Lurbuk in the common room, you can wait until he either sits in the corner of his room or goes to sleep late at night. There should be no one else in the room, so a single sneak attack should be enough to eliminate him silently. It is also possible to wait until he's sitting in the common room, and then sneak into the room across from him, facing his back. From this position it can be safe to shoot him with an arrow, and as long as the arrow used can take him out with one blow, it will still be a stealthy kill. You can also rent a bed from the innkeeper. When she leaves to show you to your room, you can kill Lurbuk without her witnessing the kill. A creative, albeit risky, way to get the job done is to cast a Frenzy spell on him. Provided that you are not seen or heard, the effect will cause everyone in the inn to see Lurbuk as a hostile, attacking and killing him for you.

Another way to kill him is similar to the bow and arrow method above. Sneak into the room across from him and wait until you are hidden. Once hidden, release an offensive Shout (fire breath, frost breath, etc.) towards Lurbuk. This should do the trick since one Shout should be sufficient in killing him.

Note: invisibility helps with sneaking and hiding in the room across from Lurbuk.

Like most assassination targets, you may choose to have a conversation with Lurbuk before killing him:

| Topic | Dialogue |
| --- | --- |
| *"Someone hired the Dark Brotherhood to kill you, Lurbuk."* | *"Ha! Oh, that's a good one, friend. Killing Lurbuk... I mean, can you even imagine something so ludicrous? Depriving the world of my unique talents?"* |
| *"Sing me a song, bard. A song of fear, and death!"* | *"Hmm... All right... How about this? Shadows creep, and... and phantoms leap! A man got... he got scared. And the demons dared! To um... visit upon him all which they feared! Brilliant, I know. It's a gift."* |
| *(Remain Silent)* | *"What's the matter, friend? Khajiit got your tongue? Maybe you need a little ditty to loosen your gob, hmm? There once was a stranger, with eyes full of danger, he spoke not a word, but his meaning was heard... Sing on, sweet Lurbuk, sing on!"* |

### Reward

| Levels | Reward |
| --- | --- |
| 1–9 | 250 |
| 10–19 | 400 |
| 20–29 | 500 |
| 30–39 | 600 |
| 40+ | 750 |

## Notes

- If you have started but not yet completed the quest [Laid to Rest](/wiki/Skyrim:Laid_to_Rest "Skyrim:Laid to Rest"), Lurbuk may still be standing outside of Movarth's Lair. For this reason, it is recommended that you either dismiss the townspeople or finish Laid to Rest. Otherwise, you will be spotted when killing Lurbuk and thus incur a bounty.
- If you ask Nazir for additional information, he will tell you that Lurbuk is so hated that he had multiple Brotherhood contracts out on him and [Astrid](/wiki/Skyrim:Astrid "Skyrim:Astrid") had to hold a lottery to decide who was able to put in the contract.
- It's quite possible for Lurbuk to have already died by the time you would normally get this contract quest. If this is the case, then the contract will just be skipped entirely.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage DBSideContract05 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest DBSideContract05`.

Ma'randru-jo fights back.

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Locate [Ma'randru-jo](/wiki/Skyrim:Ma%27randru-jo "Skyrim:Ma'randru-jo").
2. Kill him.
3. Return to [Nazir](/wiki/Skyrim:Nazir "Skyrim:Nazir") and receive your reward.

## Detailed Walkthrough

When Ma'randru-jo is not wandering the roads of Tamriel, he can be found in one of the caravan camps led by Ri'saad. The caravan travels the route between [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") and [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") and spends two full days camped outside each city before alternating. Since he does not stay stationary, he can be hard to find. However, the map indicates his position. To find him simply travel to his known location, check the map, then travel to his new location. Continue this until he is found.

Once you have located him, you may talk to him. Like most other assassination targets, you are given three dialogue choices. If you choose to insult him, he will attack you first, so you can then kill him without the fear of incurring a bounty and being arrested by the town guard, or attacked by the rest of the Khajiit merchants. Alternatively, you can sneak kill him without being detected by the rest of the merchants.

| Topic | Dialogue | Response |
| --- | --- | --- |
| *"I'm going to beat you like a house cat."* (if the player is a non-Khajiit)  *"You are a disgrace to our race! I spit on your fur!"* (if the player is a Khajiit) | *"What? You dare challenge Ma'randru-jo? You will suffer for your insolence!"* | Becomes hostile and attacks |
| *"You're one hard mage to track down, Ma'randru-jo."* | *"And why would you be looking for me, hmm? I'm not sure I appreciate your presence here. Friend."* | Walks away |
| *(Remain silent)* | *"Now aren't you a strange one. Well, if you're here to shop, shop. If not, find some other caravan to stalk."* | Walks away |

Return to the sanctuary and speak with [Nazir](/wiki/Skyrim:Nazir "Skyrim:Nazir") to complete the quest and receive a reward of leveled Gold. If you're a Khajiit, Nazir will remark *"How went your encounter with Ma'randru-jo? Back in Hammerfell, I always loved watching two cats rip each other to shreds..."*.

### Reward

| Levels | Reward |
| --- | --- |
| 1–9 | 250 |
| 10–19 | 400 |
| 20–29 | 500 |
| 30–39 | 600 |
| 40+ | 750 |

## Notes

- [Ri'saad](/wiki/Skyrim:Ri%27saad "Skyrim:Ri'saad"), the caravan leader, is essential. If the other Khajiit attack, you will be unable to kill him.

# Skyrim:Kill Maluril

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Dark Brotherhood.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Dark_Brotherhood.png) | **Kill [Maluril](/wiki/Skyrim:Maluril "Skyrim:Maluril") in [Mzinchaleft](/wiki/Skyrim:Mzinchaleft "Skyrim:Mzinchaleft").** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Nazir](/wiki/Skyrim:Nazir "Skyrim:Nazir") |
| Location(s): | [Mzinchaleft](/wiki/Skyrim:Mzinchaleft "Skyrim:Mzinchaleft") |
| Reward: | Leveled gold |
| ID: | DBSideContract10 |
| Suggested Level: | 16 |
| --- | |
| |  |  |  | | --- | --- | --- | | **← Previous** [Kill Agnis](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_Agnis "Skyrim:Kill Agnis") | **Concurrent** [Kill Helvard](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_Helvard "Skyrim:Kill Helvard") | **Next →** [Kill Safia](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_Safia "Skyrim:Kill Safia") | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | ← Previous | [Kill Agnis](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_Agnis "Skyrim:Kill Agnis") | | Concurrent | [Kill Helvard](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_Helvard "Skyrim:Kill Helvard") | | → Next | [Kill Safia](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_Safia "Skyrim:Kill Safia") | | |

Maluril in combat

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Get the contract from [Nazir](/wiki/Skyrim:Nazir "Skyrim:Nazir").
2. Kill [Maluril](/wiki/Skyrim:Maluril "Skyrim:Maluril") in [Mzinchaleft](/wiki/Skyrim:Mzinchaleft "Skyrim:Mzinchaleft").
3. Report back to Nazir.

### Get the Contract

When [Nazir](/wiki/Skyrim:Nazir "Skyrim:Nazir") hands you the quest, he will not only reveal the target's location to be the ancient Dwarven ruin of [Mzinchaleft](/wiki/Skyrim:Mzinchaleft "Skyrim:Mzinchaleft"), he will also provide a bit of fair warning of [Maluril](/wiki/Skyrim:Maluril "Skyrim:Maluril"): *"He's dangerous. Very dangerous. A rogue Dark Elf mage doing research into Dwarven artifacts should be both respected... and feared. Just not by you."* Leave Nazir and travel to Mzinchaleft, in the tundra southwest of [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar").

### Mzinchaleft

The exterior is guarded by up to six leveled [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") so dispose of them and head inside. The ruin consists of three zones, but your target is in the first zone, so there will be nothing but leveled bandit enemies to face. Make your way through the tunnels and fight the opposition. After the second chamber, you will encounter an intersection and a locked door to the north. The bandit guarding the door holds the [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Maluril%27s_Room_Key "Skyrim:Maluril's Room Key"), so do what you have to do to claim it. Unlock the door and enter Maluril's Room where you will encounter a surprisingly peaceful [Dunmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Elf "Skyrim:Dark Elf") obviously not looking for trouble.

You can now talk to him and choose between three different options, but even if his responses will be hostile, he will not attack you, nor will he summon any enemies to fight you. You will have no other option but to kill him in cold blood; he uses a [Staff of Firebolts](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Firebolts "Skyrim:Staff of Firebolts").

| Topic | Dialogue | Response |
| --- | --- | --- |
| *(Remain silent)* | *"Who are you? Why are you here? Leave this place. I have much work to conduct...."* | Ends conversation |
| *"Fascinating race, the Dwemer. Powerful... and extinct."* | *"Yes... quite. But if that power could be harnessed. Controlled. The possibilities would be... But... who exactly are you? And why are you in here? I think it best you leave Mzinchaleft. These ruins can be quite... dangerous."* | Ends conversation |
| *"The only thing you will discover in Mzinchaleft is death."* | *"Death? Oh, there's death to be found here, to be sure. But not my own!"* | Turns hostile |

Before leaving, read through the [Speech](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech "Skyrim:Speech") skill book *[A Dance in Fire, v7](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Dance_in_Fire,_v7 "Skyrim:A Dance in Fire, v7")*. Additionally, *[Maluril's Journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Maluril%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Maluril's Journal")* can be found on the table, providing some insight into who ordered his demise.

### Reward

Return to Nazir in the sanctuary and tell him the good news. He will be quite satisfied and will comment: *"I hope the elf didn't give you too much trouble. I once got set on fire by a sorcerer. Nasty business, that. But I digress. Here's your payment."* He then hands you the reward, a leveled amount of gold.

| Levels | Reward |
| --- | --- |
| 1–9 | 250 |
| 10–19 | 400 |
| 20–29 | 500 |
| 30–39 | 600 |
| 40+ | 750 |

## Notes

- With version 3.0.3 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), Maluril's journal will no longer be present in Mzinchaleft until this quest has begun.

## Bugs

- Maluril belonging to the Dark Brotherhood faction can cause you to get expelled from the Dark Brotherhood if he gets attacked at the wrong time.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.7, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Kill Narfi

## Overview

Kill Narfi

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Get the contract from [Nazir](/wiki/Skyrim:Nazir "Skyrim:Nazir").
2. Travel to [Ivarstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivarstead "Skyrim:Ivarstead").
3. Assassinate [Narfi](/wiki/Skyrim:Narfi "Skyrim:Narfi").
4. Report back to Nazir to collect your reward.

### Get the Contract

Right after your [initiation](/wiki/Skyrim:With_Friends_Like_These... "Skyrim:With Friends Like These...") into the [Dark Brotherhood](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood"), guild leader [Astrid](/wiki/Skyrim:Astrid "Skyrim:Astrid") will confess that no "real" jobs are available at the moment and that you should talk to [Nazir](/wiki/Skyrim:Nazir "Skyrim:Nazir") for smaller contract work. Nazir will give three targets to you at the same time, so you are free to pick what order you do them in. On [Narfi](/wiki/Skyrim:Narfi "Skyrim:Narfi"), he will comment that *"He's a hapless beggar living in some ruins just outside the village of [Ivarstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivarstead "Skyrim:Ivarstead"). Easy even for you."*

### Kill a Beggar

Make your way to Ivarstead, the small settlement at the foot of the [Throat of the World](/wiki/Skyrim:Throat_of_the_World "Skyrim:Throat of the World"), and locate Narfi. Due to the roaming creek separating Narfi's worn-out house from the rest of Ivarstead, there are no watchful eyes from the Ivarstead guards, and as such, you can kill him in any manner you want. The easiest method is to kill him in his sleep; he goes to bed at 4am, so take advantage of the darkness and sneak into the cabin right after that time and dispose of the beggar. Note that the sawmill across the lake gets busy right after 7am, so don't wait too long.

If you speak to Narfi before you kill him, you are given three dialogue options; you may only pick one as the conversation ends and you can't speak to him again.

| Topic | Dialogue |
| --- | --- |
| *(Remain silent)* | *"Do... do you want something? Look, if you ain't gonna talk, or spare no coin, just go away..."* |
| *"Your pathetic existence has come to an end, Narfi."* | *"Oh... Oh no... Please, please... I ain't never harmed no one... Old Narfi just wants to be left alone..."* |
| *"Beg! Beg for your miserable life!"* | *"No! Oh, by the gods, please no!"* |

Narfi won't defend himself as a result of any of these dialogue options, so if you are seen killing him, you cannot avoid a bounty.

### Reward

Once Narfi is dead, travel back to the [sanctuary](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood_Sanctuary "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood Sanctuary") and receive your reward of leveled gold from [Nazir](/wiki/Skyrim:Nazir "Skyrim:Nazir"), who will also comment, *"Congratulations. You slaughtered an emaciated beggar in cold blood. You are truly an opponent to be feared."*

| Levels | Reward |
| --- | --- |
| 1–9 | 250 |
| 10–19 | 400 |
| 20–29 | 500 |
| 30–39 | 600 |
| 40+ | 750 |

## Notes

- As soon as you accept the contract from Nazir, you will be unable to complete the [miscellaneous](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivarstead#Miscellaneous_Quests "Skyrim:Ivarstead") Ivarstead quest [The Straw that Broke](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Straw_that_Broke "Skyrim:The Straw that Broke").
- It's quite possible for Narfi to have already died by the time you would normally get this contract quest. If this is the case, then the contract will just be skipped entirely.

## Quest Stages

| Contract: Kill Narfi (DBSideContract01) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | I must travel to the town of Ivarstead and kill the beggar Narfi. I may use any means at my disposal. When I am done, I am to return to Nazir at the Sanctuary and collect my reward. *Objective 10:* Kill Narfi |
| 20 |  | *Objective 20:* Report back to Nazir |
| 200 | ☑ | Narfi is dead, and I have collected my reward from Nazir at the Sanctuary. |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 255.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage DBSideContract01 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest DBSideContract01`.

# Skyrim:Kill Safia

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Dark Brotherhood.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Dark_Brotherhood.png) | **Kill a [pirate captain](/wiki/Skyrim:Safia "Skyrim:Safia") on her own [ship](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Wave "Skyrim:Red Wave").** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Nazir](/wiki/Skyrim:Nazir "Skyrim:Nazir") |
| Location(s): | Near [East Empire Company Warehouse](/wiki/Skyrim:East_Empire_Company_Warehouse "Skyrim:East Empire Company Warehouse") |
| Reward: | Leveled gold |
| ID: | DBSideContract12 |
| --- | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | **← Previous** [Kill Maluril](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_Maluril "Skyrim:Kill Maluril"), [Kill Helvard](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_Helvard "Skyrim:Kill Helvard"), [Kill Agnis](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_Agnis "Skyrim:Kill Agnis") |  | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | ← Previous | [Kill Maluril](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_Maluril "Skyrim:Kill Maluril"), [Kill Helvard](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_Helvard "Skyrim:Kill Helvard"), [Kill Agnis](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_Agnis "Skyrim:Kill Agnis") | | |

Safia's ship: The [Red Wave](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Wave "Skyrim:Red Wave")

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Travel to the [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") harbor.
2. Get onto [Safia](/wiki/Skyrim:Safia "Skyrim:Safia")'s Ship, the [Red Wave](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Wave "Skyrim:Red Wave").
3. Kill Safia.
4. Report back to [Nazir](/wiki/Skyrim:Nazir "Skyrim:Nazir") and claim your reward.

## Detailed Walkthrough

Make your way to the [East Empire Company Warehouse](/wiki/Skyrim:East_Empire_Company_Warehouse "Skyrim:East Empire Company Warehouse"), just outside of [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"), and then board the ship the [Red Wave](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Wave "Skyrim:Red Wave"). Even though boarding the ship is considered trespassing, the "guards" (crew members) will not actually confront you if they see you. All they will do is say "you're not supposed to be here" and then leave you alone. [Safia](/wiki/Skyrim:Safia "Skyrim:Safia") can be found in the middle deck of the ship, walking around switching chairs every few minutes or eating.

Note that two of the Red Wave's crew members are considered essential and thus cannot be killed and will continue fighting a little after you "defeat" them, which also gives you bounty. Therefore, it is best to avoid any combat with the crew.

You may have the following conversation with Safia:

| Topic | Dialogue |
| --- | --- |
| *"I represent the Dark..."* | *"The Dark Brotherhood? Yeah, yeah, yeah. You think this is the first contract I've had on my life? I'm a pirate, sweetie. Assassination attempts are an occupational hazard. Now, shall we?"* |
| *"You face the Dread Lord..."* | *"Sithis? Let me guess: "In the Void!" By the gods, you Dark Brotherhood are a predictable lot, aren't you? Okay, here's how this works. You try to assassinate me, and I kill you. Horribly. I have done this dance before, you know."* |
| *(Remain Silent)* | *"Ah, I see. The old Dark Brotherhood "silent intimidation" treatment. Oh, I know who you are. Don't be so surprised. You ain't the first assassin sent to kill me. Won't be the last. Now let's get this over with."* |

Each dialogue option causes her to initiate combat, thus allowing you to kill her without gaining a bounty. Her crew will also fail to defend her if she initiates combat.

After the kill, report back to [Nazir](/wiki/Skyrim:Nazir "Skyrim:Nazir") for some leveled gold as a reward:

:   *"You haven't faced that pirate captain yet, have you? Safia? I only ask because you're still alive..."*
:   **Safia is dead.**
:   *"By Sithis, now I am truly impressed! To kill a pirate captain, on her own ship no less? Simply masterful! You've not only earned your payment, but my respect as well. And believe me, friend - that does not come easily. I'm afraid that concludes our business. You have exhausted all available additional contracts. But I'm sure you've got plenty to keep you busy right about now, hmm?"*

### Reward

| Levels | Reward |
| --- | --- |
| 1–9 | 250 |
| 10–19 | 400 |
| 20–29 | 500 |
| 30–39 | 600 |
| 40+ | 750 |

## Notes

- This quest can conflict with the Thieves Guild quest [The Dainty Sload](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Dainty_Sload "Skyrim:The Dainty Sload").
- Since several members of the crew are essential - including the one for the aforementioned Thieves Guild quest - the fight can go badly, and a large bounty can be incurred.
- [Redwave](/wiki/Oblivion:Redwave "Oblivion:Redwave") was also the name of a unique [cutlass](/wiki/Oblivion:Cutlass "Oblivion:Cutlass") in *[Oblivion](/wiki/Oblivion:Oblivion "Oblivion:Oblivion")*, a [quest](/wiki/Oblivion:The_Ghost_Ship_of_Anvil "Oblivion:The Ghost Ship of Anvil") reward for recovering a family heirloom from a [ship](/wiki/Oblivion:The_Serpent%27s_Wake "Oblivion:The Serpent's Wake") haunted by the ghosts of a crew murdered by a Dark Brotherhood member. It is unknown if there is any intended connection between the two.

## Bugs

- Sometimes after approaching [Safia](/wiki/Skyrim:Safia "Skyrim:Safia") and talking to her, she will not turn hostile.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.8, fixes this bug.

| 20 |  | *Objective 20:* Report back to Nazir |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 255.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage DBSideContract12 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest DBSideContract12`.

# Skyrim:Kill the Bandit Leader (Jarl)

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Slay a [bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") leader for [Siddgeir](/wiki/Skyrim:Siddgeir "Skyrim:Siddgeir"), the [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") of [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath").** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Siddgeir](/wiki/Skyrim:Siddgeir "Skyrim:Siddgeir") |
| Location(s): | [Radiant](#Radiant_Options) |
| Reward: | Leveled Gold Option to purchase the deed to [Lakeview Manor](/wiki/Skyrim:Lakeview_Manor "Skyrim:Lakeview Manor")[HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") |
| [Disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition"): | 1→2; 0→1 ([Siddgeir](/wiki/Skyrim:Siddgeir "Skyrim:Siddgeir")) |
| ID: | Favor154 |
| Difficulty: | Medium |
| --- | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | **← Previous** [Siddgeir's Rare Gift](/wiki/Skyrim:Rare_Gifts "Skyrim:Rare Gifts") or have started [Build Your Own Home (Falkreath)](/wiki/Skyrim:Build_Your_Own_Home "Skyrim:Build Your Own Home")[HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") | **Next →** [Thane of Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane_of_Falkreath "Skyrim:Thane of Falkreath") | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | ← Previous | [Siddgeir's Rare Gift](/wiki/Skyrim:Rare_Gifts "Skyrim:Rare Gifts") or have started [Build Your Own Home (Falkreath)](/wiki/Skyrim:Build_Your_Own_Home "Skyrim:Build Your Own Home")[HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") | | → Next | [Thane of Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane_of_Falkreath "Skyrim:Thane of Falkreath") | | |

*"The cut they were giving me was good at first, but now it's time to clean things up."*

## Radiant Options

This is a radiant quest which is received from [Siddgeir](/wiki/Skyrim:Siddgeir "Skyrim:Siddgeir") if he is the [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") of [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath"). The bandit camp is chosen from the following list: [Bilegulch Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Bilegulch_Mine "Skyrim:Bilegulch Mine"), [Cracked Tusk Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Cracked_Tusk_Keep "Skyrim:Cracked Tusk Keep"), [Embershard Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Embershard_Mine "Skyrim:Embershard Mine"), [Knifepoint Ridge](/wiki/Skyrim:Knifepoint_Ridge "Skyrim:Knifepoint Ridge"), [Bannermist Tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Bannermist_Tower "Skyrim:Bannermist Tower").

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Speak to [Siddgeir](/wiki/Skyrim:Siddgeir "Skyrim:Siddgeir"), the [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") of [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath").
2. Travel to the assigned dungeon.
3. Kill the [bandit leader](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_Leader "Skyrim:Bandit Leader").
4. Return to Siddgeir.

## Detailed Walkthrough

The normal prerequisite for this quest is [Rare Gifts](/wiki/Skyrim:Rare_Gifts "Skyrim:Rare Gifts"), a [radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant") quest which can be given by six different people. If you have received that quest from any of the other five, then you cannot receive it from Siddgeir, and you must complete the other version before you can get it from Siddgeir. It is advisable that, if possible, Siddgeir's version of Rare Gifts should be completed soon after leaving Helgen, as the mead he wants can be found near the exit to the keep.

If you have [Hearthfire](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") installed, then at level 9 a courier will deliver a [letter](/wiki/Skyrim:Letter_from_Jarl_(Jarl%27s_Name)_of_(Jarl%27s_City) "Skyrim:Letter from Jarl (Jarl's Name) of (Jarl's City)") from the Jarl of [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath"). Reading it will trigger the Falkreath version of [Build Your Own Home](/wiki/Skyrim:Build_Your_Own_Home "Skyrim:Build Your Own Home") and, when this quest is running, talking to [Siddgeir](/wiki/Skyrim:Siddgeir "Skyrim:Siddgeir") will allow you to start the Bandit Leader quest without any prerequisites.

After completing the prerequisite quest or receiving the letter from Siddgeir, talk to him in order to initiate this quest.

Once you have reached the assigned dungeon, you will only have to kill the bandit leader of that dungeon; killing the lesser enemies is not mandatory, but would make your job easier.

### Reward

Return to Siddgeir to collect your reward of gold.

| Levels | Reward |
| --- | --- |
| 1–9 | 500 |
| 10–19 | 750 |
| 20–29 | 1,000 |
| 30–39 | 1,250 |
| 40+ | 1,500 |

## Notes

- Siddgeir is the only Jarl of Falkreath who gives this quest, which is the last prerequisite he requires before starting the [Thane of Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane_of_Falkreath "Skyrim:Thane of Falkreath") quest. If [Dengeir](/wiki/Skyrim:Dengeir_of_Stuhn "Skyrim:Dengeir of Stuhn") is jarl, then he will already consider you a friend, and start that quest without any further prerequisites.
- The quest will not be available if you have another ["kill the leader" bounty quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Bounty:_Bandit_Boss "Skyrim:Bounty: Bandit Boss") active.
- The target location and boss are radiantly chosen the first time entering the Falkreath location, usually long before Siddgeir gives the quest.
- if you have the concurrent quest [Kill Helvard](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_Helvard "Skyrim:Kill Helvard"), remember never to turn in the killing bandit quest right after killing Helvard, or you will lose the chance to elevate Jarl's relationshiprank to 2, thus never be able to receive the next quest to become a thane nor be authorized to buy the property [Lakeview Manor](/wiki/Skyrim:Lakeview_Manor "Skyrim:Lakeview Manor"), the right method is either to turn in the killing bandit quest before killing Helvard, or go somewhere else after killing Helvard, then come back to turn in the killing bandit quest, the reason behind is about relationshiprank, the relationshiprank mechanism is also mentioned in [Kill Helvard page](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_Helvard#Notes "Skyrim:Kill Helvard").

## Bugs

- If you start this quest after Rare Gifts, before you reach level 9 and then get a letter from a courier, a sidequest to see jarl will remain active forever.

- If you did not talk to [Farengar Secret-Fire](/wiki/Skyrim:Farengar_Secret-Fire "Skyrim:Farengar Secret-Fire") during the [Bleak Falls Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleak_Falls_Barrow_(quest) "Skyrim:Bleak Falls Barrow (quest)") quest yet, you will not get the option to ask the jarl for any jobs, nor will you be able to tell him you got the [letter](/wiki/Skyrim:Letter_from_Jarl_(Jarl%27s_Name) "Skyrim:Letter from Jarl (Jarl's Name)"). This will block you from becoming a thane and thus accessing Lakeview Manor until you progress the main quest. If you want to evade starting [Dragon Rising](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Rising "Skyrim:Dragon Rising") to avoid enabling dragons in Skyrim but still want access to Lakeview Manor, you can progress the Bleak Falls Barrow quest to the point where you need to give Farengar the tablet and stop there. This will make Siddgeir give you this quest and you will be able to progress normally to became the thane. **?**

- If you start or complete this quest while having a "kill the leader" bounty quest active for the same location, the kill will just act as if you completed that quest, and not credit you for this quest. **?**

Notes

- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage Favor154 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest Favor154`.

# Skyrim:Kill the Bandit Leader

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This page is currently being rewritten as part of the [Skyrim Quest Redesign Project](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").** The page is being rewritten and checked in several stages. All users are welcome to make changes to the page. If you make a change that is relevant to the project, please update this template accordingly, and make sure you have observed the [project guidelines](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project#Guidelines "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").  Details  **Walkthrough**: written by multiple users, *not checked*  **Reward**: written by [RobinHood70](/wiki/User:RobinHood70 "User:RobinHood70"), *not checked* |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Do a favor by slaying a bandit leader.** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Radiant](#Radiant_Options) |
| Location(s): | [Radiant](#Radiant_Options) |
| Reward: | Leveled gold and/or skill increase, possible follower |
| [Disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition"): | min 1 (quest giver) |
| ID: | Favor104 |

*"Time to die!"*

## Radiant Options

This is a radiant quest that you can receive from any of the following four people. Apart from Ahtar's quest, which has a fixed location, the dungeon is randomly determined based on the quest giver's hold.

| Questgiver | Questgiver home | Dungeon(s) | Region | Dialogue Trigger | Rewards |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| [Ahtar](/wiki/Skyrim:Ahtar "Skyrim:Ahtar") | [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") | [Broken Oar Grotto](/wiki/Skyrim:Broken_Oar_Grotto "Skyrim:Broken Oar Grotto") | [Haafingar](/wiki/Skyrim:Haafingar "Skyrim:Haafingar") | "What's this problem you have?" | Leveled gold and he'll follow |
| [Annekke Crag-Jumper](/wiki/Skyrim:Annekke_Crag-Jumper "Skyrim:Annekke Crag-Jumper") | [Darkwater Crossing](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkwater_Crossing "Skyrim:Darkwater Crossing") | [Cragslane Cavern](/wiki/Skyrim:Cragslane_Cavern "Skyrim:Cragslane Cavern"), [Gallows Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Gallows_Rock "Skyrim:Gallows Rock"), [Lost Knife Hideout](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_Knife_Hideout "Skyrim:Lost Knife Hideout"), [Stony Creek Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Stony_Creek_Cave "Skyrim:Stony Creek Cave"), [Uttering Hills Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Uttering_Hills_Camp "Skyrim:Uttering Hills Camp") | [Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch "Skyrim:Eastmarch") | "You were an adventurer?" | +1 to [Light Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Light_Armor "Skyrim:Light Armor") skill and she'll follow |
| [Brunwulf Free-Winter](/wiki/Skyrim:Brunwulf_Free-Winter "Skyrim:Brunwulf Free-Winter") | [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") | [Cragslane Cavern](/wiki/Skyrim:Cragslane_Cavern "Skyrim:Cragslane Cavern"), [Gallows Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Gallows_Rock "Skyrim:Gallows Rock"), [Lost Knife Hideout](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_Knife_Hideout "Skyrim:Lost Knife Hideout"), [Stony Creek Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Stony_Creek_Cave "Skyrim:Stony Creek Cave"), [Uttering Hills Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Uttering_Hills_Camp "Skyrim:Uttering Hills Camp") | [Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch "Skyrim:Eastmarch") | "Ulfric doesn't care about outsiders?" | +1 to [Heavy Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Heavy_Armor "Skyrim:Heavy Armor") skill and leveled gold |
| [Fanari Strong-Voice](/wiki/Skyrim:Fanari_Strong-Voice "Skyrim:Fanari Strong-Voice")[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") | [Skaal Village](/wiki/Skyrim:Skaal_Village "Skyrim:Skaal Village")[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") | [Bloodskal Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloodskal_Barrow "Skyrim:Bloodskal Barrow"), [Brodir Grove](/wiki/Skyrim:Brodir_Grove "Skyrim:Brodir Grove"), [Damphall Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Damphall_Mine "Skyrim:Damphall Mine"), [Hrodulf's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Hrodulf%27s_House "Skyrim:Hrodulf's House"), [Wreck of the Strident Squall](/wiki/Skyrim:Wreck_of_the_Strident_Squall "Skyrim:Wreck of the Strident Squall") | [Solstheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Solstheim "Skyrim:Solstheim") | "What can I do to help the Skaal?" | Leveled gold |

Quest Reward for Ahtar, Brunwulf, and Fanari

| Levels | Reward |
| --- | --- |
| 1–9 | 500 |
| 10–19 | 750 |
| 20–29 | 1,000 |
| 30–39 | 1,250 |
| 40+ | 1,500 |

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Talk to the quest giver.
2. Travel to the bandit lair or dungeon.
3. Return to the quest giver for your reward.

## Notes

- If you kill [Captain Hargar](/wiki/Skyrim:Captain_Hargar "Skyrim:Captain Hargar") during the quest [Lights Out!](/wiki/Skyrim:Lights_Out! "Skyrim:Lights Out!"), or by clearing out the grotto without the quest, then Ahtar won't give you his quest and his disposition will need to be raised in another way in order to have him become a follower.
- Because this is a favor quest which affects the quest giver's disposition, it will count towards the "Help the People" part of the [thane](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane "Skyrim:Thane") quest for the quest giver's hold.
- The quest [Harsh Master](/wiki/Skyrim:Harsh_Master "Skyrim:Harsh Master") can have identical quest objectives.
- Version 3.0.1 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch") adds the missing bandit camp keywords to [Orphan's Tear](/wiki/Skyrim:Orphan%27s_Tear "Skyrim:Orphan's Tear") and [Ironback Hideout](/wiki/Skyrim:Ironback_Hideout "Skyrim:Ironback Hideout"), resulting in them also becoming possible targets for this quest.
- Brunwulf Free-Winter only gives the quest when he's not a Jarl. However, if Brunwulf gives you the quest and the [Empire captures Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Windhelm "Skyrim:Battle for Windhelm") later on, you can still finish it after he becomes Jarl.
- The Solstheim locations for this quest contain [Reavers](/wiki/Skyrim:Reaver "Skyrim:Reaver") instead of regular bandits. Your journal will still say "bandit leader", though.

## Bugs

- If you are sent to Gallows Rock after you have already completed the [Companions](/wiki/Skyrim:Companions "Skyrim:Companions") quest [The Silver Hand](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Silver_Hand "Skyrim:The Silver Hand"), then the previously-killed generic Silver Hand members, as well as the unique [Krev the Skinner](/wiki/Skyrim:Krev_the_Skinner "Skyrim:Krev the Skinner"), will all have respawned.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.1, addresses this issue. This version makes sure that Krev doesn't respawn, while Version 2.0.9 makes sure that no Silver Hand respawn at all, and that the dungeon will be reset to its original state.
- If you are sent to Uttering Hills Camp and you have already completed [Summerset Shadows](/wiki/Skyrim:Summerset_Shadows "Skyrim:Summerset Shadows") for the [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)"), you will be unable to complete this quest, as the bandit leader [Linwe](/wiki/Skyrim:Linwe "Skyrim:Linwe") will already be dead, but there will be an objective arrow pointing to him as if he still needs to be killed.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.3, fixes this bug.
  -  Selecting Linwe's body in the console then typing `resurrect` will bring him back to life as soon as you resume the game. Killing him again will then count for the quest completion. (Doesn't work if you have already received the favor quest, as resurrecting Linwe—before or after entering the cave—doesn't put the quest arrow back on him and killing him again doesn't complete the quest)
  -  If Linwe's body has already disappeared, typing `setstage Favor104 15` in the console will advance the quest.
  -  If `setstage Favor104 15` doesn't help you, type the following commands: `prid C5688` and then `kill`. This should select the original quest target and kill him for you, advancing the quest to the next stage.
  -  If `prid C5688` doesn't help you, type the following commands: `prid C5675`, then `disable`, and then type `prid C5675`, then `enable`, and finally `resurrect`. This should place Linwe at the empty chair where the quest marker is pointing. Additional Summerset Shadow thieves should spawn as well.
  -  If all previous codes don't work, try `prid 7d67a`, then `resurrect` and finally `kill`.

## Quest Stages

| Kill the Bandit Leader (Favor104) | | |

| 20 | ☑ |  |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 200.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage Favor104 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest Favor104`.

# Skyrim:Kill the Forsworn Leader (Jarl)

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This page is currently being rewritten as part of the [Skyrim Quest Redesign Project](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").** The page is being rewritten and checked in several stages. *"My scouts have tracked down one of the Forsworn leaders, hiding out in their blood-soaked camps. Deal with them."*

## Radiant Options

This is a radiant quest which is received from Igmund, if he is the current Jarl of [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth"). The forsworn outpost is chosen from the following list:

| [The Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Reach "Skyrim:The Reach") |
| --- |
| [Broken Tower Redoubt](/wiki/Skyrim:Broken_Tower_Redoubt "Skyrim:Broken Tower Redoubt") [Bruca's Leap Redoubt](/wiki/Skyrim:Bruca%27s_Leap_Redoubt "Skyrim:Bruca's Leap Redoubt") [Deepwood Redoubt](/wiki/Skyrim:Deepwood_Redoubt "Skyrim:Deepwood Redoubt") [Dragon Bridge Overlook](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Bridge_Overlook "Skyrim:Dragon Bridge Overlook") [Druadach Redoubt](/wiki/Skyrim:Druadach_Redoubt "Skyrim:Druadach Redoubt") [Hag Rock Redoubt](/wiki/Skyrim:Hag_Rock_Redoubt "Skyrim:Hag Rock Redoubt") [Red Eagle Redoubt](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Eagle_Redoubt "Skyrim:Red Eagle Redoubt") [Serpent's Bluff Redoubt](/wiki/Skyrim:Serpent%27s_Bluff_Redoubt "Skyrim:Serpent's Bluff Redoubt") |

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Talk to Jarl Igmund to initiate quest.
2. Travel to the dungeon.
3. Kill the Forsworn Leader.
4. Return to Jarl Igmund in [Understone Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Understone_Keep "Skyrim:Understone Keep") to collect the gold reward.

## Detailed Walkthrough

Travel to Understone Keep in [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") and speak to Jarl Igmund to initiate the quest in which you have to kill a Forsworn Leader. He will direct you to a dungeon in [The Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Reach "Skyrim:The Reach"), which is where the Forsworn Leader is hiding. You must travel there and face the leader.

Once you travel to the dungeon you will most likely have to deal with most leveled Forsworn before you can eliminate the leader.

### Reward

Once you have dealt with him/her, return to Understone Keep to collect your reward from Jarl Igmund.

| Levels | Reward |
| --- | --- |
| 1–9 | 400 |
| 10–19 | 600 |
| 20–29 | 800 |
| 30–39 | 1,000 |
| 40+ | 1,200 |

## Notes

- If Raerek is in a room with an adept lock, wait until he is sitting by the Jarl to receive your reward. He is there by 10am.

## Bugs

- It is possible to accept this quest and then find that all NPCs are non-aggressive towards you at the site. If this is the case feel free to kill or pickpocket any non-named NPCs (normally simply named "Forsworn") because none of the other NPCs will attack you.
- Upon the initial meeting with Jarl Igmund, he may not have the dialogue option to start this quest available. Exiting Understone Keep and fast travelling somewhere else (e.g. Karthwasten) and back may resolve this.
- If you complete the No One Escapes Cidna Mine quest line before ever speaking to Jarl Igmund, he may not ever give the dialogue option to start the quest. No known fix.

## Quest Stages

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage Favor151 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest Favor151`.

# Skyrim:Kill the Giant (Jarl)

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Do a favor for the [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") of [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar") by killing a [giant](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant "Skyrim:Giant").** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Skald](/wiki/Skyrim:Skald "Skyrim:Skald") |
| Location(s): | [Radiant](#Radiant_Options) |
| Reward: | Leveled gold Option to purchase the deed to [Heljarchen Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Heljarchen_Hall "Skyrim:Heljarchen Hall")[HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") |
| [Disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition"): | =2 (Skald) |
| ID: | Favor153 |
| Required Level: | 22 |
| --- | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | **← Previous** [Waking Nightmare](/wiki/Skyrim:Waking_Nightmare "Skyrim:Waking Nightmare") | **Next →** [Thane of the Pale](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane_of_the_Pale "Skyrim:Thane of the Pale") | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | ← Previous | [Waking Nightmare](/wiki/Skyrim:Waking_Nightmare "Skyrim:Waking Nightmare") | | → Next | [Thane of the Pale](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane_of_the_Pale "Skyrim:Thane of the Pale") | | |

.jpg)

Kill a giant for the Jarl of Dawnstar.

## Radiant Options

This is a radiant quest which is received from [Skald](/wiki/Skyrim:Skald "Skyrim:Skald"), if he is currently the [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") of [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar"). The giant camp is randomly determined from the following list: [Blizzard Rest](/wiki/Skyrim:Blizzard_Rest "Skyrim:Blizzard Rest"), [Red Road Pass](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Road_Pass "Skyrim:Red Road Pass"), [Tumble Arch Pass](/wiki/Skyrim:Tumble_Arch_Pass "Skyrim:Tumble Arch Pass").

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Speak with [Skald](/wiki/Skyrim:Skald "Skyrim:Skald"), the [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") of [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar").
2. Kill the [giant](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant "Skyrim:Giant") at the given camp.
3. Return to retrieve the bounty.

## Detailed Walkthrough

The [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") of [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar"), [Skald](/wiki/Skyrim:Skald "Skyrim:Skald"), will ask you to deal with a [giant](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant "Skyrim:Giant") to send a message to all the other giants in the hold, for although they are not a problem now, the jarl believes they will be in the future. The giant can be found at one of three camps (above) and can be taken down by any means necessary.

### Reward

Once the giant is dead, return to Skald for your reward of gold:

| Levels | Reward |
| --- | --- |
| 22-29 | 1000 |
| 30-39 | 1250 |
| 40+ | 1500 |

Completing this quest is required to start the [Thane of the Pale](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane_of_the_Pale "Skyrim:Thane of the Pale") quest and [Purchase land in Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Build_Your_Own_Home "Skyrim:Build Your Own Home")[HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") if Skald is still Jarl.

## Notes

- The quest has a minimum level of 22. If you are not level 22 yet, then you cannot receive this quest from Skald. If Brina is jarl (or Skald has been removed from power and then reinstated), this quest is not required to become Thane.
- This quest requires a giant to kill. If you have cleared all of the giants from all of the giant camps, then you cannot receive this quest from Skald. To solve this issue, wait or sleep indoors for 30 days and all giant camps will have been respawned.
- This quest cannot be started if you have a bounty in The Pale.
- The dialogue for starting this quest might not appear. A probable reason is you might have another [Favors](/wiki/Skyrim:Favors "Skyrim:Favors") quest running that tasks you to kill a certain enemy. This prevents this quest from starting.
  - Another possible fix is to fast travel to a non-cleared giant camp in The Pale and back to Dawnstar, which may make the dialogue option available.

## Bugs

- Sometimes the quest objective will not be removed from the journal.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.0, fixes this bug.

- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage Favor153 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest Favor153`.

# Skyrim:Kill the Vampire

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This page is currently being rewritten as part of the [Skyrim Quest Redesign Project](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").** The page is being rewritten and checked in several stages. All users are welcome to make changes to the page. If you make a change that is relevant to the project, please update this template accordingly, and make sure you have observed the [project guidelines](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project#Guidelines "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").  Details  **Walkthrough**: written by [86.167.101.10](/wiki/Special:Contributions/86.167.101.10 "Special:Contributions/86.167.101.10"), checked by [DragonFire](/w/index.php?title=User:DragonFire&action=edit&redlink=1 "User:DragonFire (page does not exist)")  **Reward**: written by [DragonFire](/w/index.php?title=User:DragonFire&action=edit&redlink=1 "User:DragonFire (page does not exist)"), *not checked* |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Do menial work for [Sybille Stentor](/wiki/Skyrim:Sybille_Stentor "Skyrim:Sybille Stentor") by assaulting [a vampire lair](/wiki/Skyrim:Pinemoon_Cave "Skyrim:Pinemoon Cave").** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Sybille Stentor](/wiki/Skyrim:Sybille_Stentor "Skyrim:Sybille Stentor") |
| Location(s): | [Blue Palace](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Palace "Skyrim:Blue Palace"), [Pinemoon Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Pinemoon_Cave "Skyrim:Pinemoon Cave") |
| Reward: | [Jewelry](/wiki/Skyrim:Jewelry "Skyrim:Jewelry"), a free [Illusion](/wiki/Skyrim:Illusion "Skyrim:Illusion") training session |
| [Disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition"): | =1 ([Sybille Stentor](/wiki/Skyrim:Sybille_Stentor "Skyrim:Sybille Stentor")) |
| ID: | Favor109 |
| Required Level: | 10 |

The Master Vampire in Pinemoon Cave

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Speak to [Sybille Stentor](/wiki/Skyrim:Sybille_Stentor "Skyrim:Sybille Stentor").
2. Kill the Master Vampire in [Pinemoon Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Pinemoon_Cave "Skyrim:Pinemoon Cave").
3. Return to Sybille Stentor for your reward.

## Detailed Walkthrough

Speak to [Sybille Stentor](/wiki/Skyrim:Sybille_Stentor "Skyrim:Sybille Stentor") in the [Blue Palace](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Palace "Skyrim:Blue Palace") throne room and ask what her problem is. She will tell you about a local nest of [vampires](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire") which you should wipe out.

The first area of Pinemoon Cave

Make your way to [Pinemoon Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Pinemoon_Cave "Skyrim:Pinemoon Cave"), west of Solitude. It is a very small cave with only four chambers, and an assortment of vampires and wolves. You only need to kill the Master Vampire to complete the quest. He can be found in the third chamber, a large room with pews facing an altar. The Master Vampire can be found on the altar area. However, he has two companions who will also attack if you are detected. They will reanimate a corpse of a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_(dead) "Skyrim:Nord (dead)") which lies on a table in the southern part of the chamber.

Vampires attacking

If you do clear out the cave, there is a locked chest next to the altar. Also do not forget the fourth chamber, the sleeping quarters, which contains the [Illusion](/wiki/Skyrim:Illusion "Skyrim:Illusion") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Incident at Necrom](/wiki/Skyrim:Incident_at_Necrom "Skyrim:Incident at Necrom")* and another chest.

### Reward

Exit the way you came in and return to Sybille Stentor for your reward, which is [jewelry](/wiki/Skyrim:Jewelry "Skyrim:Jewelry") and a single free skill boost in Illusion.

## Notes

- Because this is a favor quest which affects Sybille's disposition, it will count towards the "Help the People" part of the [Thane of Haafingar](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane_of_Haafingar "Skyrim:Thane of Haafingar") quest.

## Quest Stages

| Kill the Vampire (Favor109) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | *Objective 10:* Kill the leader of Pinemoon Cave |
| 15 |  | *Objective 15:* Tell Sybille the vampire is dead |
| 20 | ☑ |  |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 200.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage Favor109 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest Favor109`.

# Skyrim:Kindred Judgment

## Overview
