Lord Harkon using the full extent of his power

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Speak to [Serana](/wiki/Skyrim:Serana "Skyrim:Serana").
2. Confront [Harkon](/wiki/Skyrim:Lord_Harkon "Skyrim:Lord Harkon") with [Auriel's Bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Auriel%27s_Bow "Skyrim:Auriel's Bow").
3. Slay Harkon.

## Detailed Walkthrough

**Vampire Side:**
After obtaining [Auriel's Bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Auriel%27s_Bow "Skyrim:Auriel's Bow"), [Serana](/wiki/Skyrim:Serana "Skyrim:Serana") tells you that it is time to confront her father. Head back to [Volkihar Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Volkihar_Keep "Skyrim:Volkihar Keep"). Once inside, it is not possible to initiate dialogue with any of the other vampires, who will instead direct you to [Lord Harkon](/wiki/Skyrim:Lord_Harkon "Skyrim:Lord Harkon"). He can be found upstairs in the Volkihar Cathedral, where he awaits you and Serana in his [Vampire Lord](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire_Lord "Skyrim:Vampire Lord") form. When you confront Lord Harkon, he will begin by insulting you for your disloyalty towards him. When Serana tells him that she will not let herself be sacrificed and that you are on her side, Lord Harkon will give recognition to your persuasive abilities by saying that *"This dragon has fangs"*. He makes a final insult to [Valerica](/wiki/Skyrim:Valerica "Skyrim:Valerica"), and chides Serana for becoming more like her mother. At this point, Lord Harkon will demand that you give him Auriel's Bow. If you refuse to give it to him, he will attack you. Likewise, if you give him the bow, he will betray you and attack. Because both dialogue options end in him attacking you, it is not recommended to give him Auriel's Bow, as it can be very useful during the battle.

**Dawnguard Side:**
The Dawnguard side of this quest is much like the Vampire side, except that after acquiring the bow, Serana will tell you to head back to [Isran](/wiki/Skyrim:Isran "Skyrim:Isran"). Once at [Fort Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Dawnguard "Skyrim:Fort Dawnguard"), talk to Isran, who will gather the rest of the Dawnguard. If you chose to become a vampire in order to gain access to the [Soul Cairn](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Cairn "Skyrim:Soul Cairn"), Isran will refuse to speak with you until you have been [cured](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampirism#Curing_Vampirism "Skyrim:Vampirism"). After a short speech, everyone will head out to [Castle Volkihar](/wiki/Skyrim:Castle_Volkihar "Skyrim:Castle Volkihar"). Once you arrive there, the Dawnguard, including one [armored troll](/wiki/Skyrim:Armored_Troll "Skyrim:Armored Troll"), will start the attack on the castle, beginning with four vampires ([Rargal Thrallmaster](/wiki/Skyrim:Rargal_Thrallmaster "Skyrim:Rargal Thrallmaster"), [Modhna](/wiki/Skyrim:Modhna "Skyrim:Modhna"), [Namasur](/wiki/Skyrim:Namasur "Skyrim:Namasur"), and [Stalf](/wiki/Skyrim:Stalf "Skyrim:Stalf")), a few [Gargoyles](/wiki/Skyrim:Gargoyle "Skyrim:Gargoyle") and one [Death hound](/wiki/Skyrim:Garmr "Skyrim:Garmr") who defend the outdoor approach to the castle. When they have been defeated, you will then lead the charge into Castle Volkihar, fighting the remaining vampires ([Hestla](/wiki/Skyrim:Hestla "Skyrim:Hestla"), [Salonia Caelia](/wiki/Skyrim:Salonia_Caelia "Skyrim:Salonia Caelia"), [Fura Bloodmouth](/wiki/Skyrim:Fura_Bloodmouth "Skyrim:Fura Bloodmouth"), [Orthjolf](/wiki/Skyrim:Orthjolf "Skyrim:Orthjolf"), [Vingalmo](/wiki/Skyrim:Vingalmo "Skyrim:Vingalmo"), [Garan Marethi](/wiki/Skyrim:Garan_Marethi "Skyrim:Garan Marethi"), [Ronthil](/wiki/Skyrim:Ronthil "Skyrim:Ronthil"), and [Feran Sadri](/wiki/Skyrim:Feran_Sadri "Skyrim:Feran Sadri")) and the other [Death Hound](/wiki/Skyrim:CuSith "Skyrim:CuSith"). After all the vampires have been killed, follow Isran to a gated off doorway with a pull chain to the right of it. Pull it to raise the portcullis, then head up the steps and through the doors into the Volkihar Cathedral, where you will find [Lord Harkon](/wiki/Skyrim:Lord_Harkon "Skyrim:Lord Harkon"). Alternatively, you can ignore the vampires inside the castle and go directly to the Cathedral. The conversation with Lord Harkon on the Dawnguard side is somewhat different than the conversation on the Vampire side, mainly in the tone of the conversation and in Lord Harkon's dialogue with the player. Instead of insulting the player for their lack of loyalty, [Lord Harkon](/wiki/Skyrim:Lord_Harkon "Skyrim:Lord Harkon") will admit that it was only a matter of time before [Serana](/wiki/Skyrim:Serana "Skyrim:Serana") would one day return with hatred in her heart. He then questions the player's allegiance to Serana by asking if she and [Valerica](/wiki/Skyrim:Valerica "Skyrim:Valerica") are next after dealing with him. No matter what dialogue options you choose, [Lord Harkon](/wiki/Skyrim:Lord_Harkon "Skyrim:Lord Harkon") will eventually demand that you give him [Auriel's Bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Auriel%27s_Bow "Skyrim:Auriel's Bow"), where you are faced with the same choice. Giving him Auriel's Bow is not recommended for the same reasons listed above.

It might be a good idea to time your assault against Castle Volkihar so that it occurs during the day so you can take advantage of [Sunhallowed Arrows](/w/index.php?title=Skyrim:Sunhallowed_Arrow&action=edit&redlink=1 "Skyrim:Sunhallowed Arrow (page does not exist)") used on the sun to help take down the vampires who attack outside. To make sure the assault takes place during the day, you can travel to a nearby location (example: [Icewater Jetty](/wiki/Skyrim:Icewater_Jetty "Skyrim:Icewater Jetty")), wait until morning (if you arrive there at night), and continue to the castle from there. If you have the [Clear Skies](/wiki/Skyrim:Clear_Skies "Skyrim:Clear Skies") shout, you can use it to clear away the clouds and snow to make the vampires who attack outside easier to eliminate.

### Fighting Lord Harkon

*"No... Serana... your own father...."*

Fighting Lord Harkon is the same regardless of whether you are a vampire or a member of the Dawnguard. If you are not prepared, Lord Harkon can be a difficult opponent to defeat. If you gave him Auriel's Bow, then you will be at a slight disadvantage. As soon as he exits dialogue with you, Lord Harkon will immediately summon [skeletons](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton") and [gargoyles](/wiki/Skyrim:Gargoyle "Skyrim:Gargoyle") to kill you, and will continue to do so throughout the fight. However, Serana is quite capable of handling them on her own, which leaves you to focus solely on Lord Harkon. Lord Harkon will continuously move throughout the room, firing Vampiric Drain at you and will frequently turn into a swarm of bats. As you deplete his health, Lord Harkon will turn into a swarm of bats and will materialize at the altar. As he hovers over the altar, he will create an impregnable shield of Blood Magic until he regains his health. If you have Auriel's Bow, equip it and fire at the shield, which will destroy it. Try not to waste Sunhallowed arrows during this fight, as Lord Harkon will do this repeatedly, and any arrow fired from Auriel's Bow will penetrate the shield. When his health is low, he will begin to frequently turn into mist; simply follow him until he re-materializes. Once the killing blow is struck, Lord Harkon will turn into a swarm of bats and materialize by the altar one final time, where he makes a final cry to his daughter's betrayal, and then melts into a pile of red ash. Alternatively, at the beginning of the battle, you will be free to move around when Lord Harkon is speaking to Serana, and you can even slay him outright with high enough sneak-attack damage. Again, Lord Harkon will turn materialize by the altar one final time, where he makes a final cry to his daughter's betrayal, and then melts into a pile of red ash.

After the battle is over, [Garan Marethi](/wiki/Skyrim:Garan_Marethi "Skyrim:Garan Marethi") (if you are a vampire) or [Isran](/wiki/Skyrim:Isran "Skyrim:Isran") (if you are a member of the Dawnguard) will enter the room, and will commend you for defeating Lord Harkon. He will then explain that there will be a new beginning for the Volkihar vampires or the Dawnguard, thus completing the Dawnguard questline. Serana will tell you that she will stay at Castle Volkihar or Fort Dawnguard, but will accompany you on your travels should you ask her.

### Aftermath

- While you do not corrupt [Auriel's Bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Auriel%27s_Bow "Skyrim:Auriel's Bow") bringing it to its full potential, you can still use it to block out the sun once per day with [Bloodcursed Elven Arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloodcursed_Elven_Arrow "Skyrim:Bloodcursed Elven Arrow"). While the sun is blocked out, you will not suffer from any of the penalties of sun damage during the day. After one day, the sun will return and you will need to shoot it again. Bloodcursed arrows are necessary for this function.
- A dialogue option with Serana will open up that allows you to turn Elven arrows into Bloodcursed arrows.
- The blacksmith associated with your chosen faction will stock an additional 200 Elven arrows, which you can convert into Sunhallowed or Bloodcursed arrows.
- Certain Volkihar Clan or Dawnguard side quests will become available.
- If you sided with the vampires, Garan Marethi will ask you if you want him to restore the entrance to the courtyard the next time you talk to him. The repair is free, and will be complete the next time you enter the keep.
- On the Vampire side, you will be new owner of the castle, and will now be able to take everything for free without being flagged for theft.
- On the Dawnguard side, you can ask Serana to transform you into a Vampire Lord or convince her to give up her vampirism.
- On Lord Harkon's body you will find one of the sets of [Vampire Royal Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire_Royal_Armor "Skyrim:Vampire Royal Armor") and [Harkon's Sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Harkon%27s_Sword "Skyrim:Harkon's Sword"), a unique katana. If you gave him Auriel's Bow, you can retrieve it from there as well.
- If you return to the Soul Cairn, [Valerica](/wiki/Skyrim:Valerica "Skyrim:Valerica") will be amazed at Harkon's defeat and return to Castle Volkihar. She will return to her lab, where she will restock it, and offer potions and ingredients for free. She will also give you advice on how to survive if you return to the Soul Cairn. The garden in the courtyard will be upgraded as well. Unfortunately, she won't provide blood for Bloodcursed Elven Arrows.
- [Random encounters](/wiki/Skyrim:World_Interactions "Skyrim:World Interactions") with members from the opposing faction in hold capitals and the wilderness will be less frequent. Random vampire attacks on settlements will only occur during an eclipse.

### Achievements

One [achievement](/wiki/Skyrim:Achievements "Skyrim:Achievements") is unlocked when you complete this quest:

-  **Kindred Judgement**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") (40 points/Silver)

## Notes

- Killing Lord Harkon is necessary regardless of which faction you side with.
- During the battle, the music normally heard when battling [dragons](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon") will play. If you let the battle go on long enough, one or two tracks of ordinary battle music will play, before being replaced again by Dragon music.
- If completed for the Dawnguard, everything in Volkihar Keep will still be labeled as owned and thus stolen if taken. Everyone's corpses, except for Harkon's, will never despawn, even those outside.
- It is possible, if the Sneak skill is high enough and with high enough sneak attack damage, to kill Harkon during his dialogue with Serana without any major combat.
- If you dual-cast [Pacify](/wiki/Skyrim:Pacify "Skyrim:Pacify") on the vampires during the Dawnguard version with the [Master of the Mind](/wiki/Skyrim:Master_of_the_Mind "Skyrim:Master of the Mind") perk active, they won't lower their weapons/spells, but will instead tell you to present Auriel's Bow to Lord Harkon, as if you sided with them. Unfortunately, you won't be able to buy [Heal Undead](/wiki/Skyrim:Heal_Undead "Skyrim:Heal Undead") from [Ronthil](/wiki/Skyrim:Ronthil "Skyrim:Ronthil") this way.
- The Dawnguard version of this quest may appear to freeze when Isran is summoning everybody: they will all stay there in a circle and apparently do nothing. This happens because one of the Dawnguard members has been relocated in some way (such as acting as steward[HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") at a homestead), and they are traveling to their spot in the circle. Isran will not start his speech until they arrive; waiting for several hours will allow the missing Dawnguard member to arrive to the meeting more quickly, which will then proceed as intended.
- Isran's speech after killing Lord Harkon will mention that the Dawnguard will now dedicate itself to protecting Auriel's Bow, but he never asks for it, and there is no way to give it to him.
- Isran's disposition towards Serana will change over the course of the questline, displaying some decently scripted character development. When Serana first arrives in Fort Dawnguard Isran refers to her as an "it" rather than a person, and refuses to even refer to her by her name. This attitude seems to cast Isran in a dark light initially, as the conversation takes place between the player and the other involved characters together in a bloody torture room in Fort Dawnguard. In this quest, when Isran questions whether Serana will be able to commit patricide for the greater good, not only does he refer to her by her actual name, but he even uses the pronouns "she" and "her", suggesting that he has grown to respect Serana for her personal sacrifices made for their cause. With Harkon's defeat at the end of the quest, Isran will completely change his tone and express sincere gratitude towards her. He will even allow her to stay in Fort Dawnguard even if you do not take her as a follower, regardless of her vampire status.

## Bugs

- Isran may not give his speech to begin the Dawnguard side of this quest. This is usually caused by the members of the Dawnguard failing to assemble. Taking a Dawnguard member as a follower and leaving them somewhere (or having them join the Blades), or Florentius wandering off or not making it back to the Keep after recruiting him are the most common reasons.
  - Waiting usually fixes this. You may need to wait 24 hours or longer for everyone to show up, but sometimes waiting in 1-hour increments a few times will allow the speech to proceed even though the missing members are still missing.
- You may be unable to enter Volkihar Keep despite the gate being up and the door unlocked. This may be due to having earlier trouble with [Bloodline](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloodline "Skyrim:Bloodline") and having used a work-around to progress forward in that quest. **?**
  -  Use the command `player.moveto 02003ba8`. This will place you inside the keep in a room with a fireplace, with a door that opens to the upstairs level of the main hall where Isran should be found fighting.
- When Lord Harkon's health is reduced to zero, he may become invincible, forcing you to reload a previous save from before entering Volkihar Cathedral to begin the fight again.
  - Save the game and move your character, then reload the game. When it has been reloaded, Harkon's death scene will play.
  - If that doesn't work, try disabling and re-enabling the Actor through the CC. Make sure you've already saved the game prior to that. It usually results in one ultimate death blow needed to finally bring him down and initiate the death sequence.
- Sometimes Lord Harkon will not take any damage from any attacks. Reloading a previous save will fix this. Saving before entering the final room of Castle Volkihar is recommended.
- If in stealth mode and unseen by Harkon during his dialogue with Serana, instead of speaking to you he will simply pause. Since you cannot leave the cathedral, the game will essentially be frozen. You have to either be seen by Harkon, which will trigger him to commence his dialogue with your character, or you can attack him. If you attack, you won't get the dialogue options, but the battle will play out normally.
- It is best to avoid using dragon shouts during the final battle. All sorts of bugs and collisions can occur, and on the PC, it may freeze or crash to desktop. When transitioning into bat form, hitting Harkon with Unrelenting Force may blast him into the scenery. **?**
- If his script is already buggy and you work at it long enough, it is possible to summon [Durnehviir](/wiki/Skyrim:Durnehviir_(dragon) "Skyrim:Durnehviir (dragon)") into Volkihar Cathedral during the final battle. The game will immediately crash. **?**
- Serana may stay locked in combat after Harkon dies, making it so dialogue is unavailable. Attack Serana until she goes down (or exit the room and initiate conversation), and she will speak.
  - If you exit the room and initiate conversation with Serana, her dialogue will be normal, but the other NPC may leave and you will lose the chance to speak to Isran or Garan.
- After entering Volkihar Cathedral to confront Lord Harkon, the Vampire Lord and the Revert Form powers no longer function. **?**
  -  To fix this issue, open up the console, select your character (by clicking on it or typing `prid 14`) and type `resurrect`.
- Sometimes after you've used Auriel's Bow, it can cause your weapons to malfunction, resulting in you not being able to use them. This prevents you from being able to attack with either weapons or magic. Reloading the latest saved game or transforming into a werewolf will fix this. **?**
- This quest will not start on the Vampire side if either of the two hireable Death hounds have been killed and their bodies have been removed from the game.
  - The [Official Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim:Special Edition Patch"), version 1.6.1130.0, fixes this bug.
  -  You can start the quest manually using `setstage DLC1VQ08 10`.
- The bodies of the Volkihar vampires are never cleaned up once this quest is completed on the Dawnguard side.
  -  The [Unofficial Dawnguard Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dawnguard_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dawnguard Patch"), version 2.0.0, fixes this bug.
- If the armored troll survives, it never disappears from the castle once this quest is completed on the Dawnguard side.
  -  The [Unofficial Dawnguard Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dawnguard_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dawnguard Patch"), version 2.0.9, fixes this bug.
- This quest can stall on the Vampire side if [Stalf](/wiki/Skyrim:Stalf "Skyrim:Stalf") and/or [Salonia Caelia](/wiki/Skyrim:Salonia_Caelia "Skyrim:Salonia Caelia") have been dead long enough for their bodies to be removed from the game, even though you killed them yourself [a long time ago](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bloodstone_Chalice "Skyrim:The Bloodstone Chalice").
  -  The [Unofficial Dawnguard Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dawnguard_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dawnguard Patch"), version 2.1.0, fixes this bug.
- After defeating Harkon, you may be unable to interact with Isran. You may interact normally with him back in Fort Dawnguard.
- The chest found after defeating Harkon may remain empty.
- Sometimes (very rarely) the Volkihar Cathedral Boss Room will not load after defeating all vampires in the Volkihar Keep **?**
  -  On PC this can be fixed using console command `coc DLC1VampireCastleBossRoom`
- You may sell the two Elder Scrolls to [Dexion Evicus](/wiki/Skyrim:Dexion_Evicus "Skyrim:Dexion Evicus") for 6000 gold after completing this quest, but only if allied with the Dawnguard. Since they will always remain quest items, this is the only way to remove them from the inventory.
  -  The [Unofficial Dawnguard Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dawnguard_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dawnguard Patch"), version 1.2.2, addresses this issue. ([details](https://afktrack.afkmods.com/index.php?a=issues&i=12086)) It adds the necessary dialogue in order to sell them while sided with the vampires.
- Gunmar and Sorine deliver their post quest greetings more than once due to the lack of a "say once" flag even though this isn't an issue with Isran.
  -  The [Unofficial Dawnguard Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dawnguard_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dawnguard Patch"), version 2.1.3, addresses this issue. Tracking variables have been added to prevent Gunmar and Sorine from doing so. It is unknown why they weren't added to it as well.
- Agmaer, Beleval and Ingjard may be absent during the assault on Castle Volkihar in the Dawnguard version.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.1, addresses this issue. They never got the packages added to their aliases in the quest even though all of the markers, packages, and other conditions had been set up for them.
- Celann may be given 15 crossbows in his inventory, which is clearly an error as it was a copypasta matching the amount of steel bolts he's given.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.3.7, fixes this bug.

## Quest Stages

| Kindred Judgment (DLC1VQ08) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | *Objective 10:* Speak to Serana |
| 20 |  | With Auriel's Bow in my possession, I need to rally the forces of the Dawnguard before I attempt to confront Harkon and put a stop to the prophecy. *Objective 20:* Speak to Isran *(Available only if Dragonborn are joined in Dawnguard.)* |
|  | With Auriel's Bow in my possession, it's time to confront Harkon and reshape the prophecy as I see fit. *Objective 30:* Confront Harkon with Auriel's Bow *(Available only if Dragonborn are joined in Volkihar Clan.)* |
| 40 |  | *Objective 30:* Confront Harkon with Auriel's Bow |
| 60 |  | *Objective 40:* Slay Harkon |
| 200 | ☑ |  |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 25, 30, 50, 55.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage DLC1VQ08 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest DLC1VQ08`.

*This [Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim "Skyrim:Skyrim")-related article is a [stub](/wiki/UESPWiki:Stub "UESPWiki:Stub"). You can help by [expanding it](https://en.uesp.net/w/index.php?title=Skyrim:Kindred_Judgment&action=edit).*

# Skyrim:Kjenstag Ruins

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Nordic Dwelling.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Nordic_Dwelling.png) | Nordic Dwelling: Kjenstag Ruins ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Kjenstag+Ruins)) | | |
| [Clearable](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons#Clearing "Skyrim:Dungeons") | No |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| [Level](/wiki/Skyrim:Encounter_Zone_Level "Skyrim:Encounter Zone Level") | Min: 5 |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| KjenstagRuinsExterior | |
| Region | |
| [Hjaalmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjaalmarch "Skyrim:Hjaalmarch") | |
| Location | |
| East-northeast of [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal") Southwest of [Hjaalmarch Stormcloak Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjaalmarch_Stormcloak_Camp "Skyrim:Hjaalmarch Stormcloak Camp") | |

Kjenstag Ruins

**Kjenstag Ruins** is a small [outdoor Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Dwellings "Skyrim:Nordic Dwellings") east-northeast of [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal").

## Walkthrough

It is a circular ruin with an arched entrance to the north. Inside there is a short central wall with an empty stone table in front and an adept-locked wooden [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") behind. It is possible to climb to the top of the walls via the southeast where the structure has partially crumbled or to the west by climbing a rock formation and jumping from there. However, apart from the view, there is nothing of interest up there. There are also no harvestable plants in the immediate vicinity.

Upon approaching the ruins at night between 8pm and 5am, an unnamed [ghost](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghost "Skyrim:Ghost")(reif 000725f7) will run from the entrance, leading you to an [unmarked barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Unmarked_Places_Hjaalmarch#Ghost_Barrow "Skyrim:Unmarked Places Hjaalmarch") just southeast of [Hjaalmarch Stormcloak Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjaalmarch_Stormcloak_Camp "Skyrim:Hjaalmarch Stormcloak Camp"). The barrow is being robbed by two [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit"), one of whom carries the [Block](/wiki/Skyrim:Block "Skyrim:Block") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[A Dance in Fire, v2](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Dance_in_Fire,_v2 "Skyrim:A Dance in Fire, v2")*. The barrow itself features a trap door covering a spiral staircase leading down to a sarcophagus containing a [mummified draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Containers#Draugr "Skyrim:Containers") and three items of leveled loot: a [weapon](/wiki/Skyrim:Weapons "Skyrim:Weapons"), a [necklace](/wiki/Skyrim:Necklace "Skyrim:Necklace"), and a [shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Shield "Skyrim:Shield"). As the ghost only appears once, it might be easy to miss.

## Notes

- If you happen upon the unmarked barrow between 5am and 8pm and open the trap door before approaching Kjenstag Ruins, the ghost will not appear. The sarcophagus containing the mummified draugr and loot will be open when you return to the barrow.[*verification needed*]
- If you kill the ghost before arriving at the unmarked barrow, you can get a complete set of [Ancient Nord Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancient_Nord_Armor "Skyrim:Ancient Nord Armor") from its ashes.
- Down the hill from the ruin to the north, behind a rocky cliff face and between two dead trees, is an isolated [wood chopping block](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Chopping_Block "Skyrim:Wood Chopping Block").
- Kjenstag Ruins also [appears](/wiki/Online:Kjenstag_Ruins "Online:Kjenstag Ruins") in [ESO](/wiki/Online:Online "Online:Online").

## Bugs

- The ghost may disappear when you try to follow it. **?**

# Skyrim:Klimmek's House

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This article is being developed as part of the Skyrim Houses Redesign Project. If you see this tag it means the article can still be improved. Please see the [project page](/wiki/UESPWiki:SHRP "UESPWiki:SHRP") for guidelines.** |

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |

| # of Zones | 1 |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| IvarsteadKlimmeksHouse | |

| [The Rift](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Rift "Skyrim:The Rift") | |
| Location | |
| [Ivarstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivarstead "Skyrim:Ivarstead") | |
| Special Features | |
| # of [Cooking Pots/Spits](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking "Skyrim:Cooking") | 1 |

Klimmek's House

**Klimmek's House** is a residence in the southeastern part of [Ivarstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivarstead "Skyrim:Ivarstead"), located across from [Vilemyr Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Vilemyr_Inn "Skyrim:Vilemyr Inn").

It is the home of [Klimmek](/wiki/Skyrim:Klimmek "Skyrim:Klimmek") and [Bassianus Axius](/wiki/Skyrim:Bassianus_Axius "Skyrim:Bassianus Axius"). It consists of one zone, *[Klimmek's House](#Klimmek.27s_House)*.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Bassianus Axius](/wiki/Skyrim:Bassianus_Axius "Skyrim:Bassianus Axius")\*  [Klimmek](/wiki/Skyrim:Klimmek "Skyrim:Klimmek") |

\* Moves to [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") after [The Book of Love](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Book_of_Love "Skyrim:The Book of Love").

## Related Quests

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

## Klimmek's House

Kitchen and dining area

Klimmek's house is laid out in an L-shape, with the front door entering to an open kitchen and dining area along one side of the "L", and the bedroom area situated on the other. To the left of the door as you come in is a dining table holding two loaves and one piece of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), some [sliced goat cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Sliced_Goat_Cheese "Skyrim:Sliced Goat Cheese"), a [chicken's egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken%27s_Egg "Skyrim:Chicken's Egg"), a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), and a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"). There are also two more chicken's eggs on the floor beneath the table, and a respawning food barrel in the corner to the right of the table. To the right of the door is a non-respawning cupboard holding pots and tankards on the shelves, along with a bucket and a sample of [troll fat](/wiki/Skyrim:Troll_Fat "Skyrim:Troll Fat") at the top. A respawning food barrel sits to the left of the cupboard.

To the left of the fireplace is another respawning food barrel, atop which sits a full [goat cheese wheel](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wheel"). Three gold coins rest on the mantel of the fireplace, and a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking "Skyrim:Cooking") sits on the right side of the fireplace base. To the right of the fireplace is another dining table holding two [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato"), one [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") bulb, three [seared slaughterfish](/wiki/Skyrim:Seared_Slaughterfish "Skyrim:Seared Slaughterfish"), some [sliced eidar cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Sliced_Eidar_Cheese "Skyrim:Sliced Eidar Cheese"), three loaves of bread, a head of [cabbage](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage"), and a [leek](/wiki/Skyrim:Leek "Skyrim:Leek"). Four more potatoes sit in a kettle to the left side of the table, and four woven baskets sit on the floor to the right. Above the table are some hanging ingredients, including dried [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam"), two garlic braids, and two portions of dried [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear"). Next to these hanging ingredients are two hanging racks, one of which holds two freshly caught [rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)") while the other holds two [pheasants](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant "Skyrim:Pheasant").

On the bottom of a set of shelves to the right are two bottles of alto wine and three bottles of wine, along with the books *[The Code of Malacath](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Code_of_Malacath "Skyrim:The Code of Malacath")*, *[Kolb & the Dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Kolb_%26_the_Dragon "Skyrim:Kolb & the Dragon")*, *[Olaf and the Dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Olaf_and_the_Dragon "Skyrim:Olaf and the Dragon")*, and *[A Gentleman's Guide to Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Gentleman%27s_Guide_to_Whiterun "Skyrim:A Gentleman's Guide to Whiterun")*. Next to these shelves is a non-respawning wardrobe.

Bedroom area

The bedroom area of the house starts with a bed owned by [Bassianus Axius](/wiki/Skyrim:Bassianus_Axius "Skyrim:Bassianus Axius") along the southeast wall, next to a non-respawning end table with a copy of *[Nords Arise!](/wiki/Skyrim:Nords_Arise! "Skyrim:Nords Arise!")* sitting on top for reading material. The other owned bed (belonging to the [IvarsteadKlimmekHouseFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:IvarsteadKlimmekHouseFaction "Skyrim:IvarsteadKlimmekHouseFaction")) is found on the southwest wall, flanked by a non-respawning end table on either side and with a non-respawning chest at the foot of the bed. The left end table holds a farm [hat](/wiki/Skyrim:Hat#000330b3 "Skyrim:Hat") and a [potion of haggling](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Haggling "Skyrim:Potion of Haggling"), while the right one holds a basket and four gold coins. A pair of farm [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots#0001be1b "Skyrim:Boots") sits on the floor in the left corner, in front of a medium-sized [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"). Along the left wall is a non-respawning wardrobe, atop which lie a [sabre cat pelt](/wiki/Skyrim:Sabre_Cat_Pelt "Skyrim:Sabre Cat Pelt") and a [belted tunic](/wiki/Skyrim:Belted_Tunic "Skyrim:Belted Tunic"), and next to which rests a respawning food barrel with a bucket on top. Along the right wall is a small sitting area, with a table holding two bottles of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead") and a couple of tankards.

## Notes

- The front door has an apprentice lock, the [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Klimmek%27s_House "Skyrim:Key to Klimmek's House") to which is carried by both Klimmek and Bassianus.
- At the front door to the house is a respawning food barrel.
- Behind the house is a dead tree with a growth of [scaly pholiota](/wiki/Skyrim:Scaly_Pholiota "Skyrim:Scaly Pholiota").

## Bugs

- After you clear [Shroud Hearth Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Shroud_Hearth_Barrow "Skyrim:Shroud Hearth Barrow"), Klimmek's house along with it will be marked as cleared on mini-map.

## Overview

Knifepoint Ridge

**Knifepoint Ridge** is a small [bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") [camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Camps "Skyrim:Camps") and [iron](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron "Skyrim:Iron") and [corundum](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum "Skyrim:Corundum") [mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Mines "Skyrim:Mines") northwest of [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath"). It contains only one zone, *[Knifepoint Mine](#Knifepoint_Mine)*.

## Related Quests

- **[Amulet of the Moon](/wiki/Skyrim:Amulet_of_the_Moon "Skyrim:Amulet of the Moon")**: Find the [Moon Amulet](/wiki/Skyrim:Moon_Amulet "Skyrim:Moon Amulet") for [Kharjo](/wiki/Skyrim:Kharjo "Skyrim:Kharjo"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Bandit Attack](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_Attack "Skyrim:Bandit Attack")**[HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire"): Rescue your beloved from kidnappers. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Beyond the Grave](/wiki/Skyrim:Beyond_the_Grave "Skyrim:Beyond the Grave")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Daedric_Plate "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Daedric Plate"): Follow the trail of a set of valuable [Daedric Plate](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedric_Plate_Armor "Skyrim:Daedric Plate Armor") armor.
- **[Boethiah's Calling](/wiki/Skyrim:Boethiah%27s_Calling "Skyrim:Boethiah's Calling")**: Become [Boethiah](/wiki/Lore:Boethiah "Lore:Boethiah")'s new champion.
- **[Kill the Bandit Leader](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_the_Bandit_Leader_(Jarl) "Skyrim:Kill the Bandit Leader (Jarl)")**: Slay a [bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") leader for [Siddgeir](/wiki/Skyrim:Siddgeir "Skyrim:Siddgeir"), the [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") of [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

### Exterior

There are nine bandits roaming the main camp, with several huts containing various loot or crafting tables. Working in from the perimeter where you can find up to five bandits walking around (depending on the time of day), in and near the hut to the south are a smithing [forge](/wiki/Skyrim:Forge "Skyrim:Forge"), a [workbench](/wiki/Skyrim:Workbench "Skyrim:Workbench"), and a [grindstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Grindstone "Skyrim:Grindstone"). This hut also has a novice-level [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") containing [varying loot](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists "Skyrim:Leveled Lists") of reasonable quality (gold, lockpicks, weak potions, and usually one piece of apparel), as well as a table holding a leveled [warhammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Warhammer "Skyrim:Warhammer") and a random leveled [light helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor#Light_Helmets "Skyrim:Armor"). Outside the hut, on another nearby table, there is a copy of the [Archery](/wiki/Skyrim:Archery "Skyrim:Archery") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Vernaccus and Bourlor](/wiki/Skyrim:Vernaccus_and_Bourlor "Skyrim:Vernaccus and Bourlor")*, a leveled [bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Weapons#Bows "Skyrim:Weapons"), and a sheaf of leveled [arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Ammunition#Arrows "Skyrim:Ammunition").

There is an [iron ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Iron Ore Vein") just east of the smithing hut. If you take the stairs to the west of the smithing hut and head to the right, you will find a hut containing a table with a leveled [dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Dagger "Skyrim:Dagger"). This section of the camp features a log gate to the south that leads to a campfire with a bandit near it. The entrance to the second zone, *Knifepoint Mine*, is also found beyond this gate, with a pickaxe on the ground just outside the entrance and another by some crates and sacks to the left. Returning to the smithing hut then heading through a small gap in the palisade to the north, a third and final hut is found containing an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Labs "Skyrim:Alchemy Labs"), two potions or poisons, an [apothecary's satchel](/wiki/Skyrim:Apothecary%27s_Satchel "Skyrim:Apothecary's Satchel"), and a loose sample of frost mirriam.

### Knifepoint Mine

The boulders blocking the path through the mine

The hideout of Boethiah's Champion

Entering the mine leads to a small room, with a tunnel down to the east blocked by a cave-in (unless the quest [Boethiah's Calling](/wiki/Skyrim:Boethiah%27s_Calling "Skyrim:Boethiah's Calling") is active). There will likely be a bandit chief near the campfire in the small room. There are two iron ore veins here, and a dead [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_(dead) "Skyrim:Imperial (dead)") prisoner in a cage next to the fire; the cage contains an additional three iron ore veins, and is secured with a leveled lock. There is an unlocked chest and a weapon rack with a pickaxe along the back wall. Throughout the mine are also many patches of mushrooms to be harvested, including [bleeding crown](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleeding_Crown "Skyrim:Bleeding Crown"), [blisterwort](/wiki/Skyrim:Blisterwort "Skyrim:Blisterwort"), [fly amanita](/wiki/Skyrim:Fly_Amanita "Skyrim:Fly Amanita"), [imp stool](/wiki/Skyrim:Imp_Stool "Skyrim:Imp Stool"), [Namira's rot](/wiki/Skyrim:Namira%27s_Rot "Skyrim:Namira's Rot"), and [white cap](/wiki/Skyrim:White_Cap "Skyrim:White Cap").

If the quest Boethiah's Calling is active, you can descend through the otherwise blocked tunnel to find a bandit by an alchemy lab behind a makeshift wall of crates and barrels to the left. Two shelving units and three barrels near the alchemy lab hold a range of potions, poisons, and ingredients. Two [corundum ore veins](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Corundum Ore Vein") can be found in this area: one at the bottom of the ramp where you entered, and a second to the right of the locked gate in the southeastern corner. You can then continue down the northern path, which contains a [flammable gas trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Flammable_Gas "Skyrim:Flammable Gas") and three more corundum ore veins, or you can open the locked gate, giving you a good vantage point overlooking the main room.

In the main room you will find the [Champion of Boethiah](/wiki/Skyrim:Champion_of_Boethiah "Skyrim:Champion of Boethiah"), if you have the related quest active, as well as a few bandits. There are over a dozen corundum ore veins here. To one side will be a smelter and a grindstone in front of a wooden ramp leading up to a makeshift house; on the other side you will see a wooden walkway leading to the previous locked gate. There is a master-locked chest under the wooden ramp accessible through a gap in the scaffolding to the left of the smelter; just before the chest is a barrel with cheese on top (see [bugs](#Bugs)). Lying on a crate north of the grindstone is a [satchel](/wiki/Skyrim:Containers#Satchel "Skyrim:Containers"). In the makeshift house is another unlocked chest, a single bed, a dresser, several food barrels, and a bow on a table. There is a tanning rack to the right just outside the entrance to the house, while farther to the right is a small tunnel which loops back around to the main chamber and contains several [glowing mushrooms](/wiki/Skyrim:Glowing_Mushroom "Skyrim:Glowing Mushroom").

## Notes

- If you climb the ridge west-southwest of the camp, you'll find some skeletal remains. The skeleton has a leveled bow and a [knapsack](/wiki/Skyrim:Knapsack "Skyrim:Knapsack") (containing common loot), which are splattered with blood, and is on the high rocky promontory directly west overlooking the mine entrance.

## Bugs

- Clearing out this location before Boethiah's Calling has begun may prevent the latter from starting at all.
  - The [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch"), version 1.4, fixes this bug.
- This location may not be marked as cleared on your map if you enter for the first time during the quest Boethiah's Calling.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.5, fixes this bug.
- Upon clearing this mine and returning at a later point, you may find that the tunnel leading down to the left from the first room is still blocked by the cave-in, leaving no way to progress through the mine.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.1, fixes this bug.
  - Exiting and reentering the mine may fix this, possibly requiring multiple attempts.
- If you have already received the quest Boethiah's Calling and have the objective to kill her current champion, you will be unable to complete the quest [Kill the Bandit Leader](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_the_Bandit_Leader_(Jarl) "Skyrim:Kill the Bandit Leader (Jarl)") in Knifepoint Ridge. The quest marker will point to where the bandit chief stands instead of over his head, and even if you kill everyone in the mine, the quest will not be completed. Waiting until Knifepoint Ridge has reset does not fix the problem.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.1, fixes this bug.
  - Typing `setstage Favor154 20` in the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") will finish the quest, allowing you to turn it in to the Jarl; however, you won't get the gold reward.
- In the area under the wooden ramp leading to the barrel with goat cheese and on to the chest, there is one spot where it is possible to get "stuck". If you are unfortunate enough to find it, the only option is to reload a saved game. The trouble spot is on the zigzag before the barrel; if you stick to the outside of the tunnel, you should avoid it. **?**

# Skyrim:Knifepoint Ridge

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Camp.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Camp.png) | Camp: Knifepoint Ridge ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Knifepoint+Ridge)) | | |

Knifepoint Ridge

**Knifepoint Ridge** is a small [bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") [camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Camps "Skyrim:Camps") and [iron](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron "Skyrim:Iron") and [corundum](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum "Skyrim:Corundum") [mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Mines "Skyrim:Mines") northwest of [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath"). It contains only one zone, *[Knifepoint Mine](#Knifepoint_Mine)*.

## Related Quests

- **[Amulet of the Moon](/wiki/Skyrim:Amulet_of_the_Moon "Skyrim:Amulet of the Moon")**: Find the [Moon Amulet](/wiki/Skyrim:Moon_Amulet "Skyrim:Moon Amulet") for [Kharjo](/wiki/Skyrim:Kharjo "Skyrim:Kharjo"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Bandit Attack](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_Attack "Skyrim:Bandit Attack")**[HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire"): Rescue your beloved from kidnappers. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Beyond the Grave](/wiki/Skyrim:Beyond_the_Grave "Skyrim:Beyond the Grave")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Daedric_Plate "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Daedric Plate"): Follow the trail of a set of valuable [Daedric Plate](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedric_Plate_Armor "Skyrim:Daedric Plate Armor") armor.
- **[Boethiah's Calling](/wiki/Skyrim:Boethiah%27s_Calling "Skyrim:Boethiah's Calling")**: Become [Boethiah](/wiki/Lore:Boethiah "Lore:Boethiah")'s new champion.
- **[Kill the Bandit Leader](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_the_Bandit_Leader_(Jarl) "Skyrim:Kill the Bandit Leader (Jarl)")**: Slay a [bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") leader for [Siddgeir](/wiki/Skyrim:Siddgeir "Skyrim:Siddgeir"), the [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") of [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

### Exterior

There are nine bandits roaming the main camp, with several huts containing various loot or crafting tables. Working in from the perimeter where you can find up to five bandits walking around (depending on the time of day), in and near the hut to the south are a smithing [forge](/wiki/Skyrim:Forge "Skyrim:Forge"), a [workbench](/wiki/Skyrim:Workbench "Skyrim:Workbench"), and a [grindstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Grindstone "Skyrim:Grindstone"). This hut also has a novice-level [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") containing [varying loot](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists "Skyrim:Leveled Lists") of reasonable quality (gold, lockpicks, weak potions, and usually one piece of apparel), as well as a table holding a leveled [warhammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Warhammer "Skyrim:Warhammer") and a random leveled [light helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor#Light_Helmets "Skyrim:Armor"). Outside the hut, on another nearby table, there is a copy of the [Archery](/wiki/Skyrim:Archery "Skyrim:Archery") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Vernaccus and Bourlor](/wiki/Skyrim:Vernaccus_and_Bourlor "Skyrim:Vernaccus and Bourlor")*, a leveled [bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Weapons#Bows "Skyrim:Weapons"), and a sheaf of leveled [arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Ammunition#Arrows "Skyrim:Ammunition").

There is an [iron ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Iron Ore Vein") just east of the smithing hut. If you take the stairs to the west of the smithing hut and head to the right, you will find a hut containing a table with a leveled [dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Dagger "Skyrim:Dagger"). This section of the camp features a log gate to the south that leads to a campfire with a bandit near it. The entrance to the second zone, *Knifepoint Mine*, is also found beyond this gate, with a pickaxe on the ground just outside the entrance and another by some crates and sacks to the left. Returning to the smithing hut then heading through a small gap in the palisade to the north, a third and final hut is found containing an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Labs "Skyrim:Alchemy Labs"), two potions or poisons, an [apothecary's satchel](/wiki/Skyrim:Apothecary%27s_Satchel "Skyrim:Apothecary's Satchel"), and a loose sample of frost mirriam.

### Knifepoint Mine

The boulders blocking the path through the mine

The hideout of Boethiah's Champion

Entering the mine leads to a small room, with a tunnel down to the east blocked by a cave-in (unless the quest [Boethiah's Calling](/wiki/Skyrim:Boethiah%27s_Calling "Skyrim:Boethiah's Calling") is active). There will likely be a bandit chief near the campfire in the small room. There are two iron ore veins here, and a dead [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_(dead) "Skyrim:Imperial (dead)") prisoner in a cage next to the fire; the cage contains an additional three iron ore veins, and is secured with a leveled lock. There is an unlocked chest and a weapon rack with a pickaxe along the back wall. Throughout the mine are also many patches of mushrooms to be harvested, including [bleeding crown](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleeding_Crown "Skyrim:Bleeding Crown"), [blisterwort](/wiki/Skyrim:Blisterwort "Skyrim:Blisterwort"), [fly amanita](/wiki/Skyrim:Fly_Amanita "Skyrim:Fly Amanita"), [imp stool](/wiki/Skyrim:Imp_Stool "Skyrim:Imp Stool"), [Namira's rot](/wiki/Skyrim:Namira%27s_Rot "Skyrim:Namira's Rot"), and [white cap](/wiki/Skyrim:White_Cap "Skyrim:White Cap").

If the quest Boethiah's Calling is active, you can descend through the otherwise blocked tunnel to find a bandit by an alchemy lab behind a makeshift wall of crates and barrels to the left. Two shelving units and three barrels near the alchemy lab hold a range of potions, poisons, and ingredients. Two [corundum ore veins](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Corundum Ore Vein") can be found in this area: one at the bottom of the ramp where you entered, and a second to the right of the locked gate in the southeastern corner. You can then continue down the northern path, which contains a [flammable gas trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Flammable_Gas "Skyrim:Flammable Gas") and three more corundum ore veins, or you can open the locked gate, giving you a good vantage point overlooking the main room.

In the main room you will find the [Champion of Boethiah](/wiki/Skyrim:Champion_of_Boethiah "Skyrim:Champion of Boethiah"), if you have the related quest active, as well as a few bandits. There are over a dozen corundum ore veins here. To one side will be a smelter and a grindstone in front of a wooden ramp leading up to a makeshift house; on the other side you will see a wooden walkway leading to the previous locked gate. There is a master-locked chest under the wooden ramp accessible through a gap in the scaffolding to the left of the smelter; just before the chest is a barrel with cheese on top (see [bugs](#Bugs)). Lying on a crate north of the grindstone is a [satchel](/wiki/Skyrim:Containers#Satchel "Skyrim:Containers"). In the makeshift house is another unlocked chest, a single bed, a dresser, several food barrels, and a bow on a table. There is a tanning rack to the right just outside the entrance to the house, while farther to the right is a small tunnel which loops back around to the main chamber and contains several [glowing mushrooms](/wiki/Skyrim:Glowing_Mushroom "Skyrim:Glowing Mushroom").

## Notes

- If you climb the ridge west-southwest of the camp, you'll find some skeletal remains. The skeleton has a leveled bow and a [knapsack](/wiki/Skyrim:Knapsack "Skyrim:Knapsack") (containing common loot), which are splattered with blood, and is on the high rocky promontory directly west overlooking the mine entrance.

## Bugs

- Clearing out this location before Boethiah's Calling has begun may prevent the latter from starting at all.
  - The [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch"), version 1.4, fixes this bug.
- This location may not be marked as cleared on your map if you enter for the first time during the quest Boethiah's Calling.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.5, fixes this bug.
- Upon clearing this mine and returning at a later point, you may find that the tunnel leading down to the left from the first room is still blocked by the cave-in, leaving no way to progress through the mine.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.1, fixes this bug.
  - Exiting and reentering the mine may fix this, possibly requiring multiple attempts.
- If you have already received the quest Boethiah's Calling and have the objective to kill her current champion, you will be unable to complete the quest [Kill the Bandit Leader](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_the_Bandit_Leader_(Jarl) "Skyrim:Kill the Bandit Leader (Jarl)") in Knifepoint Ridge. The quest marker will point to where the bandit chief stands instead of over his head, and even if you kill everyone in the mine, the quest will not be completed. Waiting until Knifepoint Ridge has reset does not fix the problem.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.1, fixes this bug.
  - Typing `setstage Favor154 20` in the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") will finish the quest, allowing you to turn it in to the Jarl; however, you won't get the gold reward.
- In the area under the wooden ramp leading to the barrel with goat cheese and on to the chest, there is one spot where it is possible to get "stuck". If you are unfortunate enough to find it, the only option is to reload a saved game. The trouble spot is on the zigzag before the barrel; if you stick to the outside of the tunnel, you should avoid it. **?**
