He has marked me so that the guardian skeever, wolf and mudcrab should appear to me when I visit their lairs. *Objective 30:* Defeat the Guardian Mudcrab  *Objective 31:* Defeat the Guardian Skeever  *Objective 32:* Defeat the Guardian Wolf |
| 50 |  | I met a hunter named Froki who sent me on Kyne's Sacred Trials. I have defeated the first three guardian beasts as instructed. *Objective 50:* Return to Froki |
| 51 |  | The Nord hunter Froki is guiding me through the Sacred Trials of Kyne. I defeated the first group of guardians and have been tasked to seek out the guardian bear, sabrecat and mammoth spirits. *Objective 60:* Defeat the Guardian Bear  *Objective 61:* Defeat the Guardian Mammoth  *Objective 62:* Defeat the Guardian Sabre Cat |
| 70 |  | The Nord hunter Froki is guiding me through Kyne's Sacred Trials. I have defeated several guardian spirits as instructed. *Objective 70:* Return to Froki |
| 71 |  | The Nord hunter Froki is guiding me through the Sacred Trials of Kyne. I have defeated several spirit guardians and have now been asked to seek out the Troll guardian as my final challenge. *Objective 80:* Defeat the Guardian Troll |
| 80 |  | The Nord hunter Froki guided me through the Sacred Trials of Kyne. I have defeated the final guardian, a troll spirit. *Objective 100:* Return to Froki |
| 100 | ☑ | The Nord hunter Froki is guiding me through the Sacred Trials of Kyne. I had to defeat the guardian spirits of many beasts, and was rewarded with the Blessing of Kyne. |
| 200 | ☒ |  |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 10, 15, 30, 31, 32, 60, 61, 62.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage dunHunterQST stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest dunHunterQST`.

Kynesgrove

**Kynesgrove** is a small [settlement](/wiki/Skyrim:Settlements "Skyrim:Settlements") south of [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm").

Steamscorch Mine Camp

[Ganna](/wiki/Skyrim:Ganna_Uriel "Skyrim:Ganna Uriel") and [Gemma Uriel](/wiki/Skyrim:Gemma_Uriel "Skyrim:Gemma Uriel") came to Kynesgrove to start a lumber mill without realizing the nearby grove's trees were sacred to [Kyne](/wiki/Lore:Kyne "Lore:Kyne"). The settlement contains remnants of the grove they initially cut. They now mine [malachite](/wiki/Skyrim:Malachite "Skyrim:Malachite") for a living, unable to afford starting a lumber mill elsewhere. They can be heard constantly arguing about the life they left behind in [Cyrodiil](/wiki/Lore:Cyrodiil "Lore:Cyrodiil"). [Kjeld](/wiki/Skyrim:Kjeld "Skyrim:Kjeld") runs the settlement and will [buy malachite ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Mine_Ore "Skyrim:Mine Ore") from you. [Iddra](/wiki/Skyrim:Iddra "Skyrim:Iddra") runs the [Braidwood Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Braidwood_Inn "Skyrim:Braidwood Inn"). [Dravynea the Stoneweaver](/wiki/Skyrim:Dravynea_the_Stoneweaver "Skyrim:Dravynea the Stoneweaver") keeps the mine from collapsing and getting too warm with a potion she makes from [frost salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Salts "Skyrim:Frost Salts").

The settlement consists of [Braidwood Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Braidwood_Inn "Skyrim:Braidwood Inn"), [Steamscorch Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Steamscorch_Mine "Skyrim:Steamscorch Mine") (a malachite mine), and a [camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Steamscorch_Mine#Steamscorch_Mine_Camp "Skyrim:Steamscorch Mine") containing three tents used by the miners. There is a [smelter](/wiki/Skyrim:Smelter "Skyrim:Smelter") outside the mine, a [grindstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Grindstone "Skyrim:Grindstone") beside the inn, and a [stone quarry](/wiki/Skyrim:Stone_Quarry "Skyrim:Stone Quarry") just east of the inn. Next to the camp is a vegetable patch containing six [leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Leek "Skyrim:Leek"), four [gourds](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourd "Skyrim:Gourd"), eight [potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato") plants, and ten [cabbages](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage"). A [wood chopping block](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Chopping_Block "Skyrim:Wood Chopping Block") and a [tanning rack](/wiki/Skyrim:Tanning_Rack "Skyrim:Tanning Rack") are also found near the vegetable patch. A short distance downhill from the inn is a chicken coop consisting of two [chicken nests](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken%27s_Egg "Skyrim:Chicken's Egg") for the two [chickens](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken "Skyrim:Chicken") that wander the settlement. There are a number of [dragon's tongue](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon%27s_Tongue "Skyrim:Dragon's Tongue") plants around the settlement as well as a [nightshade](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightshade "Skyrim:Nightshade") plant and a [snowberry](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries") bush around the camp. Uphill to the south are some [beehives](/wiki/Skyrim:Beehive "Skyrim:Beehive") and [red mountain flowers](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Red Mountain Flower") among the trees. To the east is a [dragon mound](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Mounds#Kynesgrove_Resurrection "Skyrim:Dragon Mounds") where the [dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon") [Sahloknir](/wiki/Skyrim:Sahloknir "Skyrim:Sahloknir") is resurrected by [Alduin](/wiki/Skyrim:Alduin "Skyrim:Alduin") during the quest [A Blade in the Dark](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Blade_in_the_Dark "Skyrim:A Blade in the Dark").

- **[Dravynea's Frost Salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Dravynea%27s_Frost_Salts "Skyrim:Dravynea's Frost Salts")**: Find some [frost salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Salts "Skyrim:Frost Salts") for [Dravynea the Stoneweaver](/wiki/Skyrim:Dravynea_the_Stoneweaver "Skyrim:Dravynea the Stoneweaver").

- **[A Blade in the Dark](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Blade_in_the_Dark "Skyrim:A Blade in the Dark")**: Prove you are Dragonborn to [Delphine](/wiki/Skyrim:Delphine "Skyrim:Delphine") by slaying the dragon [Sahloknir](/wiki/Skyrim:Sahloknir "Skyrim:Sahloknir").

#### Creation Club

- **[Battle of the Champions](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_of_the_Champions "Skyrim:Battle of the Champions")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War_Champions "Skyrim:Civil War Champions"): A battle between two [Civil War](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War "Skyrim:Civil War") champions is about to begin.

## Notes

- Despite Ganna Uriel mentioning that she and her sister built a lumbermill at Kynesgrove, it is nowhere to be found. The [Creation Kit](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Creation_Kit "Skyrim Mod:Creation Kit") identifies the bank of the river just down the hill from Kynesgrove as "Frostbark Lumber Mill", which suggests the location she describes was cut from the game.
- Kynesgrove is one of the most common places to encounter dragons, as they often fly overhead.
- Kynesgrove also [appears](/wiki/Online:Kynesgrove "Online:Kynesgrove") in [ESO](/wiki/Online:Online "Online:Online").

## Bugs

- If [Klija Wolf-Claw](/wiki/Skyrim:Klija_Wolf-Claw "Skyrim:Klija Wolf-Claw") appears at Kynesgrove but you then side with the [Legion](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") and kill her during the quest [Battle of the Champions](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_of_the_Champions "Skyrim:Battle of the Champions") [CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War_Champions "Skyrim:Civil War Champions"), this version of her will not be disabled, and she will continue to live at Steamscorch Mine Camp. **?**
- One of the pieces of malachite ore outside the mine may be buried under the ground, making it irretrievable.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.2, fixes this bug.
- There is a broken navmesh in the mine, making the back 1/3 of the mine largely inaccessible to the NPCs when they work there.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.3, fixes this bug.
- After [A Blade in the Dark](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Blade_in_the_Dark "Skyrim:A Blade in the Dark") is finished, the town guards may comment on a dragon attack here as though it took place somewhere else.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.3.8, fixes this bug.

Labyrinthian

**Labyrinthian** is a large [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins") southeast of [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal") containing [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr"), [skeletons](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton"), [trolls](/wiki/Skyrim:Troll "Skyrim:Troll"), [wisps](/wiki/Skyrim:Wisp "Skyrim:Wisp"), and the [dragon priest](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Priest "Skyrim:Dragon Priest") [Morokei](/wiki/Skyrim:Morokei_(creature) "Skyrim:Morokei (creature)"). It contains four zones: *[Labyrinthian](#Labyrinthian)*, *[Labyrinthian Chasm](#Labyrinthian_Chasm)*, *[Labyrinthian Thoroughfare](#Labyrinthian_Thoroughfare)*, and *[Labyrinthian Tribune](#Labyrinthian_Tribune)*.

Its [word wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Word_Wall "Skyrim:Word Wall") teaches part of the [Slow Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Slow_Time "Skyrim:Slow Time") [dragon shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts"). The entrance to the ruin may only be opened with the [Torc of Labyrinthian](/wiki/Skyrim:Torc_of_Labyrinthian "Skyrim:Torc of Labyrinthian"). Therefore, the interior of the dungeon is inaccessible until the quest [The Staff of Magnus](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Staff_of_Magnus "Skyrim:The Staff of Magnus") has been started.

## Related Quests

- **[The Staff of Magnus](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Staff_of_Magnus "Skyrim:The Staff of Magnus")**: Retrieve the [Staff of Magnus](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Magnus "Skyrim:Staff of Magnus").

### Exterior

Situated in a mountain pass between [Hjaalmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjaalmarch "Skyrim:Hjaalmarch") and [Whiterun Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Hold "Skyrim:Whiterun Hold"), Labyrinthian is the ruins of an ancient Nord city. The outdoor ruins contain the entrance to *Labyrinthian*, as well as two other separate locations: [Shalidor's Maze](/wiki/Skyrim:Shalidor%27s_Maze "Skyrim:Shalidor's Maze") and [Lost Valkygg](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_Valkygg "Skyrim:Lost Valkygg"). The exterior is patrolled by four [frost trolls](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Troll "Skyrim:Frost Troll").

Approaching from Whiterun Hold, the pass is to the northeast of [Dustman's Cairn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dustman%27s_Cairn "Skyrim:Dustman's Cairn"), northwest of [Silent Moons Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Silent_Moons_Camp "Skyrim:Silent Moons Camp"). The approach is made under two huge arches, followed by the first wall with a smaller arch through it. This is where the first frost troll roams. From the top of the first flight of stairs, you will see various levels around the ruins, with stairs up and down. From the bottom of the first flight of stairs, you can either climb stairs on the left to a raised area with three [burial urns](/wiki/Skyrim:Burial_Urn "Skyrim:Burial Urn"), or continue along the main path. Ahead is a circular building, the entrance to which is on the northwestern side. In the center is the skeleton of a [Breton](/wiki/Skyrim:Breton "Skyrim:Breton"), beside which is a [note](/wiki/Skyrim:Hired_Thug%27s_Missive "Skyrim:Hired Thug's Missive") that explains what happened to the Breton and the [Wooden Mask](/wiki/Skyrim:Wooden_Mask "Skyrim:Wooden Mask") that gives access to [Bromjunaar Sanctuary](/wiki/Skyrim:Bromjunaar_Sanctuary "Skyrim:Bromjunaar Sanctuary"). There is an [Orcish dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Orcish_Dagger "Skyrim:Orcish Dagger") stuck in the Breton's ribs.

To the east of the circular building is the entrance to Shalidor's Maze, with an [urn](/wiki/Skyrim:Urn "Skyrim:Urn") and a novice-locked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") by the entrance. To the left of the entrance to Shalidor's Maze is the exit for Lost Valkygg. Entering this door will only give access to the final room. To the west of the circular building are two empty stone huts, with a flight of stairs up to an empty raised area. Beyond this to the northwest is a ruined tower with another frost troll inside. There are two large urns and a damaged flight of wooden stairs that lead nowhere in the tower. From outside the tower, to the northwest is an arch through the northern outer wall. To the left are wide stairs that lead up to the first of several terraces that ultimately lead to the main entrance to Labyrinthian. The first terrace is devoid of anything of interest. Continuing up the next flight, there is a large urn beside the stairs. The third terrace leads around to the right to a lookout point and a burial urn. The main flight of stairs leads up to the "Ceremonial Door", which is the main entrance to the interior of Labyrinthian and may only be opened with the Torc of Labyrinthian. Labyrinthian has a second exit named *Labyrinthian, Tribune* to the southeast, but a bolted door early on prevents using this as another entrance.

At the bottom of the stairs up to Labyrinthian is an empty cart, with a path to the east between two flights of stairs that leads to nothing of interest. Along the path is the third of the frost trolls beside a building that contains an urn. At the end of the path, there is an area to the left of the wide stairs. At the far eastern end of this area, underneath a bridge joining the outer wall to a raised section above you, there is an unlocked chest. The wide stairs lead up to the raised section, with a bridge to the north leading to the outer wall, and a second flight of stairs to the southeast leading to the entrance to Lost Valkygg. North of the empty cart are stairs down to a lower area. The western section of the lower area features several empty stone huts. To the east are stairs up to a level with the last of the frost trolls. At the top of the stairs is an arch with an unlocked chest underneath, next to a cave-in. Crossing the bridge from the eastern raised section to the outer wall and following it west, the second of the lookout points has a random [bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bow "Skyrim:Bow") lying on it. A short way farther along are stairs leading back down to the lower area with the empty stone huts. At the far western end of the outer wall is a burial urn.

The approach from Hjaalmarch is found by traveling from Morthal toward [Stonehills](/wiki/Skyrim:Stonehills "Skyrim:Stonehills") mine. Shortly before reaching some rubble on the left-hand side of the road, there is a turnoff to the right (south). Follow this to the bottom of a set of stairs and a path leading up, passing several switchback turns until you reach the ruin's northern entrance through the outer wall. There are several cages around the entrance arch.

### Labyrinthian

Upon activating the ceremonial door, the Torc of Labyrinthian is removed from your inventory and becomes a knocker on the door. You then appear inside the ruin in a large room, with several dead lootable skeletons lying about the room all facing toward the exit. There are two iron [weapons](/wiki/Skyrim:Weapons "Skyrim:Weapons") among the skeletons, as well as a [banded iron shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Banded_Iron_Shield "Skyrim:Banded Iron Shield"). Around the room are three large urns, and near the east wall is a stone table with stone benches surrounding it. On the table is a random resist cold [potion](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions") and a random spell tome of [Detect Life](/wiki/Skyrim:Detect_Life_(spell) "Skyrim:Detect Life (spell)"), [Ironflesh](/wiki/Skyrim:Ironflesh "Skyrim:Ironflesh"), [Telekinesis](/wiki/Skyrim:Telekinesis "Skyrim:Telekinesis"), or [Waterbreathing](/wiki/Skyrim:Waterbreathing_(spell) "Skyrim:Waterbreathing (spell)"). To the north, there are a few steps down to an unlocked iron door that leads further into the ruin. Beyond the door is a corridor, with a flight of stairs on your left up to an urn and a [blisterwort](/wiki/Skyrim:Blisterwort "Skyrim:Blisterwort") fungus. Farther along, there is a burial urn on the left, and two more blisterwort fungi, one on each side of the path. At the bottom is a closed gate with a lever to the left, as well as three [white cap](/wiki/Skyrim:White_Cap "Skyrim:White Cap") fungi, two urns, and a burial urn.

Beyond the gate you can see several hostile skeletons, some of which are magic users, standing around a huge room. The corresponding lever only raises the gate for a few seconds; however, there is another lever on the other side that also triggers the gate. As soon as you enter and engage the skeletons, a [skeletal dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeletal_Dragon "Skyrim:Skeletal Dragon") will rise from a mound in the middle of the room and join the fight. It breathes [frost](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Breath "Skyrim:Frost Breath"), so be prepared. Arrows cannot be shot through the closed gate, but some spells and shouts can. It is possible to raise the gate and shoot through the open entrance without entering. You can also stand on the other side of the gate and repeatedly conjure Atronachs, a Familiar or Dremora (alternatively, the [Dead Thrall](/wiki/Skyrim:Dead_Thrall "Skyrim:Dead Thrall") spell allows you to resurrect dead enemy magicians) until all of the skeletons have been dealt with. You can thus eliminate the skeletons and even the dragon before even entering the room. In addition, the dragon doesn't fit through the gate, so if you have entered, you can retreat back through it to take cover. There are four large urns and four burial urns around the room. To the east is an exit from the room, down a flight of stairs. At the bottom of the stairs is a plinth with an etched tablet on top, from which stairs descend to the south to a pair of doors that open into *Labyrinthian Chasm*. There is an urn buried in the rubble in an alcove just to the north of the plinth.

|  |
| --- |
| **Etched Tablet**  Hail All - Brave City Bromjunaar  Forever These Walls Shall Stand  May Enemies See Her Majesty  May All Quake to Behold Her |

### Labyrinthian Chasm

This zone starts with another room with twin stairways proceeding down; however, the left-hand stairway has suffered a cave-in, with an urn and two burial urns among the rubble. Against the west wall is a set of shelves which holds nothing but clutter, while hiding behind a pillar is an unlocked chest. As you descend the right-hand stairway, you will hear the voice of Morokei, which will drain your [magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Magicka "Skyrim:Magicka") every time you hear him, and a [frost spirit](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Spirit "Skyrim:Frost Spirit") will spawn from a door with frost and ice around it. On your immediate right, standing in an alcove, is a slumbering draugr. At the rear of the room is an alcove with a plinth holding a *[Spell Tome: Flames](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Tome:_Flames "Skyrim:Spell Tome: Flames")*. The only other items of note in this room are two white cap mushrooms. When you cast Flames (or any other fire-based [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction") spell) at the icy door, it will open, revealing the path forward.

As you pass through the door, you will hear Morokei's voice again, and will see a natural walkway on which a draugr stands below you over a large chasm. Be careful, as there are several draugr in this area, and any fighting can alert several to converge on you. Several of them are leveled, and may include [deathlords](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr_Deathlord "Skyrim:Draugr Deathlord") who can knock you off the walkways using [shouts](/wiki/Skyrim:Unrelenting_Force "Skyrim:Unrelenting Force"), resulting in a long drop that could potentially kill you. As you descend the first walkway, there is a second draugr at the end of the walkway standing by a doorway leading to the south. The walkway also continues down from here.

Lightning Rune

Through the doorway, you will find stairs going down, with another leveled draugr roaming at the bottom next to a lit brazier. The path enters a corridor to the left; at the corner is a damaged sarcophagus with an [ancient Nord helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancient_Nord_Helmet "Skyrim:Ancient Nord Helmet") and [sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancient_Nord_Sword "Skyrim:Ancient Nord Sword") inside. The corridor leads to an unlocked iron door with a [lightning rune](/wiki/Skyrim:Lightning_Rune "Skyrim:Lightning Rune") on it. Behind the door is a room containing a draugr, who will normally hear you destroying the rune and come to investigate. The room contains a table with an [arcane enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanter "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanter") built into it and a chair drawn up in front, with the skeleton of a [novice conjurer](/wiki/Skyrim:Novice_Conjurer "Skyrim:Novice Conjurer") that was obviously killed where he sat in the chair. There is blood over the enchanter and floor. To the left of the table is an unlocked chest. On the table is a random filled [soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems"), a copy of *[Immortal Blood](/wiki/Skyrim:Immortal_Blood "Skyrim:Immortal Blood")*, a *[Spell Tome: Equilibrium](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Tome:_Equilibrium "Skyrim:Spell Tome: Equilibrium")*, and two bowls of [bone meal](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Meal "Skyrim:Bone Meal"). In an alcove to the right of the table is an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Lab "Skyrim:Alchemy Lab"), with two bowls [fire salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Salts "Skyrim:Fire Salts"), a bowl of [ectoplasm](/wiki/Skyrim:Ectoplasm "Skyrim:Ectoplasm"), a bowl of bone meal, a [deathbell](/wiki/Skyrim:Deathbell "Skyrim:Deathbell"), and a [giant lichen](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant_Lichen "Skyrim:Giant Lichen") sample in boxes on the floor to either side of it. You will need to backtrack to the chasm to continue onward.

Following the path down the next walkway, as you approach the walkway with the arch over it, you hear Morokei's voice again. At this point, you alert another leveled draugr to your presence, even when sneaking. There are quite a few [nightshade](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightshade "Skyrim:Nightshade") plants along these walkways. Ahead over the arched walkway is a well-lit doorway; proceed through the doorway and follow the path up and around the corner to the right. Ahead is an urn and two [fly amanita](/wiki/Skyrim:Fly_Amanita "Skyrim:Fly Amanita") mushrooms. The path turns to the left and enters a room patrolled by another leveled draugr. On the far side of the bridge, on the left, is a stone bowl containing a [deer hide](/wiki/Skyrim:Deer_Hide "Skyrim:Deer Hide") and a piece of [gold ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold_Ore "Skyrim:Gold Ore"). On the left by the bridge is a leveled [potion of enhanced stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Enhanced_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Enhanced Stamina") and a leveled [potion of the berserker](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_the_Berserker "Skyrim:Potion of the Berserker"). Just out of sight is a second draugr, which is standing in an alcove with a table holding a burial urn and a [gold sapphire ring](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold_Sapphire_Ring "Skyrim:Gold Sapphire Ring"). At the end of the room is another cave-in, with two partially buried burial urns and a gold ore among the rubble. Stairs lead down nearby, running back toward the bridge you crossed. At the bottom is another brightly lit area, with an open door to the northeast, and three sets of shelves and an urn along the back wall. One of the shelves has been knocked over, and contains nothing of interest. The other two contain a [salt pile](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_Pile "Skyrim:Salt Pile"), a sample of [scaly pholiota](/wiki/Skyrim:Scaly_Pholiota "Skyrim:Scaly Pholiota") fungus, two deathbell flowers, a bowl of bone meal, and a filled random soul gem.

Through the door, you enter a cave-like area with a path leading down to a stream flowing north to south. To the right is a ledge leading up to a [dead Argonian](/wiki/Skyrim:Argonian_(NPC) "Skyrim:Argonian (NPC)") with an [ancient Nord greatsword](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancient_Nord_Greatsword "Skyrim:Ancient Nord Greatsword") sticking out of the corpse, and an unlocked chest and a small [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse") beside the body. Take the path down to the stream. To the north, you see an iron door at the end. To the south, you see stairs leading up; take this route to search the bottom of the chasm you've been steadily descending. There are two hanging mosses and a [Nirnroot](/wiki/Skyrim:Nirnroot "Skyrim:Nirnroot") on your right. At the end, opposite the stairs, is a ramp leading back up to where you previously descended.

Returning below and heading north along the stream, you will again hear Morokei's voice. At the end, the iron door leads to *Labyrinthian Thoroughfare*.

### Labyrinthian Thoroughfare

Upon entering the zone, you are still following the stream. After a short distance, there is a closed gate ahead. Passing through the gate, you can hear a skeleton ahead around the corner. There is also a draugr that you will have to fight along with the skeleton. There is a path in the northwest corner, and a novice-locked gate in the southwest. Through the gate, on your right is a stone bowl containing a third piece of gold ore. To the left, the path heads downstream to bars blocking the way. On your right is a path that leads to two unlocked chests and two burial urns. Again there is a path on your right, which ends at a broken walkway with a path below you on the right and a doorway below you ahead. Jumping down here will take you to the same place as if you were to turn around and go the other way.

If you return to the first small chamber, the path in the northwest corner leads to a skeleton magic user. If you jump you can ambush him as he is facing the direction you would be coming if you had backtracked. There are two [Namira's rot](/wiki/Skyrim:Namira%27s_Rot "Skyrim:Namira's Rot") mushrooms and a burial urn in the corner, with the path continuing to the north. Immediately on your right, behind some vegetation in shallow water, are four pieces of [malachite ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Malachite_Ore "Skyrim:Malachite Ore"). You may need to push them up out of the water in order to pick them up. The path turns to the west, then south, and meets up with the broken walkway found on the other route. The only way onward is through the doorway to the west. You can hear a troll nearby.

The doorway leads into a room with scattered bones and three barred windows on your right. You are at the top of two short sets of stairs. Behind the stairs in an alcove to the south is a skeleton that can be looted and an unlocked chest. In the western corner of the room is a [bleeding crown](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleeding_Crown "Skyrim:Bleeding Crown") mushroom. There are a couple more skeletons to be looted in the room. Looking through the windows to the north, you will see a large cavern, with walls partitioning the cavern, bars blocking an arch, and a walkway with several roaming skeletons. To the east in the initial room is a large urn near a corridor guarded by a troll. The corridor heads north, and after two turns enters the huge cavern seen through the windows.

You enter the large cavern at the top of a flight of stairs leading down to a bridge to the west over the cavern floor. Looking from the top step, down to the west you will see two skeletons standing guard and two [gold ore veins](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Gold Ore Vein") on the ground (see [bugs](#Bugs)). From the bottom of the first flight of stairs, you can see two more skeletons standing on top of the wall with the barred arch ahead. Following the path west across the bridge leads to an area with a rock pillar in the middle. Behind the pillar is a troll, and to the right of the troll is a tunnel continuing to the west. Through the tunnel, you enter another cave with another troll, quite a bit of vegetation, and scattered bones and blood. There are three blisterwort fungi and four nightshade plants in this cave, along with an urn, a burial urn, and an unlocked chest at the back.

Return to the main chamber and approach the barred arch, where you will yet again hear Morokei's voice. The lever to open the bars is to the right of the arch. As you pass under the arch, on your right is a large urn and a burial urn, with a second burial urn near a flag and a lit brazier. In front of you are two large sculptures blocking your view of the rest of the cavern. You will need to move around these to the left. Behind the sculptures is a graveyard patrolled by three wisps. At the center of the graveyard, an etched tablet is found below the brazier. Turn around and head up some stairs to the south that lead to the top of the wall, where you will find an unlocked chest with a highly leveled magicka [poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Poison "Skyrim:Poison") next to it. Pass through the graveyard to the northwestern corner, where you will find stairs up to a raised section across the rear of the cavern guarded by a [wispmother](/wiki/Skyrim:Wispmother "Skyrim:Wispmother"). After defeating her, activate the wisps' remnant [glow cores](/wiki/Skyrim:Glow_Dust "Skyrim:Glow Dust") to collect glow dust from their remains. There is a row of coffins on shelves along the back, some of which may contain a few septims or bone meal. To the left of the coffins is an unlocked chest. The path to the east crosses a wooden bridge, which has a [hanging moss](/wiki/Skyrim:Hanging_Moss "Skyrim:Hanging Moss") growing from it, toward a door with flames covering it. This door reacts similarly to the frost door found earlier, producing a [fire spirit](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Spirit "Skyrim:Fire Spirit") and Morokei's voice. There are two [scrolls of Ice Spike](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Ice_Spike "Skyrim:Scroll of Ice Spike") and a *[Spell Tome: Frostbite](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Tome:_Frostbite "Skyrim:Spell Tome: Frostbite")* (the spell that may be used to open the door) to the left of the door.

Through the door is a corridor that ends in a cave-in, with two burial urns among the rubble. Before the cave-in is a path to the north that passes through a closed gate into a room with the start of a spiral staircase leading down; however, the staircase is blocked after a few feet, ending only with a white cap fungus. There is a tunnel heading east, with a skeleton standing guard partway along. Using a ranged weapon to deal with the skeleton will alert a [spectral warhound](/wiki/Skyrim:Spectral_Warhound "Skyrim:Spectral Warhound") and a spectral [draugr wight](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr_Wight "Skyrim:Draugr Wight"). There are two white cap fungi along this tunnel. As you approach the end, you will hear Morokei's voice yet again. At the end is a [trap door](/wiki/Skyrim:Trap_Door "Skyrim:Trap Door"), with water cascading down into it from above. Looking down, you can see more spectral enemies below. There is a tunnel to the southeast that turns and continues down, before opening into a wider corridor. There are three blisterwort fungi and three nightshade plants growing along the tunnel.

At the bottom of the stairs is a doorway that leads into a room. As you approach, a sarcophagus will burst open, revealing a leveled spectral draugr on the left. You emerge on a raised area, with wooden stairs down to the lower part of the room. There is a spectral draugr and a skeleton standing guard at the bottom, who will be alerted while you fight the first spectral draugr. On the raised section opposite where you entered is a set of shelves containing a [gold ingot](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold_Ingot "Skyrim:Gold Ingot") and a random soul gem; behind the shelves, on a platform you can jump to, are two burial urns and two pieces of gold ore. On the lower level are three nightshade plants and one blisterwort fungus. To the west is a closed wooden door.

Through the door is a corridor that leads to below the trap door you previously passed, featuring two leveled spectral draugr and possibly a dead troll. There are a two urns and two burial urns around the room, and against the eastern wall is a set of shelves holding another burial urn. In the northwestern corner is a doorway into a corridor that has a bleeding crown mushroom growing in a stone bowl to the south, and an iron door to the north. This door leads to *Labyrinthian Tribune*.

|  |
| --- |
| **Etched Tablet**  Here Lie the Hallowed Dead of Bromjunaar  May Ever Their Souls Be Their Own |

### Labyrinthian Tribune

Upon entering the zone, you are in a badly damaged catacomb area, with quite a lot of vegetation including two blisterwort mushrooms. As you descend to the west, you will pass two [dead draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Containers#Draugr "Skyrim:Containers") that can be looted. At the bottom, at the start of a corridor leading south, is a leveled spectral draugr, with another leveled draugr and a spectral warhound around the corner out of sight. At the bottom of the corridor is a plinth with a *[Spell Tome: Steadfast Ward](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Tome:_Steadfast_Ward "Skyrim:Spell Tome: Steadfast Ward")*, with an unlocked chest and two food barrels beside it. An open door to the west leads down a flight of stairs into another room. Take care, as this room has a total of five [spellcaster traps](/wiki/Skyrim:Spellcaster_Trap "Skyrim:Spellcaster Trap"). The first is on your right as you enter, the second is farther along on your left, and three more are at the far end of the room. The first and second traps fire frostbite, the central end trap fires [firebolts](/wiki/Skyrim:Firebolt "Skyrim:Firebolt"), and the other two end traps fire flames. There is also a [frost rune](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Rune "Skyrim:Frost Rune") on the floor partway along. On your left as you enter the room is an unlit brazier holding a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine") and a basket that contains two [iron ingots](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ingot "Skyrim:Iron Ingot"), a random [potion of resist magic](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Resist_Magic "Skyrim:Potion of Resist Magic"), a random [potion of lasting potency](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Lasting_Potency "Skyrim:Potion of Lasting Potency"), and a random [potion of extra magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Extra_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Extra Magicka").

Through the doorway at the end where the three spellcaster traps are, you will enter what appears to be a typical tower, with stairs up on the left leading to another door exiting to a wooden ramp up to a higher level of the tower. Through the door, you can see another leveled spectral draugr; fighting this spectral draugr will alert another that is on the ramp, and possibly a third that is in the room above. Climb the ramp, harvesting hanging mosses on the way, and a nightshade plant at the top of the ramp. The room above contains a leveled spectral draugr, unless you've already dealt with it. There is an urn and several barrels in this room, some of which contain [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients"). There is a flight of wooden stairs leading up again, with an unlocked chest and a burial urn underneath. Climbing the wooden stairs to the top level, you will find an unlocked chest and a stone bowl that contains a piece of malachite ore. Return to the bottom of the wooden ramp and follow the earthen ramp down to a flooded section. Under the water, you will find either in a stone bowl or on the bottom two pieces of malachite ore and a piece of gold ore, as well as a skeleton reaching for a [gold diamond ring](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold_Diamond_Ring "Skyrim:Gold Diamond Ring"). There is a corridor to the west.

The corridor descends a flight of stairs; as you descend, you will hear Morokei again. In front of you are two sets of shackles, one of which holds the remains of a skeleton with a random [dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Dagger "Skyrim:Dagger") among the bones. To the south is an adept-locked gate, while the passage to the north turns to the west and descends to a pair of iron doors. Through the locked gate is a small catacomb, with four alcoves behind a lit brazier. There is a leveled [shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Shield "Skyrim:Shield") in one of the alcoves, and a random potion and a random poison in another. There is also a random potion on the ground, near an enchanted ancient Nord weapon and the [Ancient Helmet of the Unburned](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancient_Helmet_of_the_Unburned "Skyrim:Ancient Helmet of the Unburned").

Through the iron doors, you are at the top of stairs leading down to a throne with its back to you. On your left is a burial urn and an urn. The word wall that teaches you a word from the Slow Time shout is in front of the throne, and a leveled spectral draugr is sitting in it. There is also a spectral warhound roaming the area, and several nightshades and blisterwort fungi growing around the room. At the bottom of the stairs, on the right is a rock pillar with a tree beside it; behind the pillar is an unlocked chest. The path continues to the west past the right-hand side of the word wall into a corridor flanked by a row of pillars on each side; before you enter the corridor, there is a skeleton in the rocks to your right with a [silver sapphire necklace](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Sapphire_Necklace "Skyrim:Silver Sapphire Necklace"). There is space to walk behind the pillars, which allows you to sneak up on at least one of two spectral draugr. There are also two skeletons in this area. There is a low ledge behind the pillars on each side, with a bowl of [glow dust](/wiki/Skyrim:Glow_Dust "Skyrim:Glow Dust"), a sample of nightshade, three [ebony ingots](/wiki/Skyrim:Ebony_Ingot "Skyrim:Ebony Ingot"), a salt pile, a [canis root](/wiki/Skyrim:Canis_Root "Skyrim:Canis Root"), and a bowl of bone meal on them. At the end of the room is a doorway into a circular room, with another doorway to the south and altars to the west and north. The altars hold a random poison, a random filled soul gem, and a burial urn.

The doorway to the south leads to a corridor ending at a pair of iron doors. These open into the room with Morokei. He is protected by an energy field being cast by two enthralled mages standing on walkways above. You will need to kill/damage the mages first in order to be able to harm Morokei. Once he is defeated, don't forget to loot his ash pile for both the [Staff of Magnus](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Magnus "Skyrim:Staff of Magnus") and the mask: [Morokei](/wiki/Skyrim:Morokei_(item) "Skyrim:Morokei (item)"). There are several hanging mosses and deathbells growing in this room. At the far end is a waterfall falling into a pool. In the pool is a [slaughterfish](/wiki/Skyrim:Slaughterfish "Skyrim:Slaughterfish"), an unlocked chest, and five loose [slaughterfish eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Slaughterfish_Egg "Skyrim:Slaughterfish Egg"), while two clusters of eggs are at the edge of the pool. Climb then descend the sets of stairs to the east to enter the area behind the wall, which features a deathbell plant, a hanging moss, a burial urn, and two unlocked chests (one slightly hidden around the side of the stairs to the west). The exit is at the rear of the room through another pair of iron doors. The doors lead to a stairway, with a barred wooden door at the top. Through this door is a tunnel, with a white cap mushroom and a large urn on the left, and stairs up on the right to a lowered gate, with the lever on the right-hand side.

As soon as you lift the gate, the door opposite opens and a [Thalmor](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor "Skyrim:Thalmor") agent named [Estormo](/wiki/Skyrim:Estormo "Skyrim:Estormo") enters; he stands in place, waiting for you to approach. This gives you plenty of time to prepare for battle, or just to start firing ranged weapons or spells at him. If you approach, he will ask you to hand over the staff, and will admit that [Ancano](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancano "Skyrim:Ancano") wants you dead. Once you have dealt with him, there is an unlocked chest behind the table on the left along with three barrels, one of which contains ingredients. On the other table is a [silver sapphire necklace](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Sapphire_Necklace "Skyrim:Silver Sapphire Necklace") on a plate.

Through the door that Estormo came through is a small catacomb area, with a burial urn on your left. On your right are stairs up to a circular room with a lootable skeleton, a [knapsack](/wiki/Skyrim:Knapsack "Skyrim:Knapsack") by the wall on the right, and a ladder exit from Labyrinthian opposite. The exit emerges near the second of the two large arches on the approach from Whiterun Hold.

## Notes

- Although a [loading screen](/wiki/Skyrim:Loading_Screens "Skyrim:Loading Screens") quote states that [caravans](/wiki/Skyrim:Khajiit_Traders "Skyrim:Khajiit Traders") sometimes pass through Labyrinthian, in-game they never do, as their routes take them around the ruin, not through it.
- Labyrinthian also appears in *[Arena](/wiki/Arena:Labyrinthian "Arena:Labyrinthian")* (where it is noted for being a particularly large and confusing dungeon to navigate and a location for one of the pieces of the [Staff of Chaos](/wiki/Arena:Staff_of_Chaos "Arena:Staff of Chaos")) and [ESO](/wiki/Online:Labyrinthian "Online:Labyrinthian").
- Version 3.0.8 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch") changes the lighting of the bridge end caps to the "snowy" version.
- The beam being channeled at Morokei by the two spectral mages is an actual spell. The description of it is: "Morokei Channel +75 Channeling Beam 1sec". If you come into contact with it, it doesn't do anything.

## Bugs

- The trolls outside of the dungeon respawn despite it being classed as a "no-reset zone". **?**
- The loading screens for Labyrinthian were meant to stop once The Staff of Magnus is finished, but they never stop due to incorrect conditions governing this.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.1, fixes this bug.
- Labyrinthian cannot be independently cleared, as it contains no marked boss. It can only be marked as cleared by clearing Lost Valkygg, even though the two locations are separate areas with different map markers.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.1, addresses this issue. Morokei has been marked as the boss, allowing Labyrinthian to be independently cleared.
- You may not be able to interact with one of the gold ore veins.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.0, fixes this bug.
- The spirits here (dunLabyrinthianFireMagi and dunLabyrinthianFrostMagi) have incorrect ash piles set.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.3, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Laid to Rest

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This page is currently being rewritten as part of the [Skyrim Quest Redesign Project](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").** The page is being rewritten and checked in several stages. All users are welcome to make changes to the page. If you make a change that is relevant to the project, please update this template accordingly, and make sure you have observed the [project guidelines](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project#Guidelines "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").  Details  **Walkthrough**: written by [Beezer1029](/wiki/User:Beezer1029 "User:Beezer1029"), *not checked*  **Reward**: written by [Roger](/wiki/User:Roger "User:Roger"), *not checked* |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Investigate a tragic house fire, and discover an insidious plot against the town.** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Morthal guards](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal_Guard "Skyrim:Morthal Guard") OR [Idgrod Ravencrone](/wiki/Skyrim:Idgrod_Ravencrone "Skyrim:Idgrod Ravencrone") OR [Sorli the Builder](/wiki/Skyrim:Sorli_the_Builder "Skyrim:Sorli the Builder") or [Jonna](/wiki/Skyrim:Jonna "Skyrim:Jonna") |
| Location(s): | [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal"), [Movarth's Lair](/wiki/Skyrim:Movarth%27s_Lair "Skyrim:Movarth's Lair") |

| [Disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition"): | =2 (Jarl of [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal")), =1 ([Thonnir](/wiki/Skyrim:Thonnir "Skyrim:Thonnir")), =-2 ([Hroggar](/wiki/Skyrim:Hroggar "Skyrim:Hroggar") if Alva is killed), =-2 ([Lami](/wiki/Skyrim:Lami "Skyrim:Lami") if Alva is killed) |
| ID: | MS14 |
| Suggested Level: | 6 |

The ghost of [Helgi](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgi%27s_Ghost "Skyrim:Helgi's Ghost")

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Find the burned down house.
2. Learn about the house fire from a [local guard](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal_Guard "Skyrim:Morthal Guard"), the [jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl"), or [innkeeper](/wiki/Skyrim:Jonna "Skyrim:Jonna").
3. After learning about the fire, talk to the Jarl of [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal").
4. Visit the house and find a lead.
5. After dark, defeat [Laelette the Vampire](/wiki/Skyrim:Laelette_the_Vampire "Skyrim:Laelette the Vampire"), and tell [Thonnir](/wiki/Skyrim:Thonnir "Skyrim:Thonnir") about his wife.
6. Follow up on the lead and learn who set the fire.
7. Visit the culprit's home and obtain evidence of a plot against the town.
8. Report your findings to the jarl and be tasked with eliminating the threat.
9. Lead a group of townspeople in the defense of Morthal.

### This Fire Burns

Just about everyone around town will be gossiping about [Hroggar](/wiki/Skyrim:Hroggar "Skyrim:Hroggar")'s house that recently burned down, with his wife and daughter inside. Since Hroggar shacked up with [Alva](/wiki/Skyrim:Alva "Skyrim:Alva") the very next day, many townspeople suspect foul play. Once you've found the charred ruins of the house, next to [Highmoon Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Highmoon_Hall "Skyrim:Highmoon Hall"), you can take your inquiry straight to the jarl, who will ask for your help in this matter: to sift through the ashes others are afraid to touch. Alternatively, after discovering the house, but before seeing the jarl, a [guard](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal_Guard "Skyrim:Morthal Guard") will approach you, asking for help, and initiating the quest. Similarly, visiting [Jonna](/wiki/Skyrim:Jonna "Skyrim:Jonna") at [Moorside Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Moorside_Inn "Skyrim:Moorside Inn") before visiting the jarl will also set you on your way.

In any case, another search of the burned house will rouse the ghost of [Helgi](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgi%27s_Ghost "Skyrim:Helgi's Ghost"), Hroggar's daughter. She describes dying in the fire. Even though she is a ghost, she is still a little girl. Agree to play hide-and-seek after dark with her, and in return she will reveal who set the fire. She also tells you that the game will begin at nighttime, so the other player in the game can join you. When you ask about this other player, Helgi becomes fearful, saying the other is close and may hear her. Then, she challenges you *"If you can find me first, I can tell you"*, and promptly disappears.

### Hide and Seek with a Ghost

At this point, though it is not indicated with a quest marker, you have the option of going to the jarl to tell her you saw the ghost of Helgi. If you tell Jonna first about the spirit, she will direct you to the jarl to tell your tale. Speaking to the jarl will give you some insight into the game and direct you to the grave where Helgi was buried. You can also tell Hroggar that you saw Helgi's ghost and he will respond with chilling indifference. You will receive a quest marker indicating where to "find Helgi in the dark". Wait until nightfall to find Helgi "hiding" in her grave in a small plot behind the house. It's a short distance away, up and to the right, marked with cairns. Someone else will also be there, prepared to fight once they see you.

### I've Been Expecting You...

Laelette attacks

When you arrive, Thonnir's missing wife [Laelette](/wiki/Skyrim:Laelette_the_Vampire "Skyrim:Laelette the Vampire") is already there. Defeat Laelette and activate Helgi's spirit. She will be pleased that you won the game and found her before Laelette. She will then tell you the heart-wrenching story of how an unwilling Laelette was forced to burn the house. Laelette, in an effort to save the child, attempted to turn her into a vampire, but Helgi was too far gone from the fire and perished. She will then tell you that she is tired and wants to sleep. Meanwhile, Laelette's husband, [Thonnir](/wiki/Skyrim:Thonnir "Skyrim:Thonnir"), arrives at Helgi's grave, distraught at finding Laelette dead. Speak to Thonnir and he will tell you that he thought Laelette had left him to join the [resistance](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks"). Ask him if there was anything strange going on before she left and he tells you that his wife had begun spending a lot of time with Alva, and was supposed to have met her on the night she disappeared. Alva claimed that Laelette never showed up. Here you inform the grieving husband your deductions about what really went on that night the women were to have met. Thonnir is incensed at the idea that Alva may be a vampire; he refuses to believe you and reiterates that you have no proof of Alva's undead status. A new quest directive invites you to investigate Alva.

### The Detective

Break into [Alva's house](/wiki/Skyrim:Alva%27s_House "Skyrim:Alva's House") across town, where Hroggar is now living as well. Hroggar will be immediately hostile if he is in the house when you arrive. If you break in during the day, Hroggar will not be there, though Alva will be—sleeping in her coffin. If you break in at night, Alva will most likely be outside of the house, and the coffin will be empty but for her journal. Whichever time of day you break in, make your way into the basement to discover Alva's coffin and [her journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Alva%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Alva's Journal"). If Alva is in her coffin when you visit, you will need to deal with her, but her demise is not necessary to advance the quest. Read the journal to discover how all the events unfolded, including how she was turned by the master vampire [Movarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Movarth_Piquine "Skyrim:Movarth Piquine"), the plot to enslave the townspeople of Morthal for their blood, and the beginnings of your investigation. Take Alva's journal back to Highmoon Hall and the jarl will reward you with a small sum of leveled gold. She then asks one more favor: travel to Movarth's Lair and eliminate the threat. She has gathered a small group of townspeople, led by Thonnir, to travel with you.

### To Movarth's Lair

The agitated mob who, as it turns out, is not 100% prepared to fight a centuries-old master vampire

Thonnir, enraged by the events that took his wife's life, leads the charge whether you're ready or not. Once the party arrives at the lair, however, everyone but Thonnir flees in terror. Thonnir offers you a choice of whether he accompanies you or not. He's essential, so he won't die, but he can't hold his own well, and you don't require his assistance to advance the quest. Whatever you choose, enter the one-zone lair and dispatch the vampire thralls and Movarth. Movarth is a [vampire boss](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire#Vampire_Bosses "Skyrim:Vampire") that can regenerate health, and is generally pretty tough. If you didn't take care of Alva in her own house, she will be in the lair, and possibly aid you in killing the other vampires. You can then kill her yourself if you'd like, though this may result in a bounty if Thonnir sees you do it (this sometimes can occur even if he's outside).

### Return to the Jarl of Morthal

As you leave the lair, Helgi's ghost will appear and thank you for avenging her mother's death. Return to Morthal and the jarl will reward you with a leveled amount of gold and the jarl's increased disposition towards you.

### Reward

|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| First payout:   | Levels | Reward | | --- | --- | | 1–9 | 250 | | 10–19 | 400 | | 20–29 | 500 | | 30–39 | 600 | | 40+ | 750 | | Second payout:   | Levels | Reward | | --- | --- | | 1–9 | 400 | | 10–19 | 600 | | 20–29 | 800 | | 30–39 | 1,000 | | 40+ | 1,200 | |

If you have the *[Hearthfire](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire")* add-on installed, you'll also be able to purchase the deed to [Windstad Manor](/wiki/Skyrim:Windstad_Manor "Skyrim:Windstad Manor") following the completion of this quest.

## Notes

- If you cast [Clairvoyance](/wiki/Skyrim:Clairvoyance_(spell) "Skyrim:Clairvoyance (spell)") before finding Helgi's grave, it will prematurely lead you out of town to Movarth's Lair.
- Alva's journal will only appear after the objective to investigate her house is set. It won't be in her coffin unless you've talked to Thonnir about her.
- Although you need to tell Thonnir about Laelette, you will never be given the option to tell [their son](/wiki/Skyrim:Virkmund "Skyrim:Virkmund") what happened to her. Thonnir also never tells him, and Virkund's post-quest dialogue doesn't change at all.
- If you break into Alva's house during either night or day, right after taking her journal, you may see her rushing towards Movarth's Lair (usually she starts from the inn). Afterwards her dead body might be seen within the lair —she is killed by Movarth if the two meet.
- If Hroggar dies before the quest starts, the quest will still proceed as normal.
- Thonnir, as a follower, will refuse to stop following you before reaching Movarth's Lair. (His presence will also remove any bonus damage from sneak attacks if he can see you.) However, when you and the mob are near Movarth's Lair, you can speak to Thonnir and the mob (except Thonnir) goes home. Then Thonnir can also be asked to stop following you.
- You can inform both Alva and Hroggar of your findings at two points in the investigation, being the first encounter with Helgi and Laelette's death, resulting in two very different reactions. While Alva will be intrigued by the revelation that she's the town's suspect and evidence points toward her, Hroggar will be largely uncaring and ultimately express his unwavering support of Alva at the mention of his daughter's ghost. He buys into the story that Laelette said goodbye to only Alva before leaving town, regardless of the evidence contradicting that.
  - Although never confirmed, Thonnir's reluctance to believe Alva had anything to do with Laelette's vampirism possibly suggests that Alva had enthralled him to an extent as well.
- Inside of Thonnir's House, there's a miscellaneous item known as [Michaela's Flagon](/wiki/Skyrim:Michaela%27s_Flagon "Skyrim:Michaela's Flagon"), internally known as `MS14FlagonA`. Similarly, in Jorgen and Lami's House, there's a wine known as [Jessica's Wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Food#Jessica.27s_Wine "Skyrim:Food") to be found, internally known as `MS14WineAltoA`. Their internal names tie these items to this quest, but it is unknown what their relevance would have been. The names of their apparent owners aren't tied to any existing NPCs either, used or otherwise.
- If you recruit [Benor](/wiki/Skyrim:Benor "Skyrim:Benor") as a follower during the quest, he will still join the mob. He will rejoin you after the scene outside Movarth's Lair. If you enter Movarth's Lair before talking to the mob outside, he won't follow you in unless you exit and talk to them. If Benor hasn't been recruited by then, you can still do so once the mob retreats.

### Before killing Laelette

- Idgrod may tell you that need to "find evidence about the accusation against Alva" prior to you reaching that point in the quest, including immediately after receiving the quest. **?**
- Laelette can be found before dusk, where she would normally spawn, above the burnt house. She is invisible, but not hostile, and you can speak to her. She doesn't have anything interesting to say.
  - She can even be visible and invulnerable to any kind of damage, although she can turn hostile if targeted by magic or arrows, at least in the Special Edition **?**
- In very rare cases, when playing "hide and seek" with Helgi, you may not fight Laelette because she will be killed by unknown causes. This does not stop or hinder the quest though.
- When playing "hide and seek" with Helgi, Laelette may not be at the coffin. When activating Helgi's coffin, you will still hear her say *"Make Laelette go away"* though. Laelette can be found on the cliffside just above the coffin, completely unresponsive and temporarily invulnerable. She may also be wandering Morthal, and hostile.
- You can tell Alva that people thought Hroggar burned his house down for her even though there is no logical reason for you to know that yet.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2, fixes this bug.

### Before taking the journal to the Jarl

- Speaking to [Thonnir](/wiki/Skyrim:Thonnir "Skyrim:Thonnir") after killing Laelette, but before examining Helgi's coffin, prevents you from doing so afterwards and prevents the ghost of [Helgi](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgi%27s_Ghost "Skyrim:Helgi's Ghost") from appearing. Seemingly though, the quest can still be completed once all other stages are done, and you will still receive your reward from the jarl.
- Hroggar may not be hostile when you enter Alva's house at night. However, if you talk to him, he will still yell about how he won't let you hurt Alva.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.6, fixes this bug.
- Alva may erroneously teleport herself to Movarth's Lair if she is in her coffin when you read her journal, potentially causing her to disappear right in front of you, which obviously breaks immersion.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.8, fixes this bug.

### After taking the journal to the Jarl

- If you ignore the mob and go to the cave without talking to anyone they will still follow you there. If you enter the cave and clear it without help, the mob will be waiting outside after Movarth is killed. You won't be able to talk to Thonnir. The game may move the entire mob to [Fort Greymoor](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Greymoor "Skyrim:Fort Greymoor") upon quest completion.
- If Alva is not killed before raiding [Movarth's Lair](/wiki/Skyrim:Movarth%27s_Lair "Skyrim:Movarth's Lair"), she will be found there, fighting against other vampires, and will not be hostile toward you. Attacking her there will be considered a crime.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.6, addresses this issue. She is no longer hostile towards the other vampires and is hostile towards you instead.
- Alva may fail to move to Movarth's Lair fast enough and can end up disrupting the mob scene outside.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.1, addresses this issue. She will now be script moved at the appropriate time to avoid this.
  - When Alva is defeated, but still alive, the cave will be marked as cleared. You may need to try entering the cave alone or loading the autosave from inside the cave to have Alva and others reappear (the Vampire lord might even respawn due to this bug). **?**
- If Alva is not killed in Movarth's Lair at the end of Laid to Rest, she will be found back in Morthal a few days later. Attacking her is considered a crime at this point.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.9, addresses this issue. She will no longer return to Morthal once she goes to Movarth's Lair.
  - If Alva is left alive in the cave, Hroggar will not update to the next phase of the quest and, once becoming thane, the game will crash as Hroggar is scripted to appear in the Hall. **?**
- If you shoot Movarth undetected, he may run and eventually get stuck in a wall where you cannot hit him. Leaving and reentering the dungeon will reset him to his initial position in his chair. **?**
- There is a bug that prevents Movarth's Lair from becoming cleared.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.2, fixes this bug.
  -  If you want to update the "cleared" status, enter the following command in the console: `SetLocationCleared 0001BDFC 1`
- Once you kill Movarth and make your way out of the cave, Helgi begins speaking her dialogue line immediately, and attempting to speak with her and initiate the only available dialogue line about avenging her and her mother causes her to stop speaking and disappear. It can be assumed that she was supposed to have a forcegreet, and the available dialogue option was supposed to trigger her dialogue.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.6, addresses this issue. The line of dialogue they had her able to use should not have been enabled since you can't use it until she's begun her hello line anyway, and that hello line is what disables her.
- If you kill Alva, Hroggar's disposition towards you gets a hit (-2), even though he will thank you for saving him from Alva. He will also continue to use some lines of dialogue from when he was her thrall. Killing Alva will cause Lami's disposition towards you to fall to -2 as well.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.3, addresses this issue. ([details](https://afktrack.afkmods.com/index.php?a=issues&i=19404)) Their disposition towards Alva will be reset to 0, but only after the player picks up the journal in the basement.
- After quest completion, Alva is supposed to be removed from the Morthal crime faction, but isn't.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.8, addresses this issue. The script call was doing it wrong.
- After quest completion, Hroggar isn't added back to the Morthal crime faction, which may lead to him being treated as aggressive, and can lead to fights with guards.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.5, fixes this bug. ([details](https://afktrack.afkmods.com/index.php?a=issues&i=20141))
- After quest completion, Hroggar may become hostile if Alva's status as a vampire is known and you encounter him afterwards.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.7, fixes this bug.
- The fix from Unofficial Skyrim Patch 1.3.2 created a new bug, as the "boss" vampires it introduced did not respawn and may therefore break radiant quests.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.3.4, fixes this bug.

### Persistent

- Idgrod may not engage in dialogue with you.
  - Clear any delivery mission listed [here](/wiki/Skyrim:Delivery "Skyrim:Delivery") first, then return to the Jarl.
- After killing Alva while she is in her cellar, Hroggar might still be hostile upon entering the house at night. He will also talk like he's still a thrall if you talk to him outside.
- If you encounter Alva in the main area of the house as she is returning home or leaving, she may not be hostile, but will still shout that she is going to kill you.
- If you enter Alva's house while Hroggar is in it, and you calm him with a calm spell in order to get the journal and continue the quest, Hroggar will still be hostile if you enter Alva's house again, where he seems to remain. Even after completing the quest he will attack you on sight.
  - Calming him again and then waiting seems to fix this issue and he'll be friendly again, thanking you for freeing him from Alva.
- Helgi's voice lacks the ghost effect used by other spirits.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.1, fixes this bug.

## Quest Stages

| 30 |  | Morthal's Jarl has asked me to investigate the house fire that killed Hroggar's wife and child. Hroggar took Alva as a lover immediately after the fire, and many in the town think he did it. *Objective 30:* Investigate the burned house |

| 95 |  | Morthal's Jarl has asked me to investigate the house fire that killed Hroggar's wife and child. The vampire Alva enslaved Hroggar and had his family killed in a house fire. Alva's master in Movarth's Lair plans to enslave the entire town. *Objective 95:* Show Alva's Journal to the Jarl |

Alva's master in Movarth's Lair plans to enslave the entire town. The Jarl now wants me to destroy Movarth and put an end to his plot. *Objective 100:* Kill the master vampire |
| 120 |  | *Objective 120:* Return to Morthal's Jarl |
| 200 | ☑ | Morthal's Jarl asked me to investigate the house fire that killed Hroggar's wife and child. The vampire Alva enslaved Hroggar and had his family killed in a house fire. Alva's master in Movarth's Lair planned to enslave the entire town. |
| *Unknown* |  | *Objective 50:* Ask around about Laelette |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 1, 5, 6, 7, 9, 10, 25, 80, 90, 97, 110, 130.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage MS14 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest MS14`.

# Skyrim:Lake Fjalding

## Overview

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Body of Water: Lake Fjalding ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&x=66298&y=62779)) ([lore page](/wiki/Lore:Lake_Fjalding "Lore:Lake Fjalding")) | | |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| Region | |
| [Solstheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Solstheim "Skyrim:Solstheim") | |
| Location | |
| By [Thirsk Mead Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Thirsk_Mead_Hall "Skyrim:Thirsk Mead Hall") | |

Lake Fjalding

**Lake Fjalding** is a frozen lake near [Thirsk Mead Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Thirsk_Mead_Hall "Skyrim:Thirsk Mead Hall").

It is the largest lake on [Solstheim](/wiki/Lore:Solstheim "Lore:Solstheim"), although it is covered by ice year-round. It is commonly used as a mating ground for the [horkers](/wiki/Skyrim:Horker "Skyrim:Horker") of the island. The [Iggnir River](/wiki/Skyrim:Iggnir_River "Skyrim:Iggnir River") to the south and the [Isild River](/wiki/Skyrim:Isild_River "Skyrim:Isild River") to the north meet here. The [Isinfier Plains](/wiki/Lore:Isinfier_Plains "Lore:Isinfier Plains") lie to the south.

# Skyrim:Lake Geir

## Overview

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Body of Water: Lake Geir ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Lake+Geir)) ([lore page](/wiki/Lore:Lake_Geir "Lore:Lake Geir")) | | |
| Region | |
| [The Rift](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Rift "Skyrim:The Rift") | |
| Location | |
| West of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") | |

Lake Geir

**Lake Geir** is a lake in the western [Rift](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Rift "Skyrim:The Rift").

[Ivarstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivarstead "Skyrim:Ivarstead") is located on the shores of Lake Geir. In the center of the lake there is an island which is home to [Geirmund's Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Geirmund%27s_Hall "Skyrim:Geirmund's Hall"). [Catfish](/wiki/Skyrim:Catfish "Skyrim:Catfish")[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing "Skyrim:Fishing") can be found swimming in the waters here.

Geographically, the lake is fed by the [Treva River](/wiki/Skyrim:Treva_River "Skyrim:Treva River") and is drained by [Darkwater River](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkwater_River "Skyrim:Darkwater River") (see [Bugs](#Bugs)).

## Related Quests

- **[Caught in the Rain](/wiki/Skyrim:Caught_in_the_Rain "Skyrim:Caught in the Rain")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing "Skyrim:Fishing"): Catch rainy weather fish.
- **[Forbidden Legend](/wiki/Skyrim:Forbidden_Legend "Skyrim:Forbidden Legend")**: Investigate the forgotten [Gauldur Legend](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_Legends "Skyrim:Lost Legends").
- **[The Straw that Broke](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Straw_that_Broke "Skyrim:The Straw that Broke")**: Discover what is plaguing [Narfi](/wiki/Skyrim:Narfi "Skyrim:Narfi")'s mind.

## Notes

- On the eastern shore is a row boat containing two sacks beached opposite a small island with a tree stump. On the island there are two [treasure hunters](/wiki/Skyrim:Treasure_Hunter_(bandit) "Skyrim:Treasure Hunter (bandit)") who will attack upon seeing you. They have dug up an unlocked chest containing minor loot. You will find two [white cap](/wiki/Skyrim:White_Cap "Skyrim:White Cap") and a [mora tapinella](/wiki/Skyrim:Mora_Tapinella "Skyrim:Mora Tapinella") that can be harvested on the island. Further inland is their camp including a small tent, two bedrolls, an open, empty chest, four sacks and three barrels, one of which has on it a bottle of [Honningbrew mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Honningbrew_Mead "Skyrim:Honningbrew Mead"), a small [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"), and a [note](/wiki/Skyrim:Note_(treasure) "Skyrim:Note (treasure)") directing you to the treasure on the island. There are also three rabbits hanging beside the tent that can be harvested. There is also a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe") next to where the rabbits are hanging.
- The name "Lake Geir" is sourced from the [Skyrim Prima Game Guide](/wiki/Books:The_Elder_Scrolls_V:_Skyrim:_Prima_Official_Game_Guide "Books:The Elder Scrolls V: Skyrim: Prima Official Game Guide").

## Bugs

- The water current markers are pointing in the wrong direction, such that the lake appears to be fed by an unseen underground spring at the bottom of The Throat of the World (directly behind Vilemyr Inn) and drains towards [Treva River](/wiki/Skyrim:Treva_River "Skyrim:Treva River") and [Lake Honrich](/wiki/Skyrim:Lake_Honrich "Skyrim:Lake Honrich") in addition to draining into Darkwater River. **?**

# Skyrim:Lake Honrich

## Overview

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Body of Water: Lake Honrich ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Lake+Honrich)) ([lore page](/wiki/Lore:Lake_Honrich "Lore:Lake Honrich")) | | |
| Region | |
| [The Rift](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Rift "Skyrim:The Rift") | |
| Location | |
| Southwest of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") | |

Lake Honrich

**Lake Honrich** is a lake in the eastern [Rift](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Rift "Skyrim:The Rift"), immediately southwest of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften"). It is drained by the [Treva River](/wiki/Skyrim:Treva_River "Skyrim:Treva River") and was named Lake Honnith in the [First Era](/wiki/Lore:First_Era "Lore:First Era"). [Goldenglow Estate](/wiki/Skyrim:Goldenglow_Estate "Skyrim:Goldenglow Estate") occupies a cluster of islands in the middle of the lake.

Lake Honrich is a popular spot for fishermen across Skyrim, and it even has a [fishery](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften_Fishery "Skyrim:Riften Fishery") found on its eastern shores in Riften.

## Related Quests

- **[Vald's Debt](/wiki/Skyrim:Vald%27s_Debt "Skyrim:Vald's Debt")**: Find the [Quill of Gemination](/wiki/Skyrim:Quill_of_Gemination "Skyrim:Quill of Gemination") to clear [Vald](/wiki/Skyrim:Vald "Skyrim:Vald")'s debt to [Maven Black-Briar](/wiki/Skyrim:Maven_Black-Briar "Skyrim:Maven Black-Briar").

## Bugs

- The water current markers are pointing in the wrong direction, such that the lake appears to be fed by the Treva River and drain into Riften Canalside. **?**

# Skyrim:Lake Ilinalta

## Overview

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Body of Water: Lake Ilinalta ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Lake+Ilinalta)) ([lore page](/wiki/Lore:Lake_Ilinalta "Lore:Lake Ilinalta")) | | |
| Region | |
| [Falkreath Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Hold "Skyrim:Falkreath Hold") | |
| Location | |
| North of [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath") | |

Lake Ilinalta, viewed from the [Guardian Stones](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Guardian_Stones "Skyrim:The Guardian Stones")

**Lake Ilinalta** is a lake in west-central [Falkreath Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Hold "Skyrim:Falkreath Hold"). It is the source of the [White River](/wiki/Skyrim:White_River "Skyrim:White River"), and contains [Ilinalta's Deep](/wiki/Skyrim:Ilinalta%27s_Deep "Skyrim:Ilinalta's Deep") and the [Lady Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Lady_Stone "Skyrim:The Lady Stone"). It is also the largest lake in Skyrim. The lake is believed by many people to be cursed due to the fact that an Imperial fort sank into the waters. One man's [journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Fisherman%27s_Journal_(Ilinalta%27s_Deep) "Skyrim:Fisherman's Journal (Ilinalta's Deep)") even notes that he couldn't find anybody willing to take him into the lake.

## Notes

- Lake Ilinalta is mentioned as a landmark in *[An Explorer's Guide to Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:An_Explorer%27s_Guide_to_Skyrim "Skyrim:An Explorer's Guide to Skyrim")*.
- The chest for [Treasure Map X](/wiki/Skyrim:Treasure_Map_X "Skyrim:Treasure Map X") can be found to the east of the [Lady Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Lady_Stone "Skyrim:The Lady Stone").
- An unmarked shipwreck is located along the southern coast of the lake, somewhat to the west of the lake's center. One portion of the wreck contains a treasure chest with gold. This is also an excellent place to harvest [Nordic barnacles](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Barnacle "Skyrim:Nordic Barnacle"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?x=-33793&y=-59590&zoom=17&legacy=true)
- A Nordic pit near the east end of the lake has been inundated by the lake's waters. It contains an unlocked chest, an urn amidst the rubble under the stairs, several Nordic barnacle clusters, a few clams, two leveled soul gems, and a leveled weapon on an old altar. It is guarded by two [slaughterfish](/wiki/Skyrim:Slaughterfish "Skyrim:Slaughterfish"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?x=-10363&y=-58229&zoom=17&legacy=true)
- There are two [hunter's camps](/wiki/Skyrim:Unmarked_Places "Skyrim:Unmarked Places") in the lake, one on a small island and one at the mouth of the [White River](/wiki/Skyrim:White_River "Skyrim:White River").

# Skyrim:Lake Yorgrim

## Overview

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Body of Water: Lake Yorgrim ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Lake+Yorgrim)) ([lore page](/wiki/Lore:Lake_Yorgrim "Lore:Lake Yorgrim")) | | |
| Region | |
| [The Pale](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pale "Skyrim:The Pale") | |
| Location | |
| West of [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") | |

Lake Yorgrim

**Lake Yorgrim** is a lake in the eastern part of [the Pale](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pale "Skyrim:The Pale"). It is the source of [River Yorgrim](/wiki/Skyrim:River_Yorgrim "Skyrim:River Yorgrim"). Located on the banks of the lake is [Bronze Water Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Bronze_Water_Cave "Skyrim:Bronze Water Cave"). The [Nightgate Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightgate_Inn "Skyrim:Nightgate Inn") can be found to the northwest. Due east of the lake is a [dragon burial site](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Mounds "Skyrim:Dragon Mounds") belonging to [Viinturuth](/wiki/Skyrim:Viinturuth "Skyrim:Viinturuth").

The [Dwemer ruins](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwemer_Ruins "Skyrim:Dwemer Ruins") of [Irkgthand](/wiki/Skyrim:Irkngthand "Skyrim:Irkngthand") run underneath the lake.
