# Skyrim:Lakeview Manor

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This article is being developed as part of the Skyrim Houses Redesign Project. If you see this tag it means the article can still be improved. Please see the [project page](/wiki/UESPWiki:SHRP "UESPWiki:SHRP") for guidelines.** |

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Town.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Town.png) | House: Lakeview Manor ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Lakeview+Manor+%28HF%29)) | | |
| Added by | [Hearthfire](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | Never (storage is [safe](/wiki/Skyrim:Containers#Safe_Locations "Skyrim:Containers")) |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| BYOHHouse1Exterior | |
| Region | |
| [Falkreath Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Hold "Skyrim:Falkreath Hold") | |
| Location | |
| North of [Pinewatch](/wiki/Skyrim:Pinewatch "Skyrim:Pinewatch") | |
| Special Features | |
| # of [Stone Quarries](/wiki/Skyrim:Quarried_Stone "Skyrim:Quarried Stone")[HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") | 1 |

Lakeview Manor

**Lakeview Manor** is a piece of property in [Falkreath Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Hold "Skyrim:Falkreath Hold"), north of [Pinewatch](/wiki/Skyrim:Pinewatch "Skyrim:Pinewatch"). It is one of three potential homes available with the [Hearthfire](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") add-on.

Back view of the house

After installing Hearthfire, you may purchase this plot of land at the [Jarl's Longhouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl%27s_Longhouse_(Falkreath) "Skyrim:Jarl's Longhouse (Falkreath)") in [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath"). If [Siddgeir](/wiki/Skyrim:Siddgeir "Skyrim:Siddgeir") is still the [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl"), speak with his [steward](/wiki/Skyrim:Steward "Skyrim:Steward"), [Nenya](/wiki/Skyrim:Nenya "Skyrim:Nenya"); if the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") have control of the hold, speak with [Tekla](/wiki/Skyrim:Tekla "Skyrim:Tekla"), steward to the new Jarl, [Dengeir of Stuhn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dengeir_of_Stuhn "Skyrim:Dengeir of Stuhn"). You will have to complete the quest [Kill the Bandit Leader](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_the_Bandit_Leader_(Jarl) "Skyrim:Kill the Bandit Leader (Jarl)") before being allowed to purchase land if Siddgeir is Jarl. If you are level 9, then a [letter](/wiki/Skyrim:Letter_from_Jarl_(Jarl%27s_Name)_of_(Jarl%27s_City) "Skyrim:Letter from Jarl (Jarl's Name) of (Jarl's City)") from the Jarl of Falkreath may arrive; reading it gives you an objective to talk to the Jarl, as a part of the Falkreath version of [Build Your Own Home](/wiki/Skyrim:Build_Your_Own_Home "Skyrim:Build Your Own Home"). However, if this has not happened yet, then Siddgeir will require you to complete his version of [Rare Gifts](/wiki/Skyrim:Rare_Gifts "Skyrim:Rare Gifts") before giving the Bandit Leader quest, and the dialogue option to start this quest will not appear if another version of the quest is active. If Dengeir is Jarl, then he will allow you to purchase property out of thanks for your help installing him, whether this was because of events in [Season Unending](/wiki/Skyrim:Season_Unending "Skyrim:Season Unending") or because you [conquered Falkreath for the Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Rescue_from_Fort_Neugrad "Skyrim:Rescue from Fort Neugrad"). When you ask the steward if you can buy a house in the hold, you will be told that there are no houses for sale at that time, but a new plot of land is available. It will cost 5,000 gold.

Your new property, Lakeview Manor, will be marked as an undiscovered location on your map, located between Falkreath and [Riverwood](/wiki/Skyrim:Riverwood "Skyrim:Riverwood"). When you arrive on your new plot of land, you will find a drafting table, carpenter's bench, [anvil](/wiki/Skyrim:Anvil "Skyrim:Anvil"), and chest directly west of the housebuilding area, sheltered by a small cliff. Follow that same cliff face a few steps north to find the [stone quarry](/wiki/Skyrim:Stone_Quarry "Skyrim:Stone Quarry"). There is a [clay deposit](/wiki/Skyrim:Clay_Deposit "Skyrim:Clay Deposit"), [wood chopping block](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Chopping_Block "Skyrim:Wood Chopping Block") and [log pile](/wiki/Skyrim:Sawn_Log "Skyrim:Sawn Log") directly west from the carpenter's workbench, on the other side of the dirt path.

You can begin [building](/wiki/Skyrim:Construction "Skyrim:Construction") your home immediately, with materials provided in the chest when you first arrive. A unique feature at Lakeview Manor is that you have the option to build an apiary. It is initially stocked with one piece of [honeycomb](/wiki/Skyrim:Honeycomb "Skyrim:Honeycomb") and five [bees](/wiki/Skyrim:Bee "Skyrim:Bee"). When the apiary has been emptied, it will eventually be restocked with these items; it is therefore not safe to use as storage. [Bleak Falls Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleak_Falls_Barrow_(place) "Skyrim:Bleak Falls Barrow (place)") can be seen from the north end of the property, beyond [Lake Ilinalta](/wiki/Skyrim:Lake_Ilinalta "Skyrim:Lake Ilinalta").

Like the other player-built homes, you will have the option to expand onto your home with a [Main Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Main_Hall "Skyrim:Main Hall"), cellar, and three wing additions. See [this page](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Hearthfire-Furnishing_Options "Category:Skyrim-Hearthfire-Furnishing Options") for pages detailing the furnishing options in each part of your home.

Should you become a [Thane of Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane_of_Falkreath "Skyrim:Thane of Falkreath"), [Rayya](/wiki/Skyrim:Rayya "Skyrim:Rayya") will become your [housecarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Housecarl "Skyrim:Housecarl"). She will move to Lakeview Manor upon construction of the [small house](/wiki/Skyrim:Small_House_Layout "Skyrim:Small House Layout") layout.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Gunjar](/wiki/Skyrim:Gunjar_(Hearthfire) "Skyrim:Gunjar (Hearthfire)")  [Llewellyn the Nightingale](/wiki/Skyrim:Llewellyn_the_Nightingale "Skyrim:Llewellyn the Nightingale")  [Rayya](/wiki/Skyrim:Rayya "Skyrim:Rayya") [Follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Follower") |

## Related Quests

- **[Bandit Attack](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_Attack "Skyrim:Bandit Attack")**: Rescue your beloved from kidnappers. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Build Your Own Home](/wiki/Skyrim:Build_Your_Own_Home "Skyrim:Build Your Own Home")**: [Construct](/wiki/Skyrim:Construction "Skyrim:Construction") a house for yourself.

## Notes

- Compared to [Windstad Manor](/wiki/Skyrim:Windstad_Manor "Skyrim:Windstad Manor") and [Heljarchen Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Heljarchen_Hall "Skyrim:Heljarchen Hall"), Lakeview Manor sees more random spawn events, including bandits, giants, and wolves.
- A [warlock](/wiki/Skyrim:Warlock "Skyrim:Warlock") can be found a short distance behind the house on the north side, down the hill.
- [Adopted](/wiki/Skyrim:Adoption "Skyrim:Adoption") children appear to favor Lakeview Manor over [Windstad Manor](/wiki/Skyrim:Windstad_Manor "Skyrim:Windstad Manor") and [Heljarchen Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Heljarchen_Hall "Skyrim:Heljarchen Hall"). When spoken to, they sometimes remark, *"I like living here. The lake is so pretty."* (girls) or "*I went fishing at the lake. I almost caught something!"* (boys)
  - For the reactions given by your spouse, see [this page](/wiki/Skyrim:Generic_Dialogue#Spouse_Dialogue "Skyrim:Generic Dialogue").
- You can find two [iron ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore "Skyrim:Iron Ore") veins just to the south of the area, between the crafting area and the pond. There is also a [corundum ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum_Ore "Skyrim:Corundum Ore") vein up the slope to the southwest, around a large gray rock.
- Down the hill before coming to the warlock is a deceased [wood cutter](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Cutter "Skyrim:Wood Cutter") lying next to the unique battleaxe [The Woodsman's Friend](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Woodsman%27s_Friend "Skyrim:The Woodsman's Friend").

## Bugs

- There are a few bugs which affect all houses. See the [Bugs](/wiki/Skyrim:Houses#Bugs "Skyrim:Houses") section of the Houses page for details and fixes.
- Completing the [Dark Brotherhood](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood") quest [Kill Helvard](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_Helvard "Skyrim:Kill Helvard") results in a negative disposition towards you from the Jarl of Falkreath. As such they will not have a high enough disposition towards you in order to offer the dialogue option to purchase the Lakeview estate.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.4, addresses this issue. It corrects this oversight by removing the disposition modifier from the quest.
  -  You can set the Jarl's relationship to a high enough level using `player.setrelationshiprank RefID 4` (replacing "RefID" with [Siddgeir](/wiki/Skyrim:Siddgeir "Skyrim:Siddgeir")'s or [Dengeir](/wiki/Skyrim:Dengeir_of_Stuhn "Skyrim:Dengeir of Stuhn")'s).
  - Changing the jarl through the Civil War questline will automatically give you a high enough disposition with the new jarl in order to buy the property.
- When [Valdimar](/wiki/Skyrim:Valdimar "Skyrim:Valdimar") is assigned as a Housecarl for [Windstad Manor](/wiki/Skyrim:Windstad_Manor "Skyrim:Windstad Manor"), he may be found here instead.
  -  The [Unofficial Hearthfire Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Hearthfire_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Hearthfire Patch"), version 1.0.3, fixes this bug.
- Spouses are scripted to visit the top of the armory porch during the day. If you didn't get this addition, however, they will simply walk to where the stairs would be and stand there until nightfall, occasionally walking in place.
  -  The [Unofficial Hearthfire Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Hearthfire_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Hearthfire Patch"), version 1.1.2, fixes this bug.
- You may be able to hit the hawks on the roof and have them fall to the ground while at the same time still being airborne because the hawks are linked to enable parents that can prevent the script from processing their deaths properly.
  -  The [Unofficial Hearthfire Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Hearthfire_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Hearthfire Patch"), version 2.0.8, fixes this bug.
- If your spouse has been kidnapped and you get a message that says your spouse has been returned, you may find your spouse in your bed, but they will not move and you can not interact with them. **?**
- A game crash may occur in the home which will continue happening if reloading the autosave created upon entering. **?**
  - Removing the workbenches seems to fix this issue.
- The area around the house may experience physics glitches, such as flickering badly.
- The game may crash upon attempting to approach the area around the manor.
- The game may crash upon attempting to place anything on pedestal 0300a8f5 in the Trophy Room. **?**
- The objective "Speak to the Jarl of Falkreath" may become stuck in your miscellaneous quests and not disappear on speaking to the jarl.
  -  The [Unofficial Hearthfire Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Hearthfire_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Hearthfire Patch"), version 2.0.5, fixes this bug.
  -  You can fix this using the console command: `SetObjectiveCompleted BYOHHouseFalkreath 15 1`.
- The southwest side of the house next to the location for the animal pen and tanning rack (to the left of the entrance door) is a spawn point for insects. It might become glitched, allowing torchbugs and luna moths to appear during the day, and butterflies to appear during the night.
- Enemies that randomly spawn outside the house, such as bandits, may spawn inside the footprint of the house, where they cannot be reached. If you ignore them, they will disappear on their own.
  -  You can use the console command `tcl` to pass through the walls of the house and attack the hidden opponent.
  - You can use shouts to hit the enemy while you are pressed against the walls of the manor or sometimes the enemy will stick part of their body out by clipping, which is attackable. Detect Life spell will help with locating them in the structure. If killed while clipping, they can be looted.
- After purchasing the land and beginning construction, the house may not appear. **?**
- The pair of wall sconces on the wall supports on level 1 of an alchemy laboratory will not have the sconce built on the northeast support at Lakeview Manor. **?**
- The pair of wall sconces on either side of the doorway in the north room of the cellar will not have the sconce built on the west side of the doorway at Lakeview Manor.
- The door marker leading out of the basement here can clip with the ladder and sometimes cause followers or the residents to become stuck and unable to leave.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.4, fixes this bug.
- You cannot mount fish on either of the two fish plaques added by the [Fishing](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing "Skyrim:Fishing") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") if you have already done so in another house. See [this section](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing#Bugs "Skyrim:Fishing") for details.
  - The [Official Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim:Special Edition Patch"), version 1.6.629, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Landmarks

## Overview

Ruins of Bthalft

This page lists all the **landmarks** (mountains, clearings, groves, and other geographical features) in [Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim "Skyrim:Skyrim"). [Bodies of water](/wiki/Skyrim:Bodies_of_Water "Skyrim:Bodies of Water") are listed on a separate page.

### General Landmarks

:    **[Altar of Thrond](/wiki/Skyrim:Altar_of_Thrond "Skyrim:Altar of Thrond")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — A landmark west of the Temple of Miraak next to a small cave containing hagravens. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Altar+of+Thrond)
:    **[Bard's Leap Summit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bard%27s_Leap_Summit "Skyrim:Bard's Leap Summit")** — A wooden plank at the very top of Lost Valley Redoubt. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Bard%27s+Leap+Summit)
:    **[Blackbone Isle](/wiki/Skyrim:Blackbone_Isle "Skyrim:Blackbone Isle")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Dead_Man%27s_Dread "Skyrim:Dead Man's Dread") — A haunted island in the Sea of Ghosts. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Blackbone+Isle+%28CC%29)
:    **[Brodir Grove](/wiki/Skyrim:Brodir_Grove "Skyrim:Brodir Grove")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — A small circle of stones northeast of Raven Rock containing reavers. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Brodir+Grove)
:    **[Deep Folk Crossing](/wiki/Skyrim:Deep_Folk_Crossing "Skyrim:Deep Folk Crossing")** — An ancient Dwarven bridge over a weir with structures at either end in the northern part of the Reach. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Deep+Folk+Crossing)
:   **[Druadach Mountains](/wiki/Skyrim:Druadach_Mountains "Skyrim:Druadach Mountains")** — A mountain range in western Skyrim serving as a natural barrier to separate Skyrim from High Rock and Hammerfell. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Druadach+Mountains)
:    **[Frykte Peak](/wiki/Skyrim:Frykte_Peak "Skyrim:Frykte Peak")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — One of the highest points on Solstheim, near Saering's Watch. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Frykte+Peak)
:    **[Giant's Tooth](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant%27s_Tooth "Skyrim:Giant's Tooth")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Bittercup "Skyrim:Bittercup") — A small island in the Sea of Ghosts. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Giant%27s+Tooth+%28CC%29)
:    **[Gjukar's Monument](/wiki/Skyrim:Gjukar%27s_Monument "Skyrim:Gjukar's Monument")** — A stone monument commemorating an ancient battle southeast of Rorikstead. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Gjukar%27s+Monument)
:    **[Horker Island](/wiki/Skyrim:Horker_Island "Skyrim:Horker Island")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — A large island east of Skaal Village occupied by horkers. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Horker+Island)
:    **[Hvitkald Peak‎](/wiki/Skyrim:Hvitkald_Peak "Skyrim:Hvitkald Peak")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — One of the highest points on Solstheim, west of the Abandoned Lodge. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Hvitkald+Peak)
:   **[Jerall Mountains](/wiki/Skyrim:Jerall_Mountains "Skyrim:Jerall Mountains")** — A mountain range that stretches along the southern border of Skyrim. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Jerall+Mountains)
:    **[Mortrag Peak](/wiki/Skyrim:Mortrag_Peak "Skyrim:Mortrag Peak")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — One of the highest points on Solstheim, south of Castle Karstaag Ruins. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Mortrag+Peak)
:    **[Mount Moesring](/wiki/Skyrim:Mount_Moesring "Skyrim:Mount Moesring")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — One of the highest points on Solstheim, south of Moesring Pass. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Mount+Moesring)
:    **[Orphan Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Orphan_Rock "Skyrim:Orphan Rock")** — A wooded valley with a central rock plateau northeast of Helgen containing witches or hags led by a hagraven. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Orphan+Rock)
:    **[Reachwind Eyrie](/wiki/Skyrim:Reachwind_Eyrie "Skyrim:Reachwind Eyrie")** — A small Dwarven tower east-southeast of Markarth. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Reachwind+Eyrie)
:    **[Ruins of Bthalft](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruins_of_Bthalft "Skyrim:Ruins of Bthalft")** — A small Dwarven ruin south of Ivarstead containing bandits. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Ruins+of+Bthalft)
:    **[Ruins of Rkund](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruins_of_Rkund "Skyrim:Ruins of Rkund")** — A small Dwarven ruin in the mountains southwest of Riften containing a wispmother and wisps. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Ruins+of+Rkund)
:    **[Sky Haven Temple](/wiki/Skyrim:Sky_Haven_Temple "Skyrim:Sky Haven Temple")** — A large mountaintop fort that served as the major Blades temple and outpost in Skyrim, now long abandoned and in Forsworn territory. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Sky+Haven+Temple)
:    **[Stalhrim Source](/wiki/Skyrim:Stalhrim_Source "Skyrim:Stalhrim Source")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — A small outdoor Nordic ruin east of Broken Tusk Mine and southwest of Mortrag Peak. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Stalhrim+Source)
:    **[Throat of the World](/wiki/Skyrim:Throat_of_the_World "Skyrim:Throat of the World")** — The highest mountain in Tamriel, located southeast of Whiterun. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Throat+of+the+World)
:   **[Velothi Mountains](/wiki/Skyrim:Velothi_Mountains "Skyrim:Velothi Mountains")** — A mountain range that stretches along the eastern border of Skyrim. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Velothi+Mountains)
:    **[Weynon Stones](/wiki/Skyrim:Weynon_Stones "Skyrim:Weynon Stones")** — A landmark consisting of a circle of stones. It is located between Korvanjund and Fort Dunstad, just south of the path. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Weynon+Stones)

### Clearings

:    **[Autumnshade Clearing](/wiki/Skyrim:Autumnshade_Clearing "Skyrim:Autumnshade Clearing")** — A circular glade inhabited by a spriggan and its attending animals. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Autumnshade+Clearing)
:    **[Clearpine Pond](/wiki/Skyrim:Clearpine_Pond "Skyrim:Clearpine Pond")** — A pond with a small island, located west-southwest of Solitude, just to the northeast of Pinemoon Cave. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Clearpine+Pond)
:    **[Clearspring Tarn](/wiki/Skyrim:Clearspring_Tarn "Skyrim:Clearspring Tarn")** — A small mountain pool on the cliff overlooking Eastmarch, due east of Snapleg Cave and west of Shor's Stone. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Clearspring+Tarn)
:    **[Headwaters of Harstrad](/wiki/Skyrim:Headwaters_of_Harstrad "Skyrim:Headwaters of Harstrad")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — The source of the Harstrad River. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Headwaters+of+Harstrad)
:    **[Mara's Eye Pond](/wiki/Skyrim:Mara%27s_Eye_Pond "Skyrim:Mara's Eye Pond")** — A small lake due east of Gallows Rock. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Mara%27s+Eye+Pond)

### Groves

:    **[Ancestor Glade](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancestor_Glade "Skyrim:Ancestor Glade")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") — A small glade in a cavern east-southeast of Falkreath. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Ancestor+Glade+%28DG%29)
:    **[Evergreen Grove](/wiki/Skyrim:Evergreen_Grove "Skyrim:Evergreen Grove")** — A grove of trees concealing a small pond fed by a rocky stream, just southwest of Half-Moon Mill. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Evergreen+Grove)
:    **[Giant's Grove](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant%27s_Grove "Skyrim:Giant's Grove")** — A grove accessed through Fallowstone Cave containing a giant whose tribe has defiled a shrine of Malacath. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Giant%27s+Grove)
:    **[Greenspring Hollow](/wiki/Skyrim:Greenspring_Hollow "Skyrim:Greenspring Hollow")** — A shallow outdoor cave west-northwest of Whiterun containing a leveled animal. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Greenspring+Hollow)
:    **[Shrouded Grove](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrouded_Grove "Skyrim:Shrouded Grove")** — A grove with a small cave located in the Pale. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Shrouded+Grove)
:    **[Witchmist Grove](/wiki/Skyrim:Witchmist_Grove "Skyrim:Witchmist Grove")** — A small shack north of Bonestrewn Crest and south of Kynesgrove. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Witchmist+Grove)

### Passes

:    **[Brittleshin Pass](/wiki/Skyrim:Brittleshin_Pass "Skyrim:Brittleshin Pass")** — A small passage through the mountains between Whiterun Hold and Falkreath Hold containing a necromancer and skeletons. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Brittleshin+Pass)
:    **[Cold Rock Pass](/wiki/Skyrim:Cold_Rock_Pass "Skyrim:Cold Rock Pass")** — A small passage through a mountain south-southwest of Morthal containing a frost troll. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Cold+Rock+Pass)
:   **[Dunmeth Pass](/wiki/Skyrim:Dunmeth_Pass "Skyrim:Dunmeth Pass")** — A mountain pass and one of the few traversable roads through the Velothi Mountains between northwest Morrowind and northeast Skyrim. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Dunmeth+Pass)
:    **[Moesring Pass](/wiki/Skyrim:Moesring_Pass "Skyrim:Moesring Pass")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — A mountain pass due northwest of the Temple of Miraak, inhabited by rieklings guarding the nearby Strange Vessel. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Moesring+Pass)
:   **[Skybound Watch Pass](/wiki/Skyrim:Skybound_Watch_Pass "Skyrim:Skybound Watch Pass")** — A small Nordic tower and ruin northeast of Helgen containing bandits and a giant frostbite spider. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Skybound+Watch+Pass)
:    **[Wayward Pass](/wiki/Skyrim:Wayward_Pass "Skyrim:Wayward Pass")** — A pass through the mountains in the southwest of Winterhold. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Wayward+Pass)

# Skyrim:Landmarks

## Overview

Ruins of Bthalft

This page lists all the **landmarks** (mountains, clearings, groves, and other geographical features) in [Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim "Skyrim:Skyrim"). [Bodies of water](/wiki/Skyrim:Bodies_of_Water "Skyrim:Bodies of Water") are listed on a separate page.

:    **[Altar of Thrond](/wiki/Skyrim:Altar_of_Thrond "Skyrim:Altar of Thrond")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — A landmark west of the Temple of Miraak next to a small cave containing hagravens. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Altar+of+Thrond)

### Clearings

:    **[Autumnshade Clearing](/wiki/Skyrim:Autumnshade_Clearing "Skyrim:Autumnshade Clearing")** — A circular glade inhabited by a spriggan and its attending animals. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Autumnshade+Clearing)

### Groves

### Passes

:    **[Brittleshin Pass](/wiki/Skyrim:Brittleshin_Pass "Skyrim:Brittleshin Pass")** — A small passage through the mountains between Whiterun Hold and Falkreath Hold containing a necromancer and skeletons. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Brittleshin+Pass)
:    **[Cold Rock Pass](/wiki/Skyrim:Cold_Rock_Pass "Skyrim:Cold Rock Pass")** — A small passage through a mountain south-southwest of Morthal containing a frost troll. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Cold+Rock+Pass)
:   **[Dunmeth Pass](/wiki/Skyrim:Dunmeth_Pass "Skyrim:Dunmeth Pass")** — A mountain pass and one of the few traversable roads through the Velothi Mountains between northwest Morrowind and northeast Skyrim. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Dunmeth+Pass)
:    **[Moesring Pass](/wiki/Skyrim:Moesring_Pass "Skyrim:Moesring Pass")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — A mountain pass due northwest of the Temple of Miraak, inhabited by rieklings guarding the nearby Strange Vessel. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Moesring+Pass)
:   **[Skybound Watch Pass](/wiki/Skyrim:Skybound_Watch_Pass "Skyrim:Skybound Watch Pass")** — A small Nordic tower and ruin northeast of Helgen containing bandits and a giant frostbite spider. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Skybound+Watch+Pass)
:    **[Wayward Pass](/wiki/Skyrim:Wayward_Pass "Skyrim:Wayward Pass")** — A pass through the mountains in the southwest of Winterhold. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Wayward+Pass)

# Skyrim:Landmarks

## Overview

Ruins of Bthalft

This page lists all the **landmarks** (mountains, clearings, groves, and other geographical features) in [Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim "Skyrim:Skyrim"). [Bodies of water](/wiki/Skyrim:Bodies_of_Water "Skyrim:Bodies of Water") are listed on a separate page.

### General Landmarks

:    **[Altar of Thrond](/wiki/Skyrim:Altar_of_Thrond "Skyrim:Altar of Thrond")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — A landmark west of the Temple of Miraak next to a small cave containing hagravens. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Altar+of+Thrond)
:    **[Bard's Leap Summit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bard%27s_Leap_Summit "Skyrim:Bard's Leap Summit")** — A wooden plank at the very top of Lost Valley Redoubt. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Bard%27s+Leap+Summit)
:    **[Blackbone Isle](/wiki/Skyrim:Blackbone_Isle "Skyrim:Blackbone Isle")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Dead_Man%27s_Dread "Skyrim:Dead Man's Dread") — A haunted island in the Sea of Ghosts. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Blackbone+Isle+%28CC%29)
:    **[Brodir Grove](/wiki/Skyrim:Brodir_Grove "Skyrim:Brodir Grove")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — A small circle of stones northeast of Raven Rock containing reavers. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Brodir+Grove)
:    **[Deep Folk Crossing](/wiki/Skyrim:Deep_Folk_Crossing "Skyrim:Deep Folk Crossing")** — An ancient Dwarven bridge over a weir with structures at either end in the northern part of the Reach. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Deep+Folk+Crossing)
:   **[Druadach Mountains](/wiki/Skyrim:Druadach_Mountains "Skyrim:Druadach Mountains")** — A mountain range in western Skyrim serving as a natural barrier to separate Skyrim from High Rock and Hammerfell. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Druadach+Mountains)
:    **[Frykte Peak](/wiki/Skyrim:Frykte_Peak "Skyrim:Frykte Peak")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — One of the highest points on Solstheim, near Saering's Watch. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Frykte+Peak)
:    **[Giant's Tooth](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant%27s_Tooth "Skyrim:Giant's Tooth")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Bittercup "Skyrim:Bittercup") — A small island in the Sea of Ghosts. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Giant%27s+Tooth+%28CC%29)
:    **[Gjukar's Monument](/wiki/Skyrim:Gjukar%27s_Monument "Skyrim:Gjukar's Monument")** — A stone monument commemorating an ancient battle southeast of Rorikstead. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Gjukar%27s+Monument)
:    **[Horker Island](/wiki/Skyrim:Horker_Island "Skyrim:Horker Island")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — A large island east of Skaal Village occupied by horkers. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Horker+Island)
:    **[Hvitkald Peak‎](/wiki/Skyrim:Hvitkald_Peak "Skyrim:Hvitkald Peak")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — One of the highest points on Solstheim, west of the Abandoned Lodge. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Hvitkald+Peak)
:   **[Jerall Mountains](/wiki/Skyrim:Jerall_Mountains "Skyrim:Jerall Mountains")** — A mountain range that stretches along the southern border of Skyrim. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Jerall+Mountains)
:    **[Mortrag Peak](/wiki/Skyrim:Mortrag_Peak "Skyrim:Mortrag Peak")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — One of the highest points on Solstheim, south of Castle Karstaag Ruins. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Mortrag+Peak)
:    **[Mount Moesring](/wiki/Skyrim:Mount_Moesring "Skyrim:Mount Moesring")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — One of the highest points on Solstheim, south of Moesring Pass. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Mount+Moesring)
:    **[Orphan Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Orphan_Rock "Skyrim:Orphan Rock")** — A wooded valley with a central rock plateau northeast of Helgen containing witches or hags led by a hagraven. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Orphan+Rock)
:    **[Reachwind Eyrie](/wiki/Skyrim:Reachwind_Eyrie "Skyrim:Reachwind Eyrie")** — A small Dwarven tower east-southeast of Markarth. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Reachwind+Eyrie)
:    **[Ruins of Bthalft](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruins_of_Bthalft "Skyrim:Ruins of Bthalft")** — A small Dwarven ruin south of Ivarstead containing bandits. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Ruins+of+Bthalft)
:    **[Ruins of Rkund](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruins_of_Rkund "Skyrim:Ruins of Rkund")** — A small Dwarven ruin in the mountains southwest of Riften containing a wispmother and wisps. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Ruins+of+Rkund)
:    **[Sky Haven Temple](/wiki/Skyrim:Sky_Haven_Temple "Skyrim:Sky Haven Temple")** — A large mountaintop fort that served as the major Blades temple and outpost in Skyrim, now long abandoned and in Forsworn territory. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Sky+Haven+Temple)
:    **[Stalhrim Source](/wiki/Skyrim:Stalhrim_Source "Skyrim:Stalhrim Source")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — A small outdoor Nordic ruin east of Broken Tusk Mine and southwest of Mortrag Peak. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Stalhrim+Source)
:    **[Throat of the World](/wiki/Skyrim:Throat_of_the_World "Skyrim:Throat of the World")** — The highest mountain in Tamriel, located southeast of Whiterun. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Throat+of+the+World)
:   **[Velothi Mountains](/wiki/Skyrim:Velothi_Mountains "Skyrim:Velothi Mountains")** — A mountain range that stretches along the eastern border of Skyrim. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Velothi+Mountains)
:    **[Weynon Stones](/wiki/Skyrim:Weynon_Stones "Skyrim:Weynon Stones")** — A landmark consisting of a circle of stones. It is located between Korvanjund and Fort Dunstad, just south of the path. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Weynon+Stones)

### Clearings

:    **[Autumnshade Clearing](/wiki/Skyrim:Autumnshade_Clearing "Skyrim:Autumnshade Clearing")** — A circular glade inhabited by a spriggan and its attending animals. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Autumnshade+Clearing)
:    **[Clearpine Pond](/wiki/Skyrim:Clearpine_Pond "Skyrim:Clearpine Pond")** — A pond with a small island, located west-southwest of Solitude, just to the northeast of Pinemoon Cave. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Clearpine+Pond)
:    **[Clearspring Tarn](/wiki/Skyrim:Clearspring_Tarn "Skyrim:Clearspring Tarn")** — A small mountain pool on the cliff overlooking Eastmarch, due east of Snapleg Cave and west of Shor's Stone. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Clearspring+Tarn)
:    **[Headwaters of Harstrad](/wiki/Skyrim:Headwaters_of_Harstrad "Skyrim:Headwaters of Harstrad")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — The source of the Harstrad River. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Headwaters+of+Harstrad)
:    **[Mara's Eye Pond](/wiki/Skyrim:Mara%27s_Eye_Pond "Skyrim:Mara's Eye Pond")** — A small lake due east of Gallows Rock. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Mara%27s+Eye+Pond)

### Groves

:    **[Ancestor Glade](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancestor_Glade "Skyrim:Ancestor Glade")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") — A small glade in a cavern east-southeast of Falkreath. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Ancestor+Glade+%28DG%29)
:    **[Evergreen Grove](/wiki/Skyrim:Evergreen_Grove "Skyrim:Evergreen Grove")** — A grove of trees concealing a small pond fed by a rocky stream, just southwest of Half-Moon Mill. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Evergreen+Grove)
:    **[Giant's Grove](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant%27s_Grove "Skyrim:Giant's Grove")** — A grove accessed through Fallowstone Cave containing a giant whose tribe has defiled a shrine of Malacath. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Giant%27s+Grove)
:    **[Greenspring Hollow](/wiki/Skyrim:Greenspring_Hollow "Skyrim:Greenspring Hollow")** — A shallow outdoor cave west-northwest of Whiterun containing a leveled animal. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Greenspring+Hollow)
:    **[Shrouded Grove](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrouded_Grove "Skyrim:Shrouded Grove")** — A grove with a small cave located in the Pale. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Shrouded+Grove)
:    **[Witchmist Grove](/wiki/Skyrim:Witchmist_Grove "Skyrim:Witchmist Grove")** — A small shack north of Bonestrewn Crest and south of Kynesgrove. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Witchmist+Grove)

### Passes

:    **[Brittleshin Pass](/wiki/Skyrim:Brittleshin_Pass "Skyrim:Brittleshin Pass")** — A small passage through the mountains between Whiterun Hold and Falkreath Hold containing a necromancer and skeletons. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Brittleshin+Pass)
:    **[Cold Rock Pass](/wiki/Skyrim:Cold_Rock_Pass "Skyrim:Cold Rock Pass")** — A small passage through a mountain south-southwest of Morthal containing a frost troll. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Cold+Rock+Pass)
:   **[Dunmeth Pass](/wiki/Skyrim:Dunmeth_Pass "Skyrim:Dunmeth Pass")** — A mountain pass and one of the few traversable roads through the Velothi Mountains between northwest Morrowind and northeast Skyrim. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Dunmeth+Pass)
:    **[Moesring Pass](/wiki/Skyrim:Moesring_Pass "Skyrim:Moesring Pass")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — A mountain pass due northwest of the Temple of Miraak, inhabited by rieklings guarding the nearby Strange Vessel. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Moesring+Pass)
:   **[Skybound Watch Pass](/wiki/Skyrim:Skybound_Watch_Pass "Skyrim:Skybound Watch Pass")** — A small Nordic tower and ruin northeast of Helgen containing bandits and a giant frostbite spider. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Skybound+Watch+Pass)
:    **[Wayward Pass](/wiki/Skyrim:Wayward_Pass "Skyrim:Wayward Pass")** — A pass through the mountains in the southwest of Winterhold. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Wayward+Pass)

Ruins of Bthalft

This page lists all the **landmarks** (mountains, clearings, groves, and other geographical features) in [Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim "Skyrim:Skyrim"). [Bodies of water](/wiki/Skyrim:Bodies_of_Water "Skyrim:Bodies of Water") are listed on a separate page.

### Clearings

:    **[Autumnshade Clearing](/wiki/Skyrim:Autumnshade_Clearing "Skyrim:Autumnshade Clearing")** — A circular glade inhabited by a spriggan and its attending animals. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Autumnshade+Clearing)

### Groves

### Passes

:    **[Brittleshin Pass](/wiki/Skyrim:Brittleshin_Pass "Skyrim:Brittleshin Pass")** — A small passage through the mountains between Whiterun Hold and Falkreath Hold containing a necromancer and skeletons. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Brittleshin+Pass)
:    **[Cold Rock Pass](/wiki/Skyrim:Cold_Rock_Pass "Skyrim:Cold Rock Pass")** — A small passage through a mountain south-southwest of Morthal containing a frost troll. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Cold+Rock+Pass)
:   **[Dunmeth Pass](/wiki/Skyrim:Dunmeth_Pass "Skyrim:Dunmeth Pass")** — A mountain pass and one of the few traversable roads through the Velothi Mountains between northwest Morrowind and northeast Skyrim. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Dunmeth+Pass)
:    **[Moesring Pass](/wiki/Skyrim:Moesring_Pass "Skyrim:Moesring Pass")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — A mountain pass due northwest of the Temple of Miraak, inhabited by rieklings guarding the nearby Strange Vessel. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Moesring+Pass)
:   **[Skybound Watch Pass](/wiki/Skyrim:Skybound_Watch_Pass "Skyrim:Skybound Watch Pass")** — A small Nordic tower and ruin northeast of Helgen containing bandits and a giant frostbite spider. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Skybound+Watch+Pass)
:    **[Wayward Pass](/wiki/Skyrim:Wayward_Pass "Skyrim:Wayward Pass")** — A pass through the mountains in the southwest of Winterhold. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Wayward+Pass)

# Skyrim:Larak's Longhouse

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This article is being developed as part of the Skyrim Houses Redesign Project. If you see this tag it means the article can still be improved. Please see the [project page](/wiki/UESPWiki:SHRP "UESPWiki:SHRP") for guidelines.** |

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Home: Larak's Longhouse ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Larak%27s+Longhouse)) | | |
| # of Zones | 1 |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| MorKhazgurLaraksLonghouse | |
| Region | |
| [The Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Reach "Skyrim:The Reach") | |
| Location | |
| [Mor Khazgur](/wiki/Skyrim:Mor_Khazgur "Skyrim:Mor Khazgur") | |

[Larak](/wiki/Skyrim:Chief_Larak "Skyrim:Chief Larak")'s Longhouse

**Larak's Longhouse** is the longhouse of [Chief Larak](/wiki/Skyrim:Chief_Larak "Skyrim:Chief Larak"), located in the Orc stronghold of [Mor Khazgur](/wiki/Skyrim:Mor_Khazgur "Skyrim:Mor Khazgur").

The longhouse is in the center of the stronghold, and is immediately visible upon entering. It does not differ much from other Orc longhouses, inside and out.

## Residents

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| | Residents | | --- | | **[Chief Larak](/wiki/Skyrim:Chief_Larak "Skyrim:Chief Larak")**  **[Bagrak](/wiki/Skyrim:Bagrak "Skyrim:Bagrak")**  **[Borgakh the Steel Heart](/wiki/Skyrim:Borgakh_the_Steel_Heart "Skyrim:Borgakh the Steel Heart")**  **[Sharamph](/wiki/Skyrim:Sharamph "Skyrim:Sharamph")**  **[Shuftharz](/wiki/Skyrim:Shuftharz "Skyrim:Shuftharz")** | |

### Larak's Longhouse Exterior

On the exterior, Larak's Longhouse is architecturally identical to the other longhouses. To the left of the entrance is a training dummy, which Borgakh the Steel Heart frequently wails on during the day. To the right is a wooden rack, with three harvestable salmon. Just next to that are a wooden table and chair, where Chief Larak sits during the day. Across from the longhouse is an alchemy station.

On the left side of the structure are a forge and a small hut which covers a few barrels and a novice-locked entrance to [Mor Khazgur cellar](/wiki/Skyrim:Mor_Khazgur_Cellar "Skyrim:Mor Khazgur Cellar"). On the right of the longhouse is another hut. Under it are a chest containing minor loot and a hanging rack of harvestable [pheasant](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") and [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food").

### Larak's Longhouse Interior

As you enter, to the north (directly in front of the entrance) there is a fire pit with a charred skeever just above it available for harvest. Just next to that is a hanging rack with rabbit as well as more pheasant and garlic.

To the east, on the right side of the longhouse, is Sharamph's room. It holds a weapons rack as well as a chest with minor loot next to the bed. On the opposite end of the longhouse is where all of the other Orcs sleep. Here you can find a boss chest, but be careful, as taking from this chest (as well as anything else within the stronghold) is considered stealing.

## Notes

- Even though [Chief Larak](/wiki/Skyrim:Chief_Larak "Skyrim:Chief Larak") and [Shuftharz](/wiki/Skyrim:Shuftharz "Skyrim:Shuftharz") are married, they do not sleep in the same bed. They will occasionally switch beds with each other.
- Strangely, not all of the Orcs in Mor Khazgur are scripted to sleep. These Orcs are [Bagrak](/wiki/Skyrim:Bagrak "Skyrim:Bagrak"), [Gul](/wiki/Skyrim:Gul "Skyrim:Gul"), [Ghamorz](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghamorz "Skyrim:Ghamorz"), and [Olur](/wiki/Skyrim:Olur "Skyrim:Olur").

## Overview

| Southwest of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften"), in the [Orc](/wiki/Skyrim:Orc "Skyrim:Orc") stronghold of [Largashbur](/wiki/Skyrim:Largashbur "Skyrim:Largashbur") | |

Largashbur Cellar

**Largashbur Cellar** is a cellar located in the [Orc](/wiki/Skyrim:Orc "Skyrim:Orc") stronghold of [Largashbur](/wiki/Skyrim:Largashbur "Skyrim:Largashbur") behind the [Largashbur Longhouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Largashbur_Longhouse "Skyrim:Largashbur Longhouse").

Down in the cellar

## Largashbur Cellar

Upon entering via the trapdoor, the chamber appears to be a natural cave rather than a normal cellar. There is a raised wooden platform to the northeast, with a mead barrel, a food barrel, a meat barrel, two chairs, and a small square wooden table holding a loaf of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"). To the southwest are three double-banked sets of shelves across the room, holding a large [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"), a small coin purse, three random [potions](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions"), a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe"), eight common books, a copy of the [Block](/wiki/Skyrim:Block "Skyrim:Block") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Battle of Red Mountain](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_of_Red_Mountain "Skyrim:Battle of Red Mountain")*, an [ingredient](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients") barrel, and twelve food sacks. Beyond the shelves is a counter running across the room, with a [goat cheese wheel](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wheel") on top, and a small coin purse, a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), two bottles of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), and six bottles of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead") underneath. Against the northwest wall is a novice-locked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") containing minor loot, with a round wooden table holding a [goat cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wedge") and two chairs to the right.

## Overview

Largashbur Longhouse

**Largashbur Longhouse** is the longhouse of [Chief Yamarz](/wiki/Skyrim:Chief_Yamarz "Skyrim:Chief Yamarz"), located in the Orc stronghold of [Largashbur](/wiki/Skyrim:Largashbur "Skyrim:Largashbur").

The longhouse is home to [Chief Yamarz](/wiki/Skyrim:Chief_Yamarz "Skyrim:Chief Yamarz"), [Atub](/wiki/Skyrim:Atub "Skyrim:Atub"), [Garakh](/wiki/Skyrim:Garakh "Skyrim:Garakh"), [Gularzob](/wiki/Skyrim:Gularzob "Skyrim:Gularzob") (who will be named Chief after the end of the relevant [quest](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Cursed_Tribe "Skyrim:The Cursed Tribe")), [Lob](/wiki/Skyrim:Lob "Skyrim:Lob"), [Ogol](/wiki/Skyrim:Ogol "Skyrim:Ogol") and [Ugor](/wiki/Skyrim:Ugor "Skyrim:Ugor").

## Residents

|  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| | Largashbur Longhouse | | --- | | **[Chief Yamarz](/wiki/Skyrim:Chief_Yamarz "Skyrim:Chief Yamarz")**  **[Atub](/wiki/Skyrim:Atub "Skyrim:Atub")** [Trainer (Expert)](/wiki/Skyrim:Trainers "Trainer (Expert)")[Illusion (Expert)](/wiki/Skyrim:Illusion "Illusion (Expert)") **[Garakh](/wiki/Skyrim:Garakh "Skyrim:Garakh")**  **[Gularzob](/wiki/Skyrim:Gularzob "Skyrim:Gularzob")**  **[Lob](/wiki/Skyrim:Lob "Skyrim:Lob")** [Follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Follower") **[Ogol](/wiki/Skyrim:Ogol "Skyrim:Ogol")** [Follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Follower") **[Ugor](/wiki/Skyrim:Ugor "Skyrim:Ugor")** [Follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Follower") | | | Camp | | --- | | **[Unnamed Orcs](/wiki/Skyrim:Orc "Skyrim:Orc")** | |

### Largashbur Longhouse

The Largashbur Longhouse can be found in the Orc stronghold of [Largashbur](/wiki/Skyrim:Largashbur "Skyrim:Largashbur"), near the entrance to the stronghold. Entering the longhouse is trespassing unless you have been named [Blood-Kin](/wiki/Skyrim:Blood-Kin "Skyrim:Blood-Kin") to the Orcs. Any Orc can grant you this title, but they will only do so after you have done something for them. Then all Orcs will acknowledge your status and make you welcome.

Upon entering the longhouse, the firepit is opposite the entrance, in front of the southeast wall, with a couple of pots hanging over it. In the right-hand pot is a portion of [grilled leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Grilled_Leeks "Skyrim:Grilled Leeks"). Around the hearth are a pair of [leather boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Boots "Skyrim:Leather Boots") and a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe") on a pile of firewood. There is a long wooden table to the left holding several loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), a [goat cheese wheel](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wheel"), two [charred skeever hides](/wiki/Skyrim:Charred_Skeever_Hide "Skyrim:Charred Skeever Hide"), a [potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato"), two bulbs of [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") and an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"). Above the table is a hanging rack with two [rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)") and a [pheasant](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant "Skyrim:Pheasant") hanging from it. To the left of the table, still against the southeast wall is a set of shelves holding a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), four bottles of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"), a loaf of bread and a basket on the bottom shelf containing a [cabbage](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage"). Hanging from the ceiling above the shelves are two garlic braids and a bunch of [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam"). There is a doorway to the north leading into a bedroom. There are [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") barrels and sacks all around the longhouse.

To the right of the fireplace is another set of shelves holding two bottle of Nord mead, a [bear pelt](/wiki/Skyrim:Bear_Pelt "Skyrim:Bear Pelt") and a random [helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Helmet "Skyrim:Helmet") and random [gauntlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Gauntlets "Skyrim:Gauntlets") or bracers. There is a chair in front of this against the southwest wall. In the middle of this room is a small round wooden table and four chairs, with a small square wooden table in the northwestern corner with a further two chairs. A second doorway to another bedroom is in the southwest wall, with a sideboard to the right of the doorway, it holds a [troll skull](/wiki/Skyrim:Troll_Skull "Skyrim:Troll Skull"), a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), three bunches of [jazbay grapes](/wiki/Skyrim:Jazbay_Grapes "Skyrim:Jazbay Grapes") and two fillets of [salmon meat](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Meat "Skyrim:Salmon Meat").

Through the doorway to the southwest, is a room with three single bed along the walls, an end table and a dresser that has copies of *[Thief of Virtue](/wiki/Skyrim:Thief_of_Virtue "Skyrim:Thief of Virtue")* and *[The Real Barenziah, v1](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Real_Barenziah,_v1 "Skyrim:The Real Barenziah, v1")*. There is a partitioned area to the north with a stool, bucket and copy of *[Brief History of the Empire, v2](/wiki/Skyrim:Brief_History_of_the_Empire,_v2 "Skyrim:Brief History of the Empire, v2")*. Opposite this is a dresser with an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") containing minor loot. Beyond the toilet area is another tiny room with a single bed and level-locked chest.

Through the doorway to the north is another bedroom this one is for the Chief, it has a large double bed coming out from the west wall, with an end table to the right and a dresser to the left of the bed, which holds a random [potion of stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Stamina") and a copy of *[The True Nature of Orcs](/wiki/Skyrim:The_True_Nature_of_Orcs "Skyrim:The True Nature of Orcs")*. There is also a medium [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse") on the floor to the left of the dresser. In the northern corner is an unlocked chest and against the east wall is a single bed with a table by the head and a pair of [iron boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Boots "Skyrim:Iron Boots") by the foot of the bed. On the table are five loose [septims](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold"), a [rock warbler egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Rock_Warbler_Egg "Skyrim:Rock Warbler Egg"), an [Orcish dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Orcish_Dagger "Skyrim:Orcish Dagger") and random helmet. Above the table is a bookshelf with copies of *[The wolf Queen, v2](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Wolf_Queen,_v2 "Skyrim:The Wolf Queen, v2")*, *[Chance's Folly](/wiki/Skyrim:Chance%27s_Folly "Skyrim:Chance's Folly")*, *[Brief History of the Empire, v1](/wiki/Skyrim:Brief_History_of_the_Empire,_v1 "Skyrim:Brief History of the Empire, v1")* and *[Argonian Account, Book 1](/wiki/Skyrim:Argonian_Account,_Book_1 "Skyrim:Argonian Account, Book 1")*, along with a [potion of minor healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), a small coin purse and on a second shelf a bottle of wine and a bottle of [Black-Briar mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Black-Briar_Mead "Skyrim:Black-Briar Mead").

The entrance to [Largashbur Cellar](/wiki/Skyrim:Largashbur_Cellar "Skyrim:Largashbur Cellar") is behind the longhouse. You will see a trapped door behind the barrels, bales of straw, and a level-locked chest.

Largashbur

**Largashbur** is an accursed [Orc stronghold](/wiki/Skyrim:Orc_Strongholds "Skyrim:Orc Strongholds") beset by [giants](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant "Skyrim:Giant") in the southeast of [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim"), west-southwest of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften").

The stronghold contains two zones: *[Largashbur Longhouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Largashbur_Longhouse "Skyrim:Largashbur Longhouse")* and *[Largashbur Cellar](/wiki/Skyrim:Largashbur_Cellar "Skyrim:Largashbur Cellar")*.

The stronghold features a makeshift altar to [Malacath](/wiki/Skyrim:Malacath "Skyrim:Malacath"), adorned with [Orcish Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Orcish_Armor "Skyrim:Orcish Armor"), [Orcish Boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Orcish_Boots "Skyrim:Orcish Boots"), an [Orcish Helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Orcish_Helmet "Skyrim:Orcish Helmet"), an [Orcish Shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Orcish_Shield "Skyrim:Orcish Shield"), an [Orcish Battleaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Orcish_Battleaxe "Skyrim:Orcish Battleaxe"), and seven bunches of [lavender](/wiki/Skyrim:Lavender "Skyrim:Lavender"). Largashbur is the only one of the four Orc strongholds not to have a mine, and indeed has lent two of its working-age Orcs to [Narzulbur](/wiki/Skyrim:Narzulbur "Skyrim:Narzulbur"), since Narzulbur has a mine but a shortage of workers.

As with all Orc Strongholds, you must become [Blood-Kin](/wiki/Skyrim:Blood-Kin "Skyrim:Blood-Kin") to the [Orcs](/wiki/Skyrim:Orc "Skyrim:Orc") before you are welcome in the stronghold and able to barter or receive other services.

## Largashbur Residents

|  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| | [Largashbur Longhouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Largashbur_Longhouse "Skyrim:Largashbur Longhouse") | | --- | | **[Chief Yamarz](/wiki/Skyrim:Chief_Yamarz "Skyrim:Chief Yamarz")**  **[Atub](/wiki/Skyrim:Atub "Skyrim:Atub")** [Trainer (Expert)](/wiki/Skyrim:Trainers "Trainer (Expert)")[Illusion (Expert)](/wiki/Skyrim:Illusion "Illusion (Expert)") **[Garakh](/wiki/Skyrim:Garakh "Skyrim:Garakh")**  **[Gularzob](/wiki/Skyrim:Gularzob "Skyrim:Gularzob")**  **[Lob](/wiki/Skyrim:Lob "Skyrim:Lob")** [Follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Follower") **[Ogol](/wiki/Skyrim:Ogol "Skyrim:Ogol")** [Follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Follower") **[Ugor](/wiki/Skyrim:Ugor "Skyrim:Ugor")** [Follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Follower") | | | Camp | | --- | | **[Unnamed Orcs](/wiki/Skyrim:Orc "Skyrim:Orc")** | |

#### Daedric

- **[The Cursed Tribe](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Cursed_Tribe "Skyrim:The Cursed Tribe")**: Help lift the curse placed on the [Orcs](/wiki/Skyrim:Orc "Skyrim:Orc") of Largashbur by [Malacath](/wiki/Lore:Malacath "Lore:Malacath").

### Exterior

Two [goats](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat "Skyrim:Goat") and a [horse](/wiki/Skyrim:Horse "Skyrim:Horse") are found in the exterior area.

### Buildings

- [Largashbur Longhouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Largashbur_Longhouse "Skyrim:Largashbur Longhouse") - Primary dwelling for all residents.
- [Largashbur Cellar](/wiki/Skyrim:Largashbur_Cellar "Skyrim:Largashbur Cellar") - Storage cellar and makeshift bar, with a few food barrels and sacks and a level-locked chest just outside the trapdoor entrance behind the longhouse.
- Apothecary's Shack - Exterior building with an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Lab "Skyrim:Alchemy Lab"), and a few ingredients on a set of shelves and hanging from a pole.
- Blacksmith's Shack - Exterior building with a [forge](/wiki/Skyrim:Forge "Skyrim:Forge"), a [workbench](/wiki/Skyrim:Workbench "Skyrim:Workbench"), and a [grindstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Grindstone "Skyrim:Grindstone"), and a few pieces of Orcish equipment on a set of shelves, a table, and a barrel.
- Tanner's Shed - Exterior building with a [tanning rack](/wiki/Skyrim:Tanning_Rack "Skyrim:Tanning Rack"), a food barrel, and a few pelts on a table.

## Notes

- [Lob](/wiki/Skyrim:Lob "Skyrim:Lob"), [Ogol](/wiki/Skyrim:Ogol "Skyrim:Ogol"), [Ugor](/wiki/Skyrim:Ugor "Skyrim:Ugor"), and the unnamed Orcs outside the stronghold are not essential, and can be easily killed by invading giants, even before you arrive.
- After completing [The Cursed Tribe](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Cursed_Tribe "Skyrim:The Cursed Tribe"), Lob, Ogol, and Ugor can be recruited as followers.

## Bugs

- Triggering combat here while the quest The Cursed Tribe is active can block quest progression.
  - The [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch"), version 1.1, fixes this bug.
- The giant will continue to respawn and attack the stronghold after the quest The Cursed Tribe has been completed, as the disable flag is not implemented. This can eventually result in the death of everyone within other than Atub.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.5, fixes this bug.
  -  The giant's attacks can be stopped by opening the console and entering the code `"000A0E72".disable`.
- Atub and Garakh were apparently intended to be merchants (apothecary and blacksmith respectively), but do not function as merchants themselves.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.5, addresses this issue. They were assigned the wrong settings. Once fixed, they will be affected by [Master Trader](/wiki/Skyrim:Master_Trader "Skyrim:Master Trader"), but not [Investor](/wiki/Skyrim:Investor "Skyrim:Investor").

# Skyrim:Largashbur

## Overview

Largashbur

**Largashbur** is an accursed [Orc stronghold](/wiki/Skyrim:Orc_Strongholds "Skyrim:Orc Strongholds") beset by [giants](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant "Skyrim:Giant") in the southeast of [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim"), west-southwest of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften").

The stronghold contains two zones: *[Largashbur Longhouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Largashbur_Longhouse "Skyrim:Largashbur Longhouse")* and *[Largashbur Cellar](/wiki/Skyrim:Largashbur_Cellar "Skyrim:Largashbur Cellar")*.

The stronghold features a makeshift altar to [Malacath](/wiki/Skyrim:Malacath "Skyrim:Malacath"), adorned with [Orcish Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Orcish_Armor "Skyrim:Orcish Armor"), [Orcish Boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Orcish_Boots "Skyrim:Orcish Boots"), an [Orcish Helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Orcish_Helmet "Skyrim:Orcish Helmet"), an [Orcish Shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Orcish_Shield "Skyrim:Orcish Shield"), an [Orcish Battleaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Orcish_Battleaxe "Skyrim:Orcish Battleaxe"), and seven bunches of [lavender](/wiki/Skyrim:Lavender "Skyrim:Lavender"). Largashbur is the only one of the four Orc strongholds not to have a mine, and indeed has lent two of its working-age Orcs to [Narzulbur](/wiki/Skyrim:Narzulbur "Skyrim:Narzulbur"), since Narzulbur has a mine but a shortage of workers.

As with all Orc Strongholds, you must become [Blood-Kin](/wiki/Skyrim:Blood-Kin "Skyrim:Blood-Kin") to the [Orcs](/wiki/Skyrim:Orc "Skyrim:Orc") before you are welcome in the stronghold and able to barter or receive other services.

## Largashbur Residents

|  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| | [Largashbur Longhouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Largashbur_Longhouse "Skyrim:Largashbur Longhouse") | | --- | | **[Chief Yamarz](/wiki/Skyrim:Chief_Yamarz "Skyrim:Chief Yamarz")**  **[Atub](/wiki/Skyrim:Atub "Skyrim:Atub")** [Trainer (Expert)](/wiki/Skyrim:Trainers "Trainer (Expert)")[Illusion (Expert)](/wiki/Skyrim:Illusion "Illusion (Expert)") **[Garakh](/wiki/Skyrim:Garakh "Skyrim:Garakh")**  **[Gularzob](/wiki/Skyrim:Gularzob "Skyrim:Gularzob")**  **[Lob](/wiki/Skyrim:Lob "Skyrim:Lob")** [Follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Follower") **[Ogol](/wiki/Skyrim:Ogol "Skyrim:Ogol")** [Follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Follower") **[Ugor](/wiki/Skyrim:Ugor "Skyrim:Ugor")** [Follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Follower") | | | Camp | | --- | | **[Unnamed Orcs](/wiki/Skyrim:Orc "Skyrim:Orc")** | |

#### Daedric

- **[The Cursed Tribe](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Cursed_Tribe "Skyrim:The Cursed Tribe")**: Help lift the curse placed on the [Orcs](/wiki/Skyrim:Orc "Skyrim:Orc") of Largashbur by [Malacath](/wiki/Lore:Malacath "Lore:Malacath").

### Exterior

Two [goats](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat "Skyrim:Goat") and a [horse](/wiki/Skyrim:Horse "Skyrim:Horse") are found in the exterior area.

### Buildings

- [Largashbur Longhouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Largashbur_Longhouse "Skyrim:Largashbur Longhouse") - Primary dwelling for all residents.
- [Largashbur Cellar](/wiki/Skyrim:Largashbur_Cellar "Skyrim:Largashbur Cellar") - Storage cellar and makeshift bar, with a few food barrels and sacks and a level-locked chest just outside the trapdoor entrance behind the longhouse.
- Apothecary's Shack - Exterior building with an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Lab "Skyrim:Alchemy Lab"), and a few ingredients on a set of shelves and hanging from a pole.
- Blacksmith's Shack - Exterior building with a [forge](/wiki/Skyrim:Forge "Skyrim:Forge"), a [workbench](/wiki/Skyrim:Workbench "Skyrim:Workbench"), and a [grindstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Grindstone "Skyrim:Grindstone"), and a few pieces of Orcish equipment on a set of shelves, a table, and a barrel.
- Tanner's Shed - Exterior building with a [tanning rack](/wiki/Skyrim:Tanning_Rack "Skyrim:Tanning Rack"), a food barrel, and a few pelts on a table.

## Notes

- [Lob](/wiki/Skyrim:Lob "Skyrim:Lob"), [Ogol](/wiki/Skyrim:Ogol "Skyrim:Ogol"), [Ugor](/wiki/Skyrim:Ugor "Skyrim:Ugor"), and the unnamed Orcs outside the stronghold are not essential, and can be easily killed by invading giants, even before you arrive.
- After completing [The Cursed Tribe](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Cursed_Tribe "Skyrim:The Cursed Tribe"), Lob, Ogol, and Ugor can be recruited as followers.

## Bugs

- Triggering combat here while the quest The Cursed Tribe is active can block quest progression.
  - The [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch"), version 1.1, fixes this bug.
- The giant will continue to respawn and attack the stronghold after the quest The Cursed Tribe has been completed, as the disable flag is not implemented. This can eventually result in the death of everyone within other than Atub.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.5, fixes this bug.
  -  The giant's attacks can be stopped by opening the console and entering the code `"000A0E72".disable`.
- Atub and Garakh were apparently intended to be merchants (apothecary and blacksmith respectively), but do not function as merchants themselves.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.5, addresses this issue. They were assigned the wrong settings. Once fixed, they will be affected by [Master Trader](/wiki/Skyrim:Master_Trader "Skyrim:Master Trader"), but not [Investor](/wiki/Skyrim:Investor "Skyrim:Investor").

# Skyrim:Last Vigil

## Overview

Last Vigil

**Last Vigil** is a small [camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Camps "Skyrim:Camps") northeast of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften").

Upon reaching level 80, you will be approached by the [Ebony Warrior](/wiki/Skyrim:Ebony_Warrior "Skyrim:Ebony Warrior"), who will challenge you to meet him at this location to battle him in a duel.

## Related Quests

- **[The Ebony Warrior](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ebony_Warrior "Skyrim:The Ebony Warrior")**: Locate and defeat the [Ebony Warrior](/wiki/Skyrim:Ebony_Warrior "Skyrim:Ebony Warrior").

## Walkthrough

The camp is high in the snowy [Velothi Mountains](/wiki/Skyrim:Velothi_Mountains "Skyrim:Velothi Mountains"). Several [ore veins](/wiki/Skyrim:Ores_and_Ingots "Skyrim:Ores and Ingots") are found along the path, which starts east of [Fort Greenwall](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Greenwall "Skyrim:Fort Greenwall").

The only distinguishable features of the camp are a collapsed tent and some skeletal remains. The camp contains a [pickaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe"), a [moonstone ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Moonstone_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Moonstone Ore Vein"), a [quicksilver ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Quicksilver_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Quicksilver Ore Vein"), and a copy of the [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[The Art of War Magic](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Art_of_War_Magic "Skyrim:The Art of War Magic")*. Before starting the quest [The Ebony Warrior](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ebony_Warrior "Skyrim:The Ebony Warrior"), the camp will be occupied by a single leveled [creature](/wiki/Skyrim:Creatures "Skyrim:Creatures"), which could be a [snow bear](/wiki/Skyrim:Snow_Bear "Skyrim:Snow Bear") or a [frost troll](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Troll "Skyrim:Frost Troll") at higher levels. After starting the quest, the camp will be occupied by the Ebony Warrior, with a dead frost troll nearby.

## Notes

- Along with the [Northern Maiden](/wiki/Skyrim:Northern_Maiden "Skyrim:Northern Maiden"), this is one of only two locations added by *[Dragonborn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn")* within [Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim_(place) "Skyrim:Skyrim (place)"), and the only discoverable one.
- On the local map, the location is called *Ebony Warrior's Camp*.

## Bugs

- The skill book may be inaccessible due to a texture glitch.
- The camp does not have its parent region set to [the Rift](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Rift "Skyrim:The Rift").
  -  The [Unofficial Dragonborn Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dragonborn_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dragonborn Patch"), version 2.1.1, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Left Hand Mine

## Overview

| --- | --- | --- | --- |

| Southeast of [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") South of [Salvius Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Salvius_Farm "Skyrim:Salvius Farm") | |

| # of [Smelters](/wiki/Skyrim:Smelter "Skyrim:Smelter") | 1 |

| [Ore Veins](/wiki/Skyrim:Mining "Skyrim:Mining") | |

Left Hand Mine

**Left Hand Mine** is a small [iron](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron "Skyrim:Iron") [mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Mines "Skyrim:Mines") and [settlement](/wiki/Skyrim:Settlements "Skyrim:Settlements") southeast of [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth"). The mine contains only one zone, *[Left Hand Mine](#Left_Hand_Mine)*; the settlement's residences are detailed on separate pages.

The mine is owned by [Skaggi Scar-Face](/wiki/Skyrim:Skaggi_Scar-Face "Skyrim:Skaggi Scar-Face"), who will [buy iron ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Mine_Ore "Skyrim:Mine Ore") from you.

## Left Hand Mine Residents

|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| | [Skaggi's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Skaggi%27s_House "Skyrim:Skaggi's House") | | --- | | **[Skaggi Scar-Face](/wiki/Skyrim:Skaggi_Scar-Face "Skyrim:Skaggi Scar-Face")**  **[Sosia Tremellia](/wiki/Skyrim:Sosia_Tremellia "Skyrim:Sosia Tremellia")** | | [Daighre's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Daighre%27s_House "Skyrim:Daighre's House") | | **[Daighre](/wiki/Skyrim:Daighre "Skyrim:Daighre")**  **[Erith](/wiki/Skyrim:Erith "Skyrim:Erith")**  **[Torom](/wiki/Skyrim:Torom "Skyrim:Torom")** ([dog](/wiki/Skyrim:Dog "Skyrim:Dog")) | | | [Miner's Barracks](/wiki/Skyrim:Left_Hand_Miner%27s_Barracks "Skyrim:Left Hand Miner's Barracks") | | --- | | **[Adeber](/wiki/Skyrim:Adeber "Skyrim:Adeber")**  **[Ennoc](/wiki/Skyrim:Ennoc "Skyrim:Ennoc")**  **[Willem](/wiki/Skyrim:Willem "Skyrim:Willem")** | | | Others | | --- | | **[Gat gro-Shargakh](/wiki/Skyrim:Gat_gro-Shargakh "Skyrim:Gat gro-Shargakh")** \* **[Pavo Attius](/wiki/Skyrim:Pavo_Attius "Skyrim:Pavo Attius")** \* **[Reach Hold Guard](/wiki/Skyrim:Reach_Hold_Guard "Skyrim:Reach Hold Guard")** | |

\* Relocate to [Kolskeggr Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Kolskeggr_Mine "Skyrim:Kolskeggr Mine") after the quest [Kolskeggr Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Kolskeggr_Mine_(quest) "Skyrim:Kolskeggr Mine (quest)").

## Related Quests

- **[Kolskeggr Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Kolskeggr_Mine_(quest) "Skyrim:Kolskeggr Mine (quest)")**: Clear the [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn") from [Kolskeggr Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Kolskeggr_Mine "Skyrim:Kolskeggr Mine").
- **[Mine Ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Mine_Ore "Skyrim:Mine Ore")**: Get paid to [mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Mining "Skyrim:Mining") ore. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

### Exterior

Before crossing the stone bridge to the mining settlement, a [rock warbler egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Rock_Warbler_Egg "Skyrim:Rock Warbler Egg") is on the ground to the left. Another is across the bridge to the right. The three buildings that make up the settlement feature the [Dwemer](/wiki/Lore:Dwemer "Lore:Dwemer") architecture of nearby Markarth. [Daighre's house](/wiki/Skyrim:Daighre%27s_House "Skyrim:Daighre's House") and [Skaggi's house](/wiki/Skyrim:Skaggi%27s_House "Skyrim:Skaggi's House") are on the east side. Opposite the houses to the west is the [Miner's Barracks](/wiki/Skyrim:Left_Hand_Miner%27s_Barracks "Skyrim:Left Hand Miner's Barracks"); with *[Hearthfire](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire")* installed, a [stone quarry](/wiki/Skyrim:Stone_Quarry "Skyrim:Stone Quarry") is behind the barracks. A [goat](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat "Skyrim:Goat") and some [chickens](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken "Skyrim:Chicken") wander the settlement, and outside the barracks are two [chicken eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken%27s_Egg "Skyrim:Chicken's Egg"). The settlement initially shelters two refugees from [Kolskeggr Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Kolskeggr_Mine "Skyrim:Kolskeggr Mine") who were displaced by [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn"). Talking to them or Skaggi triggers the [quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Kolskeggr_Mine_(quest) "Skyrim:Kolskeggr Mine (quest)") to reclaim Kolskeggr Mine.

A [smelter](/wiki/Skyrim:Smelter "Skyrim:Smelter") and four pieces of [iron ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore "Skyrim:Iron Ore") on a crate are near the mine entrance in the southwestern corner of the settlement.

### Left Hand Mine

The entry tunnel goes down past a small side shaft on the right. A few specimens of [white cap](/wiki/Skyrim:White_Cap "Skyrim:White Cap"), [imp stool](/wiki/Skyrim:Imp_Stool "Skyrim:Imp Stool"), and [bleeding crown](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleeding_Crown "Skyrim:Bleeding Crown") grow at the mouth of this small shaft. The first of five iron ore veins is found there. The table ahead holds two [pickaxes](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe"). More white caps grow behind the empty barrels to the right of the table.

A crosscut divides the mine into east and west. The shaft to the west has three pairs of [iron boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Boots "Skyrim:Iron Boots") next to the shelves and three more pickaxes. On the ground is a basket holding six [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead") bottles and a [knapsack](/wiki/Skyrim:Knapsack "Skyrim:Knapsack") containing a potion and a random piece of [jewelry](/wiki/Skyrim:Jewelry "Skyrim:Jewelry"). The end of the shaft widens, and there are two iron ore veins, one to the west and one to the east.

To continue to the other end of the crosscut, the shaft to the east has a small table with an [iron helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Helmet "Skyrim:Iron Helmet"). Strangely, two [red mountain flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Red Mountain Flower") plants are growing here; one on the left side of the shaft and the other under the scaffolding ahead. When the shaft opens up, an iron ore vein is found to the east just before the scaffolding. There are several [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") sacks in this area. The final iron ore vein is on the north wall accessed from the platform at the top of the scaffolding. A small table on the platform has some loose gold coins, with a pair of [leather boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Boots "Skyrim:Leather Boots") by the table.

## Maps

- 

  Left Hand Mine

## Notes

- If Hearthfire is installed, you won't be able to tell your carriage driver at your house to take you here.

# Skyrim:Left Hand Miner's Barracks

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This article is being developed as part of the Skyrim Houses Redesign Project. If you see this tag it means the article can still be improved. Please see the [project page](/wiki/UESPWiki:SHRP "UESPWiki:SHRP") for guidelines.** |

| Console Location Code(s) | |

| [The Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Reach "Skyrim:The Reach") | |
| Location | |
| Near the [Left Hand Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Left_Hand_Mine "Skyrim:Left Hand Mine") | |

Miner's Barracks

**Left Hand Miner's Barracks** is the collective housing area for several miners who work in the [Left Hand Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Left_Hand_Mine "Skyrim:Left Hand Mine").

It is the home of three of the miners from [Left Hand Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Left_Hand_Mine "Skyrim:Left Hand Mine"), [Adeber](/wiki/Skyrim:Adeber "Skyrim:Adeber"), [Ennoc](/wiki/Skyrim:Ennoc "Skyrim:Ennoc") and [Willem](/wiki/Skyrim:Willem "Skyrim:Willem"). It consists of one area only, *[Miner's Barracks](#Miner.27s_Barracks)*

Before the quest [Kolskeggr Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Kolskeggr_Mine_(quest) "Skyrim:Kolskeggr Mine (quest)") is completed, two refugees will also live in the barracks, namely [Pavo Attius](/wiki/Skyrim:Pavo_Attius "Skyrim:Pavo Attius") and [Gat gro-Shargakh](/wiki/Skyrim:Gat_gro-Shargakh "Skyrim:Gat gro-Shargakh").

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Adeber](/wiki/Skyrim:Adeber "Skyrim:Adeber")  [Ennoc](/wiki/Skyrim:Ennoc "Skyrim:Ennoc")  [Willem](/wiki/Skyrim:Willem "Skyrim:Willem") |

## Miner's Barracks

The Barracks Interior

The barracks are obviously only used for sleeping and are pretty much empty, save for a table with three bottles of [ale](/wiki/Skyrim:Ale "Skyrim:Ale") and a basket with a [goat cheese wheel](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wheel") and some [sliced goat cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Sliced_Goat_Cheese "Skyrim:Sliced Goat Cheese"). There are two bedrolls on the floor and, along the western wall, a bed with a belongings chest with minor loot and a bucket with three samples of [iron ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore "Skyrim:Iron Ore"). All items are free to take and the beds are free to sleep in.

# Skyrim:Legends Lost

## Overview

|  |
