| Added by: | [Sunder & Wraithguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Sunder_%26_Wraithguard "Skyrim:Sunder & Wraithguard") |

Follow the trail of long-dead smugglers

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Go to [New Gnisis Cornerclub](/wiki/Skyrim:New_Gnisis_Cornerclub "Skyrim:New Gnisis Cornerclub") and read the *[Lost Caravan Guard's Note](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_Caravan_Guard%27s_Note "Skyrim:Lost Caravan Guard's Note")*.
2. Locate the lost caravan north of [Bronze Water Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Bronze_Water_Cave "Skyrim:Bronze Water Cave") and read the *[Carriage Driver's Note](/wiki/Skyrim:Carriage_Driver%27s_Note "Skyrim:Carriage Driver's Note")*.
3. Locate the lost caravan east of [Loreius Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Loreius_Farm "Skyrim:Loreius Farm") and read the *[Seedy Guard's Note](/wiki/Skyrim:Seedy_Guard%27s_Note "Skyrim:Seedy Guard's Note")*.
4. Enter [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun")'s [Hall of the Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_the_Dead_(Whiterun) "Skyrim:Hall of the Dead (Whiterun)") and read the *[Caravan Captain's Note](/wiki/Skyrim:Caravan_Captain%27s_Note "Skyrim:Caravan Captain's Note")*.
5. Locate the final caravan northwest of [Peak's Shade Tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Peak%27s_Shade_Tower "Skyrim:Peak's Shade Tower") and read *[Velyne's Letter](/wiki/Skyrim:Velyne%27s_Letter "Skyrim:Velyne's Letter")*.
6. Loot the [Attunement Crystal](/w/index.php?title=Skyrim:Attunement_Crystal&action=edit&redlink=1 "Skyrim:Attunement Crystal (page does not exist)") and journey to [Sightless Pit](/wiki/Skyrim:Sightless_Pit "Skyrim:Sightless Pit").
7. Explore Sightless Pit and use the Attunement Crystal to unlock the entrance to the Sightless Vault near the dungeon exit.
8. Solve the steam valve puzzles and defeat [the Messenger](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Messenger "Skyrim:The Messenger") to claim [Sunder](/wiki/Skyrim:Sunder "Skyrim:Sunder") and [Wraithguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Wraithguard "Skyrim:Wraithguard") as your own.

### Letters from the Red Year

Upon installing the [Sunder & Wraithguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Sunder_%26_Wraithguard "Skyrim:Sunder & Wraithguard") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club"), you will be directed to the [New Gnisis Cornerclub](/wiki/Skyrim:New_Gnisis_Cornerclub "Skyrim:New Gnisis Cornerclub") in [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") in relation to a trove of old refugee letters from the [Red Year](/wiki/Lore:Red_Year "Lore:Red Year") which have recently been uncovered. On the bar top is a *[Lost Caravan Guard's Note](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_Caravan_Guard%27s_Note "Skyrim:Lost Caravan Guard's Note")*, which can be freely taken. Reading this note will reveal that a highly secretive smuggling operation had been organized to transport some unknown cargo through Skyrim, using the refugees fleeing [Morrowind](/wiki/Lore:Morrowind "Lore:Morrowind") as cover. Several decoy caravans were employed to transport this cargo, each with a code name based on the [Great Houses](/wiki/Lore:Great_Houses "Lore:Great Houses") of Morrowind.

The author of this letter was part of the Telvanni caravan, and was reportedly carrying the cargo towards the [Nightgate Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightgate_Inn "Skyrim:Nightgate Inn"). The destroyed remains of this caravan are half-buried in snow along the road between Windhelm and the inn, just north of the entrance to [Bronze Water Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Bronze_Water_Cave "Skyrim:Bronze Water Cave"). Several destroyed [Dwarven automatons](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Automatons "Skyrim:Dwarven Automatons") surround the carriage, along with the skeletons of the unfortunate caravaneers. Unfortunately, the elusive cargo is nowhere to be found, although there is a *[Carriage Driver's Note](/wiki/Skyrim:Carriage_Driver%27s_Note "Skyrim:Carriage Driver's Note")* in an "Old Caravan Chest" at the wreckage. The author of this note complains of attacks from Dwarven automatons as well as "singing" coming from the cargo. It also reveals that the items were handed off to the Sadras caravan, which was heading for [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun").

(If [Saints and Seducers](/wiki/Skyrim:Saints_%26_Seducers "Skyrim:Saints & Seducers")[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") is also installed, the first caravan is located right next to [Svarig's](/wiki/Skyrim:Svarig "Skyrim:Svarig") Dark Seducer camp and can be discovered before starting this quest. Reading the Carriage Driver's Note without going to the cornerclub will start the quest and direct you to the next caravan with no context.)

The next ruined caravan is just off the road east of [Loreius Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Loreius_Farm "Skyrim:Loreius Farm"). You will be greeted by a familiar scene of Dwarven machines and skeletal corpses. One such skeleton can be found holding the *[Seedy Guard's Note](/wiki/Skyrim:Seedy_Guard%27s_Note "Skyrim:Seedy Guard's Note")*, which reveals that the cargo had been handed over to the Indoril caravan and that its captain was planning to stop by the [Hall of the Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_the_Dead_(Whiterun) "Skyrim:Hall of the Dead (Whiterun)") in Whiterun. Be sure to loot the nearby Old Caravan Chest for valuables, then make your way to Whiterun.

### The Plot Thickens

You will need to enter the Whiterun Catacombs once you arrive at the Hall of the Dead. This area is infested with low level undead [skeletons](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton"). Down the first set of stairs, you will find the *[Caravan Captain's Note](/wiki/Skyrim:Caravan_Captain%27s_Note "Skyrim:Caravan Captain's Note")* atop a low-lying table. According to the note, the surviving caravans took a detour towards [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath") to avoid any further Dwemer attacks. You will find their remains at a ruined campsite in the woods northwest of [Peak's Shade Tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Peak%27s_Shade_Tower "Skyrim:Peak's Shade Tower"). One of the skeletons is in fact the body of Velyne, a member of the Hlaalu caravan and seemingly one of the masterminds behind this venture. *[Velyne's Letter](/wiki/Skyrim:Velyne%27s_Letter "Skyrim:Velyne's Letter")* at last reveals that the secretive cargo is actually [Sunder](/wiki/Skyrim:Sunder "Skyrim:Sunder") and [Wraithguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Wraithguard "Skyrim:Wraithguard"), and that the Dwemer automaton attacks are the result of a fail-safe system implemented by [Kagrenac](/wiki/Lore:Kagrenac "Lore:Kagrenac") to prevent his Tools from ever leaving Morrowind. The Dwemer created a Tamriel-wide network of drones which would track down and retrieve the Tools if they were taken out of Morrowind, and would then deposit them in a vault until a Tonal Architect could come and retrieve them. Seeking to put a stop to the attacks, some of the caravan captains betrayed their employers and handed Sunder and Wraithguard over to the drones. Velyne learned of this, and managed to track the items to a vault located in [Sightless Pit](/wiki/Skyrim:Sightless_Pit "Skyrim:Sightless Pit"). She obtained a [Attunement Crystal](/w/index.php?title=Skyrim:Attunement_Crystal&action=edit&redlink=1 "Skyrim:Attunement Crystal (page does not exist)") to unseal this vault, but evidently died before an expedition could ever be organized. Take the crystal from her skeleton and be sure to loot the Old Caravan Chest before you leave.

Use the Attunement Crystal to unlock the Sightless Vault

Steam will need to be restored to both valve systems

The Tools

### Hidden Depository

Sightless Pit is a [Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer "Skyrim:Falmer")-infested dungeon in the snowy wastes southwest of [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold "Skyrim:Winterhold"). Unlike most dungeons in the game, the entrance to Sightless Pit is one-way, meaning you will need to fight your way through the entire complex in order to escape. See the [dungeon walkthrough](/wiki/Skyrim:Sightless_Pit#Walkthrough "Skyrim:Sightless Pit") for more information. Your goal is to reach the final zone, [Abandoned Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Sightless_Pit#Abandoned_Cave "Skyrim:Sightless Pit"). A new door has been added by this Creation, to the right of the lift as you enter the zone. Place the Attunement Crystal on the Dwarven Pedestal to unseal the entrance to the Sightless Vault. This is a new area added by the Creation and consists of a large central room with two side areas. Sunder and Wraithguard are locked behind gates in the center of the room and cannot be reached.

To begin unlocking the gates, you must first activate a Vault Release Valve at the back of the room. You must then solve two steam valve puzzles in the two side rooms, which will involve activating each valve several times until the steam travels in the right direction. Your goal is to direct the steam in the direction of the next valve, until you reach the end of the piping and your journal updates. You will need to fight two [Dwarven Spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Spider "Skyrim:Dwarven Spider") and two [Dwarven Spheres](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Sphere "Skyrim:Dwarven Sphere") respectively after you solve each room. With this done, the door near the original Vault Release Valve will open and an extremely powerful ebony-colored [Dwarven Centurion](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Centurion "Skyrim:Dwarven Centurion") named [the Messenger](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Messenger "Skyrim:The Messenger") will emerge.

Once you defeat this final guardian, the gates will swing open and Sunder and Wraithguard are yours to claim. On its own, Sunder does 5 points of frost, fire, and shock damage each and 15 points of damage to stamina and magicka. With Wraithguard equipped, Sunder becomes a powerful weapon, although unlike its [initial appearance](/wiki/Morrowind:Sunder "Morrowind:Sunder") in [*Morrowind*](/wiki/Morrowind:Morrowind "Morrowind:Morrowind") it will not kill you if you equip the weapon without wearing Wraithguard. Wraithguard also provides 10% resistance to shock, fire, frost, magic, disease, and poison when worn. If you've already completed [Arniel's Endeavor](/wiki/Skyrim:Arniel%27s_Endeavor "Skyrim:Arniel's Endeavor"), you will have come into possession of [Keening](/wiki/Skyrim:Keening "Skyrim:Keening"), another of Kagrenac's Tools. Keening is also empowered if wielded while Wraithguard is equipped, and it can be dual wielded along with Sunder. Before you depart, make sure you loot the chest in the room where the Messenger emerged from.

## Bugs

- The Lost Caravan Guard's Note frequently falls through the top of the bar to the shelf below, making it difficult to find.
- Upon purchasing the Sunder and Wraithguard creation, the quest may not activate causing the Attunement Crystal to not spawn.
- If you read the Carriage Driver's Note then take it, the quest may not advance. You should take it first, then read it from your inventory. **?**
- If you leave the Sightless Pit without completing the vault puzzle, you may lose the Attunement Crystal and be unable to complete the quest.
- If you only obtained one item and receive the quest again, [the Messenger](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Messenger "Skyrim:The Messenger") will not respawn even if you perform all the steps necessary to encounter it. The doors to the vault will remain inoperable and leave the quest unable to be completed.
- If you read [Velyne's Letter](/wiki/Skyrim:Velyne%27s_Letter "Skyrim:Velyne's Letter") before picking it up, you will be given the objective to "Read Velyne's Letter" but be unable to complete it.
- If one activates the Messenger release valve and quickly hides in one of the side rooms, the Messenger will not respond to attacks and can be killed easily

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage ccBGSSSE008_Quest stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest ccBGSSSE008_Quest`.

# Skyrim:Leigelf's House

## Overview

Leigelf's House in Dawnstar

**Leigelf's House** is the residence of [Leigelf](/wiki/Skyrim:Leigelf "Skyrim:Leigelf") in the center of [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar"), next to the blacksmith.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Leigelf](/wiki/Skyrim:Leigelf "Skyrim:Leigelf") |

## Related Quests

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

### Exterior

There are a few steps up to a porch on the front of the house, on the porch are two [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") barrels and a wooden bench at one end and several piles of firewood at the other. The house faces the bay and is novice-locked the majority of the time.

### Leigelf's House

Leigelf's house

This is another single-room home, on your left upon entering is a set of shelves holding two [leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Leek "Skyrim:Leek"), a [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") bulb, three [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato") and has several pieces of cheese on top. Above are two garlic braids, three bunches of [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear") and a bunch of [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam"). To the left is a basket on the floor containing two leeks and to the right is a food barrel. In the middle of the east wall and coming out from the wall is a large double bed with an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") at the foot of it. On the floor to the left of the bed are four bottles of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"). To the right of the bed is a table holding a bottle of [Black-Briar mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Black-Briar_Mead "Skyrim:Black-Briar Mead") and six loose [coins](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold").

The fireplace is in the middle of the south wall, opposite the door and has a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") in front of it, a [steel sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Sword "Skyrim:Steel Sword") on the mantelpiece and a [pickaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe") on the hearth. To the left is a hanging rack holding three [rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)") and to the left of these is a wardrobe containing [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes "Skyrim:Clothes"). To the right of the fireplace is a long wooden table still against the south wall. On the table is a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), three [sweet rolls](/wiki/Skyrim:Sweet_Roll "Skyrim:Sweet Roll"), several loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), a [cabbage](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage") and an [eidar cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wedge").

In the northwestern corner is a square wooden table and two chairs. On the table are three bottles of Nord mead, a pickaxe, five loose coins and a medium [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse").

## Notes

- The *[Prima Official Game Guide](/wiki/Books:The_Elder_Scrolls_V:_Skyrim:_Prima_Official_Game_Guide "Books:The Elder Scrolls V: Skyrim: Prima Official Game Guide")* describes the building as follows:

:   *"Because Leigelf manages Quicksilver Mine and spends most of his time obsessing about his work and his wife, his living arrangements are somewhat sparse."*

# Skyrim:Lemkil's Farmhouse

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This article is being developed as part of the Skyrim Houses Redesign Project. If you see this tag it means the article can still be improved. Please see the [project page](/wiki/UESPWiki:SHRP "UESPWiki:SHRP") for guidelines.** |

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Farm: Lemkil's Farmhouse ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Lemkil%27s+Farmhouse)) | | |
| # of Zones | 1 |

| Console Location Code(s) | |
| RoriksteadLemkilsFarm | |
| Region | |
| [Whiterun Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Hold "Skyrim:Whiterun Hold") | |
| Location | |
| [Rorikstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Rorikstead "Skyrim:Rorikstead") | |
| Special Features | |
| # of [Cooking Pots/Spits](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking "Skyrim:Cooking") | 1 |
| # of [Stone Quarries](/wiki/Skyrim:Quarried_Stone "Skyrim:Quarried Stone")[HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") | 1 |

Lemkil's Farmhouse

**Lemkil's Farmhouse** is a small farm in [Rorikstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Rorikstead "Skyrim:Rorikstead").

It is home to the widower [Lemkil](/wiki/Skyrim:Lemkil "Skyrim:Lemkil") and his twin daughters, [Britte](/wiki/Skyrim:Britte "Skyrim:Britte") and [Sissel](/wiki/Skyrim:Sissel "Skyrim:Sissel"), with the former being the older twin. The farmstead is at the eastern end of Rorikstead, along the road that passes through the village. Opposite [Cowflop Farmhouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Cowflop_Farmhouse "Skyrim:Cowflop Farmhouse").
The three family members make a point of spending as little time together as possible. When they wake at 6am they all leave the house; Lemkil only returns to sleep at 10pm after spending his evenings in the [inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostfruit_Inn "Skyrim:Frostfruit Inn"), while [Sissel](/wiki/Skyrim:Sissel "Skyrim:Sissel") spends part of her evening at [Rorik's Manor](/wiki/Skyrim:Rorik%27s_Manor "Skyrim:Rorik's Manor") learning magic, returning only to sleep. [Britte](/wiki/Skyrim:Britte "Skyrim:Britte") has nowhere to go, but has the house to herself in the evenings, going to bed at midnight.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Britte](/wiki/Skyrim:Britte "Skyrim:Britte")  [Lemkil](/wiki/Skyrim:Lemkil "Skyrim:Lemkil")  [Sissel](/wiki/Skyrim:Sissel "Skyrim:Sissel") |

## Related Quests

- **[Gather Wheat](/wiki/Skyrim:Gather_Wheat "Skyrim:Gather Wheat")**: Get paid to gather crops. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

### Exterior

There is a [lavender](/wiki/Skyrim:Lavender "Skyrim:Lavender") plant beside the wooden steps that lead up to the entrance. It is a modest single story building, with a small field to the east, where [Lemkil](/wiki/Skyrim:Lemkil "Skyrim:Lemkil") grows twenty-five [cabbages](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage"), eight [leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Leek "Skyrim:Leek") and thirteen [potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato") plants.

| Crops | Plants |
| --- | --- |
| 25 [Cabbage](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage")  8 [Leek](/wiki/Skyrim:Leek "Skyrim:Leek")  13 [Potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato") | 1 [Lavender](/wiki/Skyrim:Lavender "Skyrim:Lavender") |

### Lemkil's Farmhouse

The front door is normally locked, with a novice level lock. Upon entering there is a chair and barrels against the northeast wall. Further around against the southwest wall is a cupboard holding clutter and beside this are several more [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") barrels. There is a long wooden table and bench against the southwest wall. On the table is a flower basket containing two [chicken's eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken%27s_Egg "Skyrim:Chicken's Egg"), a bucket containing three [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato") and a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"). Above the table are three [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") braids, a bunch of [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam") and two bunches of [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear"), with a rack hanging to the right holding three [rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)") and three [pheasants](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant "Skyrim:Pheasant"). To the right of the table is a food barrel and a flower basket containing four [pine thrush eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Pine_Thrush_Egg "Skyrim:Pine Thrush Egg"). Beside these is an owned single bed coming out from the southwest wall, where Lemkil sleeps. At the foot of the bed is an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") containing minor loot. Further along the southwest wall is a fireplace with a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") and table and two chairs in front. On the table is a bottle of alto wine, a couple of loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread") and a pine thrush egg. By the hearth is a kettle containing two [leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Leek "Skyrim:Leek").

At the northwest end of the room are two owned single beds both coming out from the northwest wall where the twins sleep, with an end table between them. On the end table are two [sweet rolls](/wiki/Skyrim:Sweet_Roll "Skyrim:Sweet Roll") and a [flute](/wiki/Skyrim:Flute "Skyrim:Flute"), with a [lute](/wiki/Skyrim:Lute "Skyrim:Lute") leaning against it. To the right, against the southeast wall is a wardrobe containing [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes "Skyrim:Clothes") and to the right a dresser with three garlic braids, two bunches of elves ear and a bunch of frost mirriam hanging from the ceiling above. On the dresser is a bottle of [Black-Briar mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Black-Briar_Mead "Skyrim:Black-Briar Mead"), four bulbs of garlic, a bunch of frost mirriam and a bunch of elves ear.

## Notes

- A [grain mill](/wiki/Skyrim:Milling "Skyrim:Milling") can be found here, which can be used to produce [flour](/wiki/Skyrim:Sack_of_Flour "Skyrim:Sack of Flour")[HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") from [wheat](/wiki/Skyrim:Wheat "Skyrim:Wheat") if [Hearthfire](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") is installed. Installing Hearthfire also adds a [stone quarry](/wiki/Skyrim:Quarried_Stone "Skyrim:Quarried Stone") behind the vegetable garden.
- The [key to the house](/wiki/Skyrim:Lemkil%27s_House_Key "Skyrim:Lemkil's House Key") is carried by all three members of the family.

## Bugs

- None of the inhabitants here own the beds assigned to them. **?**

# Skyrim:Let Sleeping Wolves Lie

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png) | **Stop a necromancer from raising undead wolf minions.** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | Reading the *[Letter from Bolgeir Bearclaw](/wiki/Skyrim:Letter_from_Bolgeir_Bearclaw "Skyrim:Letter from Bolgeir Bearclaw")* delivered by courier after completion of [The Wolf Queen Awakened](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Wolf_Queen_Awakened "Skyrim:The Wolf Queen Awakened") |
| Location(s): | Necromancer's camp northwest of [Folgunthur](/wiki/Skyrim:Folgunthur "Skyrim:Folgunthur") |
| Reward: | Pet [Bone Wolf](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Wolf_(creature) "Skyrim:Bone Wolf (creature)") |
| ID: | ccBGSSSE036\_PetBWolfAcquisitionQuest |
| Added by: | [Bone Wolf](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Wolf "Skyrim:Bone Wolf") |
| --- | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | **← Previous** [The Wolf Queen Awakened](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Wolf_Queen_Awakened "Skyrim:The Wolf Queen Awakened") |  | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | ← Previous | [The Wolf Queen Awakened](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Wolf_Queen_Awakened "Skyrim:The Wolf Queen Awakened") | | |

A necromancer has been raising wolves and terrorizing locals

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Read the [*Letter from Bolgeir Bearclaw*](/wiki/Skyrim:Letter_from_Bolgeir_Bearclaw "Skyrim:Letter from Bolgeir Bearclaw").
2. Locate the necromancer northwest of [Folgunthur](/wiki/Skyrim:Folgunthur "Skyrim:Folgunthur") and read his [journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Necromancer%27s_Journal_(Bone_Wolf) "Skyrim:Necromancer's Journal (Bone Wolf)").
3. Bring the [Totem Bone](/wiki/Skyrim:Totem_Bone "Skyrim:Totem Bone") to the caged [Bone Wolf](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Wolf_(creature) "Skyrim:Bone Wolf (creature)") nearby to complete the quest.

## Detailed Walkthrough

An undead pet

### Solitude Calls for Aid

Once [The Wolf Queen Awakened](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Wolf_Queen_Awakened "Skyrim:The Wolf Queen Awakened") has been completed, a [courier](/wiki/Skyrim:Courier "Skyrim:Courier") will give you a [letter](/wiki/Skyrim:Letter_from_Bolgeir_Bearclaw "Skyrim:Letter from Bolgeir Bearclaw") from [Bolgeir Bearclaw](/wiki/Skyrim:Bolgeir_Bearclaw "Skyrim:Bolgeir Bearclaw"). After reading the note, you will be directed to a rocky overhang located along the coast northwest of [Folgunthur](/wiki/Skyrim:Folgunthur "Skyrim:Folgunthur"), just across the bay from the [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") docks. A hostile [necromancer](/wiki/Skyrim:Necromancer "Skyrim:Necromancer") has set up camp underneath the outcrop. His camp is guarded by two hostile [thrall wolves](/wiki/Skyrim:Thrall_Wolf "Skyrim:Thrall Wolf") and [werewolf pelts](/wiki/Skyrim:Werewolf_Pelt "Skyrim:Werewolf Pelt") can be found scattered all over. The necromancer will also likely resurrect the nearby dead [wolf](/wiki/Skyrim:Wolf "Skyrim:Wolf") so be prepared to face multiple enemies.

Once you have defeated the hostiles, search the necromancer to obtain his [journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Necromancer%27s_Journal_(Bone_Wolf) "Skyrim:Necromancer's Journal (Bone Wolf)"), along with a [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Wolf_Cage "Skyrim:Key to Wolf Cage") and a bloody [Totem Bone](/wiki/Skyrim:Totem_Bone "Skyrim:Totem Bone"). The key can be used to unlock the nearby cage which contains a non-hostile [Bone Wolf](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Wolf_(creature) "Skyrim:Bone Wolf (creature)"). The necromancer had not yet completed the ritual to bind the wolf to his will and it will be quite happy to have its bone back.

The quest will then conclude and you can ask the Bone Wolf to follow you. It serves as a pet, meaning it will not fight enemies but can be used to carry items. While following you, the Bone Wolf will grant you a perk buffing the damage you do to [undead](/wiki/Skyrim:Undead "Skyrim:Undead") enemies. It can also be told to wait at a city, wait at its current location (either temporarily or permanently), or wait at your house.

## Notes

- Bone Wolves previously [appeared](/wiki/Bloodmoon:Bonewolf "Bloodmoon:Bonewolf") in the [*Bloodmoon*](/wiki/Bloodmoon:Bloodmoon "Bloodmoon:Bloodmoon") expansion for [*TES III: Morrowind*](/wiki/Morrowind:Morrowind "Morrowind:Morrowind"), where they could regularly be encountered alongside [draugr](/wiki/Bloodmoon:Draugr "Bloodmoon:Draugr").
- The quest name is a reference to the phrase "let sleeping dogs lie".
- At release, the note from Bolgeir Bearclaw was added to your inventory automatically upon installing the [Bone Wolf](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Wolf "Skyrim:Bone Wolf") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club"), or as soon as you left [Helgen Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgen_Keep "Skyrim:Helgen Keep") as a new character. This was changed in the [Anniversary Edition](/wiki/Skyrim:Anniversary_Edition "Skyrim:Anniversary Edition").

## Bugs

- Sometimes the courier never arrives with the letter to start the quest.
  - You may be able to skip the letter and obtain the quest by simply going to the area the letter tells you to go to. Northwest of Folgunthur are a pair of stone obelisks that will activate the quest when approached.
  -  You can use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to add the letter to your inventory by entering `player.additem FExxx808 1`. Reading the letter will start the quest.
- Sometimes the Necromancer and the Bone wolf won't spawn at their location, despite having read the letter and being told to find them. This happens because stage 5 isn't properly completed, the quest jumps directly to stage 10.
  -  Entering `Setstage ccBGSSSE036_PetBWolfAcquisitionQuest 5` in the console will let them appear, and the quest will progress normally.

## Quest Stages

| Let Sleeping Wolves Lie (ccBGSSSE036\_PetBWolfAcquisitionQuest) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 5 |  | I have a note from Bolgeir Bearclaw. I should read it and find out if there's anything he needs assistance with. *Objective :* Read the note from Bolgeir Bearclaw |
| 10 |  | Bolgeir Bearclaw has informed me that a dark necromancer has been attacking innocents somewhere along the northern coast. The note also tells of strange creatures that accompany him. I should search the coast and see if I can unravel this mystery. *Objective :* Find the necromancer and the strange creatures |
| 15 |  | I have encountered a dark necromancer and two undead wolves. These creatures appear to be controlled by the necromancer. Putting a stop to these experiments should prevent him from raising more. *Objective :* Defeat the necromancer |
| 20 |  | I have discovered the necromancer's location. The strange creatures mentioned in the note appear to be undead wolves, raised by the dark arts of the necromancer. Putting a stop to these experiments should prevent him from raising more. *Objective :* Defeat the necromancer |
| 30 |  | The necromancer is dead. I should search his body for any clues. *Objective :* Search the necromancer |
| 40 |  | In a cage nearby, there is another of these strange creatures, who I suspect the totem belongs to. I should take it to him. *Objective :* Take the totem to the caged wolf |
| 60 | ☑ | Bone Wolf appears calm and content now that I've returned his totem. It appears he will follow me if I wish. Some may consider him strange to look upon, but there may be something deeper about him beyond his appearance. |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 50.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage ccBGSSSE036_PetBWolfAcquisitionQuest stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest ccBGSSSE036_PetBWolfAcquisitionQuest`.

# Skyrim:Liar's Retreat (quest)

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This page is currently being rewritten as part of the [Skyrim Quest Redesign Project](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").** The page is being rewritten and checked in several stages. All users are welcome to make changes to the page. If you make a change that is relevant to the project, please update this template accordingly, and make sure you have observed the [project guidelines](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project#Guidelines "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").  Details  **Walkthrough**: written by [Krusty](/wiki/User:Krusty "User:Krusty"), *not checked*  **Reward**: written by [Krusty](/wiki/User:Krusty "User:Krusty"), *not checked* |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Retrieve [the Longhammer](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Longhammer "Skyrim:The Longhammer") from a fallen [bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Rahd "Skyrim:Rahd").** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Location(s): | [Liar's Retreat](/wiki/Skyrim:Liar%27s_Retreat "Skyrim:Liar's Retreat") |
| Reward: | [The Longhammer](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Longhammer "Skyrim:The Longhammer") |
| ID: | dunLiarsRetreatQST |
| Suggested Level: | 18 |

Invasion of the [Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer "Skyrim:Falmer")

## Quick Walkthrough

**Note**: This quest does not appear in your journal.

1. Investigate what happened at [Liar's Retreat](/wiki/Skyrim:Liar%27s_Retreat "Skyrim:Liar's Retreat").
2. Discover the [Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer "Skyrim:Falmer") nest.
3. Find [Rahd](/wiki/Skyrim:Rahd "Skyrim:Rahd") and claim his [Longhammer](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Longhammer "Skyrim:The Longhammer").
4. Take the blame for the Falmer attack.

### A Falmer Invasion

This party is over

Liar's Retreat is a remote [bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") cave in the mountains between [Karthwasten](/wiki/Skyrim:Karthwasten "Skyrim:Karthwasten") and [Cliffside Retreat](/wiki/Skyrim:Cliffside_Retreat "Skyrim:Cliffside Retreat"), a long distance southwest from [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"). The peaceful exterior resembles a normal bandit hideout, but as you enter you will quickly realize that the human inhabitants got more than they bargained for when they moved in. From a small pedestal near the entrance door, you will witness several intruding [Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer "Skyrim:Falmer") battling the bandits, and emerging victorious. After passing over the bloodbath, you'll find more dead bandits everywhere, suggesting that you might best prepare yourself for a huge wave of attacking Falmer as you slowly crawl down to a homemade tavern, now soaked in blood. Fight all the Falmer and take a look around; the deceased bartender lies behind the bar, wearing the semi-rare [tavern clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#000d191f "Skyrim:Clothing"), and a slaughtered bandit [bard](/wiki/Skyrim:Bard "Skyrim:Bard") poignantly clutches his [lute](/wiki/Skyrim:Lute "Skyrim:Lute").

Take the northwestern exit and start investigating the private chambers; a cowardly bandit has barricaded the southernmost room and guards some minor loot there from within. The next blood-soaked room contains more dead bodies, while the third room holds a locked chest containing more minor loot. Head east and you will find yourself in the kitchen behind the bar, where plenty of ingredients and potions can be gathered. Backtrack a bit and notice the hole in the wall leading into a Falmer den—the Falmer seemingly broke through at this point to ambush the bandits.

### Claim the Longhammer

A [sacrifice](/wiki/Skyrim:Rahd "Skyrim:Rahd") for the [reaper](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus_Reaper "Skyrim:Chaurus Reaper")

Head into the bluish-tinted tunnel and step over yet another dead bandit. Before long, cobwebs will cover all the walls and a [frostbite spider](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider") will attack, along with another Falmer. Proceed through the tunnels until you reach a lit [torch](/wiki/Skyrim:Torch "Skyrim:Torch") on the ground. As you approach the next chamber, a few Falmer guarding some imprisoned bandits will attack. In the panic, the bandits will escape from the pens, kill their captors, and then turn on you.

Proceed through the northern tunnel and follow it as it bends. You will arrive in a chamber filled with Dwemer architecture and machinery, now used for human sacrifices by the Falmer. You will face a [chaurus reaper](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus_Reaper "Skyrim:Chaurus Reaper") and two Falmer enemies. After the battle, examine the area for some minor treasure, then head to the sacrificial altar in the middle where you will find [Rahd](/wiki/Skyrim:Rahd "Skyrim:Rahd"), a dead [Breton](/wiki/Skyrim:Breton "Skyrim:Breton"), lying next to [The Longhammer](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Longhammer "Skyrim:The Longhammer"), one of the most powerful unique weapons in the game. Claim it and leave the same way you came.

As you travel back through Liar's Retreat, more frostbite spiders will spawn in the spider nest, so be wary. When you return to the tavern area just before the entrance, a group of [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") will enter from outside to be shocked at the grisly scene. The bandit chief will call out to the fallen Rahd with the words: *"Hey, Longhammer, set us up with a round of... what in Oblivion happened in here?"* When the bandits discover you, they will assume you were responsible for the massacre, and attack immediately. Finish up this final fight, and escape with your prize.

## Bugs

- There is an inaudible conversation between a Falmer, a male Orc and a female bandit. The conversation is scripted to start playing the moment you pass the natural small window between two caves, but all characters are too far from you for subtitles to appear, and will usually only be heard if you are very close to the window and have your volume turned up.

:   :   **Orc**: *"Take the money, just let us go..."*
    :   **Bandit**: *"Shut up or they'll kill us, you idiot! Once they're gone I'll pick the lock..."*
    :   **Bandit**: (moments later) *"Come on... there! I got it, let's go!"*

- The hammer may be found under the table and inaccessible, rather than on it.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.4, fixes this bug.
- The hammer may be clipping into the ground and hence invisible. Circling the table with the cursor on the ground next to it while watching for the sudden appearance of the Interact prompt may be the only way to find and loot it.

## Quest Stages

- All of the quest stages are empty: 0, 10, 20, 30, 31, 50, 80, 81, 100.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage dunLiarsRetreatQST stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest dunLiarsRetreatQST`.
